Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Ukugcwalisa ifom yesicelo kwi-online ukuze ubhalise akusoze kwenze ukuba uvumeleke nje ngokuzenzekelayo ukuba ufikelele kunxibelelwano lobuxhakaxhaka bomatshini obukuvumela ukuba wenze iinguqu kwinkcazelo yeshishini lakho. Ukuvunywa kobhaliso lwakho kuthabatha usuku okanye iintsuku ezimbini, kwaye ke uya kukwazi ukwenza iinguqu kuphela emva kokuba uvunyiwe.

Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Kungenjalo, hambisa incwadi yesibheno kwiBhunga kwisithuba seentsuku ezingama 30.
Incwadi kufuneka ikhatshwe yimali yentlawulo eqingqiweyo eyakuqulungqwa liBhunga.
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Kwisithuba seentsuku ezingama 60 ukusukela kumhla wokufunyanwa kwesibheno sakho, iBhunga liyakwenza isigqibo ngesibheno kwaye likunike izizathu zesigqibo salo.
Ukubangaba isibheno sibhekise ekwaleni kwekomiti ukuvuselela ubhaliso lomntu obhalisiweyo, ubhaliso lwakho alunakucinywa kude kugqitywe ngesibheno.
Entla
Iindleko
Kwiinkonzo zebhanki zobuxhakaxhaka bombane kunye needipozithi nqo: Nceda usebenzise oonobumba bokuqala bamagama akho kunye nefani yakho ukuze uchaze intlawulo yakho kwisitetimenti sethu sebhanki, uze uthumele ubungqina bentlawulo ngefeksi, buhambe kunye nephepha lokuqala lefom yakho yesicelo, kwinombolo ethi: 841 1057.

Ukuya kuhala okanye ukutyelela eMazantsi Afrika
Ishishini
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Ipemethe yeshishini yipemethe enikwa umntu welizwe langaphandle ojonge ukuseka okanye ukutyala imali kwishishini eMzantsi Afrika. Yenza isicelo kwindlu yozakuzo yaseMzantsi Afrika, kwiziko elimele uMzantsi Afrika okanye kwi-ofisi yezeKhaya ekufuphi kwindawo ozakuseka kuyo ishishini.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Kufuneka:
ubenemali eyikhetshi esisiseko sobuncinane obuyi R2,5 million okanye okungenani imali eyikhetshi eyi R2 million kunye negalelo lobutyebi onabo obuxabisa iR500 000. Le mali ichazwe ngasentla kufuneka ivele kwilizwe langaphandle kwaye kufuneka ifumaneke njengenxenye yexabiso lempahla elibhalwe kwiincwadi zeshishini 
isatifiketi esiphuma emapoliseni esiqinisekisa ubume obumsulwa, esivela kuwo onke amazwe oke wena nomlingane wakho nahlala kuwo ukusukela kwiminyaka yobudala eli 18 nezabo bonke abantwana abaxhomekeke kuwe abaneminyaka yobudala eli 18 okanye nangaphezulu abazakubanawe ngelilixa ukweli lizwe isatifiketi sokugonyelwa i-yellow fever ukubangaba uhamba okanye ujonge ukuhamba ukusuka okanye ukunqumla kummandla othandwa yi-yellow fever idipozithi yeenjongo zokubuyiselwa kwilizwe ovela kulo exabisa itikiti elinye lokuya nokubuya ngenqwelomoya kwilizwe ovela kulo okanye ohlala kulo isigxina: Loo dipozithi iyakubuyiswa emva kokumka kwakho umphelo okanye emva kokuba unikwe ipemethe. Idipozithi ingahlawulwa ngetshekhi eqinisekiswe yibhanki okanye ngekhadi lemboleko yekhredithi kwindawo eneziko elilungiselelwe loo ndlela yokuhlawula 
iingxelo zonyango neze-eksreyi zomenzi-sicelo ngamnye. Abantwana abaneminyaka yobudala engaphantsi kwe 12 kunye nabasetyhini abakhulelweyo, abayikufuneka ukuba babeneengxelo ze-eksreyi.

Ukumka eMzantsi Afrika
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Ipaspoti yomntwana yincwadi efunekayo ukuze umntwana ahambele kwelinye ilizwe. Ipaspoti yomntwana ikhutshelwa abantwana baseMzantsi Afrika abangaphantsi kweminyaka eli 16 ubudala. Iyasebenza kuwo wonke amazwe ahanjelwayo, ngaphandle kokuba kugunyaziswe ngolunye uhlobo. Isebenza iminyaka emi 5 ukusukela kumhla wokukhutshwa kwayo.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Hambisa isatifiketi sokuzalwa somntwana.
Khupha iifoto zomntwana ezimbini zepaspoti, zakutshanje.
Akunyatheliswa minwe.
Kufuneka imvume yabazali bobabini okanye abalondolozi phambi kokuba umntwana anikwe ipaspoti.
Khupha isatifiketi sokubhubha ukubangaba omnye wabazali akasekho.
Phantsi kweemeko ezithile (ukungabikho komzali) xa kungakwazeki ukuba loo mzali anike imvume kwifom yesicelo, makufunyanwe imvume ebhalwe encwadini kulo mzali ungekhoyo.
Kwiimeko apho umzali alayo ukunika imvume, inkundla ejongene nemibandela elolu hlobo, mayenze isigqibo ngalo mba. Ikopi yomyalelo obandakanyekayo wenkundla mayihanjiswe nale fom yesicelo sepaspoti.
Ukubangaba abazali baqhawule umtshato (badivosile), kufuneka imvume yabo bobabini abazali, ngaphandle kokuba umyalelo wenkundla uchaza ngenye indlela (oko kukuthi, ubulondolozi bomntu omnye bunikwe umzali omnye).

Ukuhlala ixeshana elifutshane
Isicelo sepemethe yokusebenza enqanaweni elwandle
Isicelo sepemethe yokusebenza enqanaweni (elwandle)
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Ipemethe yokusebenza enqanaweni inikwa umntu welizwe langaphandle ongomnye wabasebenzi basenqanaweni. Ipemethe yokusebenza enqanaweni ikhutshelwa ithuba elingagqithiyo kwiinyanga ezintathu ngexesha. Izicelo zingenziwa kwisango lokungena eMzantsi Afrika.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Veza incwadi yesicelo esuka kumnikazi wenqanawa, kwaye ibandakanye isibhengezo sesithembiso sokuthabatha uxanduva lokuhambisana kwaloo mntu noMthetho wokuNgena eLizweni (Immigration Act, 2002).
Hambisa ubungqina bokubanako ngokwaneleyo komnikazi wenqanawa ngokuphathelelene nemali yokujongana neemfuno zemihla ngemihla kunye neendleko zonyango.
Hlawula idipozithi ukubangaba oko kubonwe kuyimfuneko liSebe lezeKhaya, ukuze uqinisekise ukuhambisana neemeko nemiqathango yepemethe yokusebenza enqanaweni. Loo dipozithi iyakubuyiselwa kuwe emva kokuba umke umphelo okanye emva kokuba unikwe ipemethe. Intlawulo yedipozithi ingenziwa ngetshekhi eqinisekiswe yibhanki okanye ngekhadi lemboleko yekhredithi kwindawo eneziko elilungiselelwe loo ndlela yokuhlawula.
Hambisa ubungqina bentlawulo ebingekakhutshwa yayo nayiphina intlawuliso yesohlwayo (ifayini) esiwiselwe isithuthi.

Ingqesho
Isicelo sepemethe yokusebenza yenani eliqingqiweyo ngokubanzi
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Ipemethe yokusebenza yenani eliqingqiweyo ngokubanzi inikwa umntu welizwe langaphandle ukubangaba loo mntu uwela phantsi kwecandelo ekugqitywe ngalo liSebe lezeKhaya qho ngonyaka, ngesaziso kwiGazethi kaRhulumente, emva kokubonisana noMphathiswa wezoRhwebo naMashishini kunye noMphathiswa weZabasebenzi. Inani leepemethe zelo candela akufanelanga lidlule inani eliqingqiweyo eliqulungqwe sisaziso.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
veza incwadi ebonisa ukuba uqeshiwe
Hambisa isiqinisekiso esenziwe ngumgcini nomlondolozi wee-akhawunti zemali olilungu lequmrhu labagcini nabahloli bee-akhawunti zemali, esichaza oku kulandelayo:
o ukuba awuyikuqeshwa phantsi kweemeko nemiqathango engaphantsi kwaleyo inikwa abemi okanye abahlali o inkcazelo ngezinto oyakuzenza kumsebenzi wakho o ukuba lo msebenzi uwela phantsi kwecandelo elifanelekileyo eliqulungqwe nguMphathiswa o ukuba sikho esi sithuba kwaye siyakugcwaliswa nguwe o ukuba unazo iikhwalifikheyshini ezisemthethweni eziyimfuneko ukuze wenze imisebenzi efuneka kwinkcazelo yezinto ozakuzenza kulo msebenzi.
Hambisa isibhengezo sokuzinikela komqashi ekubeni ahlawule imali yoqeqesho eziipesenti ezimbini. (Qaphela: Ubungqina bentlawulo kufuneka buthunyelwe kwisithuba seentsuku ezintathu kufunyenwe ipemethe).
Veza ubungqina bobhaliso kwiqumrhu lobuchule boqeqesho okanye kwibhodi yobuchule boqeqesho, ukubangaba oko kuyabandakanyeka.

Entla

Ukutshata
Isicelo sesatifiketi somtshato (umtshato wentlalo yabemi)
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Isatifiketi somtshato sibubungqina bokuba utshatile. Umtshato kufuneka uqhutywe kukho aba bantu batshatayo, amangqina amabini aphethe iincwadi zawo zezazisi kunye negosa lokutshatisa.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Aba bantu babini batshatayo, amangqina amabini kunye negosa lokutshatisa kufuneka basayine iNcwadi yokuBhalisa uMtshato kwangoko emva kokuba umtshato ugunyazisiwe.
Ungenza isicelo sokuvunywa kwiNkundla ePhakamileyo kummandla ohlala kuwo ukubangaba abazali bakho kunye noMkomishinari bayala okanye uMkomishinari uyala ukuvuma umtshato.
Abantu ababhujelweyo abafuna ukuphinda batshate kufuneka baveze isatifiketi sokubhubha somlingane ongasekhoyo. Mabathi thaca i-affidavit ukubangaba asifumaneki isatifiketi sokubhubha. I-affidavit kufuneka ingqine igama lomlingane obhubhileyo kunye nomhla wokubhubha.
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Isatifiketi somtshato esifinyeziweyo: Sikhutshwa kwangoko.
Isatifiketi esingafinyezwanga: Izicelo zingathabatha iiveki ezi 6 ukuya kwezisi 8.
Entla
Iindleko
Isatifiketi somtshato esifinyeziweyo: R11
Isatifiketi somtshato esingafinyezwanga: R53

Inkcazelo
inikwa abemi baseMzantsi Afrika abaneminyaka yobudala eli 16 okanye nangaphezulu sebenziseka kuhambo oluya kuwo onke amazwe, ngaphandle kokuba inomfakelo ogunyazisa ngenye indlela isebenziseka iminyaka eli 10 ukusukela kumhla wokukhutshwa kwayo.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Phatha kuwe incwadi yakho yesazisi okanye isatifiketi sokuzalwa xa usenza isicelo.
Nyathelisa iminwe (iifingaprinti) ukuze ifakwe kuvimba woBhaliso lweNani neeNkcukacha zaBantu.
Hambisa iifoto ezimbini ezilingana kwipaspoti.

Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Ipemethe yokufumana unyango inikwa umntu welizwe langaphandle oneenjongo zokufumana unyango eMzantsi Afrika. Loo pemethe yonyango ihlala isebenziseka iinyanga eziphelela kwisithandathu ngexesha. Yenza isicelo sepemethe yotshintshiselwano kwindlu yozakuzo yaseMzantsi Afrika okanye kwiziko elimele uMzantsi Afrika elikufuphi kuwe.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Hambisa ipaspoti yakho ekufuneka ibe iyasebenziseka iintsuku ezingekho ngaphantsi kwama 30 emva kokuphelelwa kotyelelo olucetywayo.
Hambisa ubungqina bokubanako ngokwemali ukuze umelane nezidingo zemihla ngemihla zabo bonke abantu abakhapha umntu onepemethe yonyango (ukuba bakhona), ngokwezitetimenti, iimpepha ezibonisa umvuzo, ukuba zikhona, okanye iitshekhi zabahambi.
Hambisa incwadi evela kwingcaphephe yezonyango okanye kwiziko lezonyango, ebonisa izizathu okanye imfuneko yonyango, ixesha ekulindeleke ukuba lithatyathwe lunyango kunye neenkcukacha zezicwangciso zokunyangwa eMzantsi Afrika.
Khupha omnye okanye nangaphezulu koko, kule miqulu ilandelayo, ikhaphe isicelo sakho sepemethe:
o isatifiketi sonyango esipheleleyo o isatifiketi sokuzalwa esipheleleyo o isatifiketi somtshato esipheleleyo (ukuba siyabandakanyeka)
o incwadi ebhaliweyo nefungelweyo ekuthiwa yi-affidavit BI-1712A ukubangaba kubandakanyeka ubudlelwane bobulingane obungengomtshato, ihambe nobungqina bokuhlalisana o isivumelwano esizotywe ngumntu oqeqeshelwe ukwenza njalo ngokomthetho, kwiimeko zokuhlalisana o ubungqina bomtshato wesintu, ukubangaba oko kuyabandakanyeka o umyalelo woqhawulo-mtshato, ukubangaba oko kuyabandakanyeka o ubungqina bomyalelo wenkundla onika ilungelo lokugcina abantwana, ukubangaba oko kuyabandakanyeka o isatifiketi sokubhubha, ngokuphathelelene nomlingane ongasekhoyo, ukubangaba oko kuyabandakanyeka o imvume ebhaliweyo esuka kubo bobabini abazali, okanye kumzali omnye onguye yedwa ogcina abantwana, ukuba oko kuyabandakanyeka, ihambe nobungqina bokubanguye yedwa ogcina abantwana o ubungqina bokwamkelwa komntwana ngumntu ongamzelanga ibengowakhe (adoption) ngokwasemthethweni, ukuba oko kuyabandakanyeka o umyalelo wokwahlukana ngokwasemthethweni, ukuba oko kuyabandakanyeka o isatifiketi esiphuma emapoliseni esiqinisekisa ubume obumsulwa, ukubangaba wena, menzi-sicelo, uneminyaka yobudala engama 21 nangaphezulu, ngokuphathelelene nawo onke amazwe ohleli kuwo unyaka okanye ngaphezulu konyaka o isatifiketi sokugonywa, ukuba oko kuyabandakanyeka.

Ukumka eMzantsi Afrika
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Ipaspoti yongxamiseko yincwadi efuneka ngokukhawuleza xa ujonge ukuhambela kumazwe angabamelwane angafuni ii-visa zokungena. Ipaspoti yongxamiseko ingasetyenziselwa kwanokubuyela eMzantsi Afrika ngokungxamisekileyo. Isebenziseka iinyanga ezilithoba ukusukela kumhla wokukhutshwa kwayo, kodwa isetyenziswa kuhambo olunye kuphela, ukuya kwilizwe elibandakanyekayo nokubuyela eMzantsi Afrika.

Ukuya kuhala okanye ukutyelela eMazantsi Afrika
Ingqesho
Ipemethe yokusebenza yezakhono ezikhetheke zodwa
Isicelo sepemethe yokusebenza yezakhono ezikhetheke zodwa
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Ipemethe yokusebenza yezakhono ezikhetheke zodwa inikwa umntu welizwe langaphandle onezakhono okanye iikhwalifikheyshini ezikhetheke zodwa. Inganikwa namalungu efemeli esondele nqo kuloo mntu. Izicelo zingenziwa kwindlu yozakuzo yaseMzantsi Afrika okanye kwiziko elimele uMzantsi Afrika.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ubungqina bokubanako ngokwemali, ngohlobo lwezitetimenti zebhanki, iincwadi ezibonisa umvuzo, isibhengezo sesithembiso esenziwe liziko oza kulo okanye izibhengezo zezithembiso ezenziwe ngamaziko oza kuwo, eMzantsi Afrika, iibhasari, izicwangciso zonyango, okanye imali ekhoyo, kubandakanywa amakhadi emboleko yekhredithi okanye iitshekhi zomhambi, eyakujongana neendleko ezicingelwayo zentlalo nokuphila ngexesha lokuhlala eMzantsi Afrika.
Veza incwadi ephuma kwiziko lombuso welizwe langaphandle okanye waseMzantsi Afrika okanye ephuma kwiqumrhu elimiyo laseMzantsi Afrika lezemfundo, lenkcubeko okanye lezoshishino, engqina izakhono okanye iikhwalifikheyshini zakho ezikhetheke zodwa.

Ingqesho
Isicelo sepemethe yokusebenza yokutshintshelwa kwinkampani enxulumeneyo
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Ipemethe yokutshintshelwa kwinkampani enxulumeneyo ikhutshelwa umntu welizwe langaphandle otshintshelwa yinkampani yakhe ukuze ayokusebenza kwinkampani enxulumene naleyo eMzantsi Afrika. Ixesha elithatyathwa yile pemethe yokusebenza yokutshintshelwa kwinkampani enxulumeneyo aligqithi kwiminyaka emibini. Izicelo zingenziwa kwindlu yozakuzo yaseMzantsi Afrika okanye kwiziko elimele uMzantsi Afrika.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Hambisa isiqinisekiso esenziwe ngumgcini nomhloli wee-akhawunti zemali olilungu lequmrhu labagcini nabahloli bee-akhawunti zemali, omele indawo yomqashi, esichaza imfuneko yokukuqasha kwaye esibonisa inkcazelo yezinto ozakuzenza kumsebenzi wakho.
Hambisa isiqinisekiso esenziwe ngumgcini nomhloli wee-akhawunti zemali olilungu lequmrhu labagcini nabahloli bee-akhawunti zemali, esichaza ukuba awuyikuqashwa phantsi kweemeko nemiqathango engaphantsi kwaleyo ibandakanyeka kubemi nabahlali, futhi sichaze ukuba unazo iikhwalifikheyshini ezisemthethweni ezifuneka kulo msebenzi.
Veza ubungqina bobhaliso kwiqumrhu lobuchule boqeqesho okanye kwibhodi yobuchule boqeqesho, ukubangaba oko kuyabandakanyeka.

Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Qinisekisa ukuba uyiphethe incwadi yakho yesazisi okanye isatifiketi sokuzalwa ukuze wenze isicelo.
Nyathelisa iminwe (iifingaprinti) ukuze ifakwe kuvimba woBhaliso lweNani neeNkcukacha zaBantu.
Hambisa iifoto ezimbini ezilingana kwipaspoti.
Yenza isicelo sepaspoti egunyazisiweyo kunye nencwadi yesazisi ngexesha elinye ukubangaba awunako ukulinda.
Hambisa incwadi ephuma kumqashi echaza izizathu zokuba kutheni udinga ipaspoti egunyazisiweyo.

Ukuya kuhala okanye ukutyelela eMazantsi Afrika
Ukuhla isigxina
Iipemethe yokuhlala isigxina abalingane bomtshato
Isicelo sepemethe yokuhlala isigxina - abalingane bomtshato
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Le nkonzo isebenziseka kumntu welizwe langaphandle onobudlelwane bobulingane obusisigxina nommi okanye umhlali osisigxina waseMzantsi Afrika.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Nabo ubudlelwane bobomi besigxina obuphakathi koogxa besini esinye nabezini ezahlukeneyo, bukwavumeleka, kodwa, endaweni yesatifiketi somtshato, abo gxa kufuneka ukuba bavokothekise ubizo lwabo lokuhlalisana kunye nokuxhasana kwabo ubuqu nangokwemali, ngokuthumela incwadi ebhaliweyo nefungelweyo (i-affidavit).
Ukuze iSebe lezeKhaya linike ipemethe yokuhlala isigxina kumlingane welizwe langaphandle wommi okanye womhlali osisigxina waseMzantsi Afrika, eli Sebe kufuneka laneliseke ukuba bukho ubudlelwane bobulingane obusekwe ngentembeko nangenene.
Ngugxa womtshato welizwe langaphandle, omnye kuphela ongenza isicelo sobume ngenxa yokuba etshate ummi okanye umhlali osisigxina waseMzantsi Afrika.
Kufuneka ube utshate nommi okanye umhlali osisigxina waseMzantsi Afrika ngokomthetho wentlalo yabemi okanye ngokomthetho wesiko lesiqhelo isithuba seminyaka emihlanu.
Izicelo zingenziwa kuyo nayiphina i-ofisi yezeKhaya okanye kwindlu yozakuzo yaseMzantsi Afrika okanye kwiziko elimele uMzantsi Afrika ukubangaba wenza isicelo ukwilizwe langaphandle.

Ukuhla isigxina
Isicelo sepemethe yokuhlala isigxina yabenzi-zicelo abangaphezulu kwama 21 eminyaka yobudala kwaye abangabantwana babemi baseMzantsi Afrika
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Umntu welizwe langaphandle ongumntwana wabemi baseMzantsi Afrika kwaye ongaphezulu kwama 21 eminyaka yobudala, angenza isicelo sepemethe yokuhlala isigxina.
Le nkonzo ikakhulu ilungiselelwe abantwana babazali abafumana ubumi ngokwamkelwa njengabemi emva kokuhlala ixesha elithile. Abantwana babemi baseMzantsi Afrika abangabemi ngokuzalwa nangokomnombo bayavumeleka kubumi baseMzantsi Afrika, kwaye akukho mfuneko yokuba benze izicelo zobume bokuhlala isigxina.
Izicelo zingenziwa kuyo nayiphina i-ofisi yezeKhaya okanye kwindlu yozakuzo yaseMzantsi Afrika okanye kwiziko elimele uMzantsi Afrika ukubangaba wenza isicelo ukwilizwe langaphandle.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Hambisa isatifiketi sokuzalwa.
Abazali bakho bangafuneka ukuba bathi thaca isibhengezo sesithembiso sokuncedisa ngemali, kuyaxhomekeka kubume bakho bokubanako ngokwemali.

Ukuya kuhala okanye ukutyelela eMazantsi Afrika
Ukuhla isigxina
Isicelo sepemethe yokuhlala isigxina yabenzi-zicelo abangaphantsi kwama 21 eminyaka yobudala kwaye abangabantwana babemi baseMzantsi Afrika
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Eli candela lisebenziseka kumntu welizwe langaphandle ongaphantsi kwama 21 eminyaka yobudala kwaye ongumntwana wommi okanye womhlali osisigxina waseMzantsi Afrika. Ipemethe yokuhlala isigxina ikhutshwa phantsi komqathango wokuba iyakuphelelwa kukusebenza emva kweminyaka emibini ukusukela kumhla wemini yosuku lwakho lokuzalwa leminyaka yobudala engama 21 (21st birthday), ngaphandle kokuba kwenziwe isicelo sokungqina ubume bakho bokuhlala.
Izicelo zingenziwa kuyo nayiphina i-ofisi yezeKhaya okanye kwindlu yozakuzo yaseMzantsi Afrika okanye kwiziko elimele uMzantsi Afrika ukubangaba wenza isicelo ukwilizwe langaphandle.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Abazali bafuneka ukuba bahambise ubungqina bobumi babo okanye bobume bokuhlala isigxina eMzantsi Afrika, ngokukhupha iincwadi zezazisi okanye iipemethe zokuhlala isigxina.
Ukuze ungqine ubuzali, hambisa isatifiketi sokuzalwa somntwana.
Abazali kufuneka bathi thaca isibhengezo sesithembiso senkxaso yemali.

Entla

Ukuhla isigxina
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Le nkonzo isebenziseka kumntu ozakubangumhlali wesigxina onqwenela ukwenza isicelo sokuhlala isigxina ngenxa yokuba eyifemeli yommi okanye yomhlali osisigxina waseMzantsi Afrika kwinqanaba lokuqala lokuzalana. Ngeenjongo zokuhlala isigxina, amalungu efemeli akwinqanaba lokuqala lokuzalana amiselwa njengamalungu enzalelwane kunye nabantwana abamkelwe ngabantu abangabazelanga njengababo ngokwasemthethweni okanye abazali abamkele abantwana abangabazelanga njengababo ngokwasemthethweni kunye nabazali bomnye umtshato .
Izicelo zingenziwa kuyo nayiphina i-ofisi yezeKhaya okanye kwindlu yozakuzo yaseMzantsi Afrika okanye kwiziko elimele uMzantsi Afrika ukubangaba wenza isicelo ukwilizwe langaphandle.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ummi okanye umhlali osisigxina waseMzantsi Afrika makahambise isibhengezo sesithembiso malunga noxanduva lwezemali, unyango kunye nesiqu somenzi-sicelo. Kodwa ke, xa isihlobo ingumzali womntwana ongekabinalungelo lokuzithabathela izigqibo ngokwasemthethweni, akukho mfuneko yesibhengezo sesithembiso.

Ukuya kuhala okanye ukutyelela eMazantsi Afrika
Ukuhla isigxina
Isicelo sepemethe yokuhlala isigxina - umntu oneshishini lakhe
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
DeLe nkonzo isebenziseka kumntu welizwe langaphandle ojonge ukuseka ishishini eMzantsi Afrika; okanye osele enepemethe yeshishini ukuze aqhube ishishini kweli lizwe; okanye ojonge ukutyala imali kwishishini esele likhona kweli lizwe. 
Izicelo zingathunyelwa kuyo nayiphina i-ofisi yezeKhaya kwiphondo ojonge ukuqhubela kulo ishishini. Yenza isicelo kwindlu yozakuzo yaseMzantsi Afrika okanye kwiziko elimele uMzantsi Afrika ukubangaba ukwilizwe langaphandle. 
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Umgcini nomhloli wee-akhawunti zemali olilungu lequmrhu labagcini nabahloli bee-akhawunti zemali (chartered accountant), omele indawo yakho, kufuneka ahambise uqinisekiso lokuba igalelo lemali emiselweyo kwixabiso lempahla nezinto (ekujongwe kulo) elikwiincwadi zeshishini, lityaliwe. Igalelo lemali emiselweyo liyi R2,5 million kwaye lingabekelwa bucala okanye lincitshiswe kuphela xangaba oko kuthathwa ngokuba kungumnqweno welizwe okanye xangaba oko kucelwe liSebe lezoRhwebo naMashishini.
Bakube ubume bokuhlala isigxina bufunyenwe, kuyakufuneka ukuba uvuselele uqinisekiso olwenziwe ngumgcini nomhloli wee-akhawunti zemali olilungu labagcini nabahloli bee-akhawunti zemali, kwiminyaka emibini emva komhla wokukhutshwa kwepemethe yokuhlala isigxina, uphinde kwakhona kwiminyaka emithathu emva koko. Ukungaphumeleli ukuhambisana nalo mqathango kungakhokelela ekubeni ipemethe yokuhlala isigxina iphelelwe kukusebenza.

Ukuhla isigxina
Isicelo sabantu abadla umhlalaphantsi
Isicelo sepemethe yokuhlala isigxina - abantu abadla umhlalaphantsi

Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Le nkonzo ilungiselelwe umntu welizwe langaphandle onqwenela ukudlela umhlalaphantsi eMzantsi Afrika. Akukho siqingqo esingqalileyo seminyaka yobudala. Izicelo zingenziwa kuyo nayiphina i-ofisi yezeKhaya okanye kwindlu yozakuzo yaseMzantsi Afrika okanye kwiziko elimele uMzantsi Afrika ukuba wenza isicelo ukwilizwe langaphandle.
Entla
Kungenjalo, kufuneka unike ubungqina kwiSebe lezeKhaya bokuba unomdibaniso weempahla nezinto ezinexabiso elifikelela kwingeniso-mali eyi R20 000.

Ukuya kuhala okanye ukutyelela eMazantsi Afrika
Ukuhla isigxina
Isicelo sepemethe yokuhlala isigxina - umsebenzi
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Le nkonzo ilungiselelwe umntu welizwe langaphandle onqwenela ukwenza isicelo sobume bokuhlala isigxina ngenxa yokuba enikwe ingqesho esisigxina eMzantsi Afrika. Esi sicelo kufuneka sibe ngaphakathi kweziqingqo zangonyaka ezibekwa kumaxesha ngamaxesha.
Izicelo zingenziwa kuyo nayiphina i-ofisi yezeKhaya kwiphondo ojonge ukusebenza kulo okanye kwindlu yozakuzo yaseMzantsi Afrika okanye kwiziko elimele uMzantsi Afrika ukubangaba wenza isicelo ukwilizwe langaphandle.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Umntu ozakubangumqashi wakho kufuneka athi thaca ubungqina bezi zinto zilandelayo kwiSebe lezeKhaya:
o bokuba isikhundla osinikwayo sikho o bokuba isikhundla kunye nenkcazelo yomsebenzi ozakuwenza sasikhutshiwe kwisibhengezo sokwazisa (advertised) ngendlela ebekiweyo o bokuba zange kubekho bemi baseMzantsi Afrika okanye abahlali abasisigxina abaneekhwalifikheyshini ezifanelekileyo ukuze bangene kweso sikhundla.
Department of Labour (ISebe leZabasebenzi), kufuneka liqinisekise ukuba iimeko nemiqathango yokunikwa le ngqesho ayikho ngaphantsi kwaleyo ikhoyo kwicandelo lemarike engqameneyo yabemi nabahlali. Ngokwenza njalo, iSebe leZabasebenzi lifuneka ukuba lithathele ingqalelo izivumelwano zeengxoxo ezihlanganelweyo kunye neminye imigangatho ebandakanyekayo.

Ukuya kuhala okanye ukutyelela eMazantsi Afrika
Iintsapho kunye nabantu abadla umhlalaphantsi
Isicelo sepemethe yomntu omdala umhlalaphantsi
Isicelo sepemethe yomntu odla umhlalaphantsi
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Ipemethe yomntu odla umhlalaphantsi inikwa umntu welizwe langaphandle ojonge ukudlela umhlalaphantsi eMzantsi Afrika.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Xa unqwenela ukusebenza, hambisa inkcazelo yokuba akukho mmi okanye mhlali waseMzantsi Afrika ofumanekayo ukuze athabathe loo msebenzi wenza isicelo sawo.
Hlawula idipozithi. Loo dipozithi ayiyikubuyiselwa kumntu oyifakileyo emva kokumka kwakho umphelo okanye emva kokuba unikwe ipemethe. Intlawulo yedipozithi ingenziwa ngetshekhi eqinisekiswe yibhanki okanye ngekhadi lemboleko yekhredithi kwindawo eneziko elilungiselelwe loo ndlela yokuhlawula.
Veza isatifiketi esiphuma emapoliseni esiqinisekisa ubume obumsulwa, ndawonye nengxelo yonyango neye-eksreyi. Akuyomfuneko ukuba abantwana abangaphantsi kweminyaka eli 12 yobudala kunye nabasetyhini abakhulelweyo ukuba bakhuphe ingxelo ye-eksreyi.
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Le nkonzo ithabatha ixesha elingagqithiyo kwiintsuku ezingama 30.

Ukuya kuhala okanye ukutyelela eMazantsi Afrika
Ukufunda
Isicelo sepemethe yenkqubo yokutshintshiselana ngabafundi
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Ipemethe yenkqubo yokutshintshiselana ngabafundi yipemethe enikwa umfundi welizwe langaphandle ekufanele athabathe inxaxheba kwiprojekthi okanye kwinkqubo ethile kwiziko lemfundo laseMzantsi Afrika elikwinqanaba lesithathu (imfundo ephakamileyo, umzekelo, iyunivesiti okanye iyunivesiti yobuchwepheshe.)
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Yenza isicelo kwindlu yozakuzo yaseMzantsi Afrika okanye kwiziko elimele uMzantsi Afrika.
Hambisa incwadi esuka kwiSebe leMfundo okanye kwiziko loluntu lemfundo ephakamileyo eMzantsi Afrika:
o engqina ukuba eli ziko lilo eliququzelela okanye eliphethe le nkqubo o echaza imisebenzi yale nkqubo kunye nexesha eliyakuthatyathwa yile nkqubo o engqina ukuba eli ziko liyakuthabatha uxanduva olupheleleyo malunga nalo mfundi ngelixa ekwiRiphabhlikhi kwaye umfundi wamkelelwe ukuba abhaliswe.
Hambisa incwadi esuka kwiziko elithile lelizwe langaphandle:
o engqina iinkcukacha zomfundi, kubandakanywa ubhaliso lomfundi kwiziko lemfundo ekwinqanaba lesithathu kwilizwe langaphandle o engqina umhla eyakuqala ngawo le nkqubo eMzantsi Afrika.

Isicelo semali yoncediso kwikhaya labantwana
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Ikhaya labantwana yindawo ebhalisiweyo yokunakekela abantwana. Amakhaya wabantwana angabanga imali yoncediso oluyisabhsidi yenyanga kurhulumente ukuze afezekise iindleko zawo eziqhubekayo. Imali yesabhsidi ekhutshwayo ayifani kwaye isekelwe kwiindleko eziqhubekayo zeli khaya kunye nenani labantwana abahlala kulo.
Ngamakhaya wabantwana abhalisiweyo.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Inkqubo yesicelo iyakuthabatha ngaphezulu kweenyanga ezintathu ukuze isicelo siqhubekiswe.
Esi sigqibo sisekelwe ekufumanekeni kwezinto eziyimfuneko kunye nemfuneko yale nkonzo.
Isebe likhupha ezi mali zoncediso oluyisabhsidi qho ngeenyanga ezintathu, kuxhomekeke kuqwalaselo ngokutsha lwemisebenzi yeli khaya labantwana.

Ukuya kuhala okanye ukutyelela eMazantsi Afrika
Ukuhlala ixeshana elifutshane
Ipemethe yomntu ocela ukukhuselwa ngumbuso
Isicelo sepemethe yomntu ocela ukukhuselwa ngumbuso
Inkcazelo
Isicelo sokukhuselwa ngumbuso (asylum) sisicelo somenzi-sicelo sokuba avunywe njengembacu.
Umntu ocela ukukhuselwa ngumbuso ngumntu obaleke elizweni lakhe lemvelaphi ngenxa yokoyika ukungcungcuthekiswa (ngokwentlalo, ngokwenkcubeko, ngokwezopolitiko, ngokwenkolo yobutyalike, nankqu ngokwezoqoqosho), kwaye ocela ukuvunywa njengembacu - kule meko ke eMzantsi Afrika. Umenzi-sicelo uhlala engumntu ocela ukuvunywa njengembacu ngelilixa isicelo sakhe sisaqwalaselwayo.
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Umntu ocela ukukhuselwa ngumbuso ufaka isicelo ngokwakhe kwindawo echongiweyo yoKwamkela iiMbacu, apho kwenziwa ezi zinto zilandelayo:
Umenzi-sicelo uqale aphononongwe imeko yakhe
Umenzi-sicelo unyatheliswa iminwe (iifingaprinti)
Kuziswa itoliki (ukuba oko kuyimfuneko)
IGosa lokuQulungqa uBume beeMbacu liyaqhubeka ngokulamla kule nyewe yesicelo kwaye lithabatha isigqibo malunga nesicelo sokukhuselwa ngumbuso.
Ubume bobumbacu buhlala iminyaka emibini, kodwa imbacu kufuneka ibhale incwadi icele ukuqwalaselwa ngokutsha kobume bobumbacu okanye ukongezelelwa kwexesha lokusebenziseka kobume bobumbacu, kwiinyanga ezintathu phambi kokuba obo bume bobumbacu buphelelwe.
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Izicelo zingathabatha ixesha elifikelela kwiinyanga ezintandathu.
Iindleko
Le nkonzo ayihlawulelwa.

Ukunikwa enye ipaspoti xa ilahlekile ibiwe

Ukumka eMzantsi Afrika
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Ipaspoti yokukhenketha yincwadi efunekayo xa undwendwela kwelinye ilizwe okanye xa uphinda ungena eMzantsi Afrika. Ipaspoti yokukhenketha ikhutshelwa abemi baseMzantsi Afrika abaneminyaka yobudala eli 16 okanye nangaphezulu. Iyasebenza kundwendwelo lwawo wonke amazwe ngaphandle kokuba kugunyaziswe ngolunye uhlobo. Isebenza iminyaka eli 10 ukusukela ngomhla ekhutshwe ngawo.
Kufuneka ubenencwadi yesazisi (ID) okanye isatifiketi sokuzalwa ukuze wenze isicelo. Isicelo sepaspoti kunye nesencwadi yesazisi ungazenza ngexesha elinye ukubangaba awunako ukulinda.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Uyakunyatheliswa iminwe (fingerprints) ukuze ishicilelwe kwiNcwadi eBhale iNani neeNkcukacha zaBantu belizwe.
Hambisa iifoto ezimbini ezilingana kwipaspoti.
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Ipaspoti ingakhutshwa kwisithuba seeveki ezi 6.

Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
I-visa luphawu olugunyazisiweyo olubekwa kwipaspoti esebenzisekayo yomntu welizwe langaphandle, olunika loo mntu welizwe langaphandle igunya lokungena eMzantsi Afrika.
ifunyanwe phambi kokuba umenzi-sicelo alishiye ilizwe lakhe endulukela eMzantsi Afrika ifunyanwe kwilizwe langaphandle, kwaye akunakwenziwa isicelo sayo kumasango okungena aseMzantsi Afrika kwenziwe isicelo sayo kwelo lizwe, kwindlu yozakuzo yaseMzantsi Afrika okanye kwiziko elimele uMzantsi Afrika, kumazwe apho uMzantsi Afrika umelweyo kuwo kwenziwe isicelo sayo kwindlu yozakuzo yaseMzantsi Afrika ekufuphi okanye kwiziko elimele uMzantsi Afrika elikufuphi, ukubangaba uMzantsi Afrika awumelwanga elizweni lakho. Oku kuyabandakanyeka nakubantu abaneepaspoti zozakuzelwano lwamazwe nezigunyazisiweyo abafuna iipemethe zozakuzelwano phakathi kwamazwe.
Entla
Entla
Entla

Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo

Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Kwimeko yomntu oguqulelwe amalungu esini ngoqhaqho okanye ngonyango, hambisa iingxelo ezichaza uhlobo kunye neziphumo zayo nayiphina inkqubo eyenziweyo kunye naluphina unyango olwenziwe okanye olulungiswe ziingcaphephe zonyango eziqhube lo msebenzi okanye ezifake unyango.
Kuzo zonke iimeko, nika ingxelo ekhapha isicelo, echaza imbonakalo yesini somenzi-sicelo xakungoku. Le ngxelo kufuneka iqulungqwe yingcaphephe yezonyango exilonge umenzi-sicelo ukuze kuqondwe imbonakalo yakhe ngokwesini.
Khupha ingxelo esuka kugqirha wezifo zengqondo odlene iindlebe zokucebisa umenzi-sicelo, enika iinkcukacha ezipheleleyo zale meko, ngakumbi imbali yayo kunye nobume bengqondo balo mntu ngokuphathelelene nolu guqulo lwesini.
Ukubangaba umenzi-sicelo uneminyaka yobudala eli 16 okanye nangaphezulu, kufuneka kwenziwe isicelo sencwadi yesazisi entsha.

Entla

Inkcazelo
Umntu ongummi waseMzantsi Afrika ngokomnombo nguye nabanina ozalelwe ngaphandle koMzantsi Afrika ngabazali apho okungenani omnye wabazali engummi waseMzantsi Afrika. Ukuzalwa komntwana kufuneka kubhaliswe ngokuhambisana noMthetho wokuBhaliswa kokuZalwa nokuBhubha (Births and Deaths Registration Act, 1992).
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Thumela ikopi yesi satifiketi sokuzalwa selizwe langaphandle.
Thumela ubungqina ukubangaba umzali waseMzantsi Afrika ufumene ubumi belizwe langaphandle.
Thumela ubungqina bokuzalwa kwalo mzali waseMzantsi Afrika.

Ukuhla isigxina
Isicelo sokwamkelwa njengommi
Isicelo sokwamkelwa njengommi emva kokuhlala ixesha elithile
Inkcazelo
Nawuphina umntu onepemethe yokuhlala isigxina eMzantsi Afrika uyavumeleka enze isicelo sobumi baseMzantsi Afrika ngokwenkqubo yokwamkelwa njengommi emva kweminyaka emihlanu engumhlali osisigxina.
Nawuphina umntu otshate ummi waseMzantsi Afrika uyavumeleka amkelwe njengommi kwiminyaka emibini emva kokuba efumene ipemethe yokuhlala isigxina ekhutshwe ngexesha lomtshato.
Umntwana oneminyaka yobudala engaphantsi kwama 21, onepemethe yokuhlala isigxina, uyavumeleka amkelwe njengommi kwamsinyane nje emva kokuba ikhutshiwe ipemethe.
Ukuze ufumane inkcazelo ebanzi, yiya kwiSebe lezaseKhaya
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Umzali onoxanduva angenza isicelo egameni lomntwana ongekabinalungelo lokuzenzela izigqibo ngokusemthethweni, ukubangaba phofu lo mntwana uhlala isigxina nangokusemthethweni eMzantsi Afrika.
Kuyakukhutshwa incwadi yesazisi kwaye ithunyelwe kumenzi-sicelo.
Abenzi-zicelo abalelwe izicelo bayakuxelelwa ngokunjalo.
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Izicelo zingathabatha iinyanga ezi 2 ukuya kwezi 4.

Isebenza kubantu ababengabemi baseMzantsi Afrika phambi kokuba balifulathele eli lizwe kwaye abajonge ukubuyela kubumi baseMzantsi Afrika. Inkcazelo
Ummi waseMzantsi Afrika ofuna ukubangummi welinye ilizwe kufanele enze isicelo kwiSebe lezeKhaya ukuze agcine ubumi bakhe baseMzantsi Afrika phambi kokuba afumane ubumi belinye ilizwe. Ubuzwe okanye ubumi bamazwe amabini buthetha ukuba lo mntu uthathwa ngokuba ungummi wawo omabini la mazwe.
Ubumi bamazwe amabini bunikwa abantu abaneminyaka yobudala engaphezulu kwama 21.
Yenza isicelo kwindlu yozakuzo yaseMzantsi Afrika okanye kwiziko elimele uMzantsi Afrika ukuba wenza isicelo ukwilizwe langaphandle.

Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Lo mnyenyevu wenza ukuba abemi baseMzantsi Afrika babengabemi belinye ilizwe ngaphandle kokuphulukana nobumi babo baseMzantsi Afrika. Izicelo zingenziwa kuyo nayiphina i-ofisi yezeKhaya. Yenza isicelo kwindlu yozakuzo yaseMzantsi Afrika okanye kwiziko elimele uMzantsi Afrika ukubangaba ukwilizwe langaphandle.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Abenzi-zicelo abajonge ukufumana ubumi belinye ilizwe ngaphandle kokuphulukana nobumi babo baseMzantsi Afrika kufuneka balandele le nkqubo:
Veza ikopi eqinisekisiweyo yesatifiketi sokuzalwa saseMzantsi Afrika kunye nencwadi ebhaliweyo nefungelweyo echaza ukuba akukho bumi bungobunye obufunyenweyo. Zonke iikopi zemiqulu kunye nencwadi ebhaliweyo nefungelweyo kufuneka ziqinisekiswe kuphela ngumntu oneGunya lokuQinisekisa iMiqulu okanye nguMkomishinari weZifungo.
Abenzi-zicelo kufuneka balandele le nkqubo:
Hambisa ikopi eqinisekisiweyo yesatifiketi sobumi belizwe langaphandle.
Zonke iikopi zemiqulu kufuneka ziqinisekiswe kuphela ngumntu oneGunya lokuQinisekisa iMiqulu okanye nguMkomishinari weZifungo.

Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Umnyenyevu wokubonelela ngerhafu unikwa imibutho engajonganga kwenza nzuzo, esekelwe ukubayinzuzo kuluntu ngokubanzi. Nangona kunjalo, lo mnyenyevu wokubonelela uyakufumaneka kuphela kwimibutho ehambisana nemimiselo yoMthetho weMibutho eNgajonganga kwenza Nzuzo (Non-profit Organisations Act, 1997), kunye nemithetho eyayamene nalo.
Imibutho enqwenela ukwenza izicelo zomnyenyevu wokungabandakanywa kufanele ziwele phantsi kwelinye lala macandelo alandelayo:
Iqumrhu lokugcina ngentembeko elinomqulu wokuliseka kunye nencwadi yesivumelwano sasemthethweni sentembeko, esibhaliswe kwiNqununu yeNkundla ePhezulu.
Iqumrhu labantu. Iqumrhu labantu abahlangene ngokuzithandela elilawulwa ngumgaqo-siseko.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Imibutho okungokunje enganikwanga umnyenyevu ogunyazisiweyo wokungabandakanywa kwirhafu yengeniso-mali, ingathumela ifom yesicelo egcwalisiweyo ehamba nemiqulu yokuxhasa eyimfuneko, ndawonye nesibhengezo sesithembiso esibhaliweyo nesisayiniweyo, apho abantu abenza lo msebenzi ngentembeko bathembisa ngokuhambisana nemimiselo yeCandelo 30 loMthetho weMibutho eNgajonganga kwenza Nzuzo (Non-profit Organisations Act, 1997).
Le miqulu yokuxhasa ilandelayo kufuneka ikhaphe isicelo:
o inkampani: Faka ikopi yeMimiselo kunye neMigaqo yokuManyana (ebandakanya iikopi zazo zonke izindululo ezizodwa ezibhalisiweyo ezilungisa imimiselo kunye nemigaqo)
o iqumrhu lokugcina ngentembeko: Faka ikopi yeencwadi zezivumelwano zasemthethweni zentembeko kunye nazo naziphina iincwadi zezivumelwano zasemthethweni ezilandelayo zokulungisa o iqumrhu labantu: Faka ikopi yomgaqo-siseko wakutshanje.
Imibutho esekwe ngenjongo ephambili yokunika izipho zemali yokufunda ngenxa yokugqwesa, iibhasari kunye nezipho zokufunda, uphando kunye nokufundisa, kufuneka, ngaphezulu kwale miqulu ingentla, igcwalise iSibhengezo seSithembiso eSibhaliweyo ekuthiwa yi-EI 3 Written Undertaking.
Izikolo zoluntu kunye nezizimeleyo (ezabucala), amaziko emfundo ephakamileyo, amaziko emfundo esisiseko noqeqesho lwabantu abadala (i-ABET), ndawonye namaziko emfundo noqeqesho oluqhubekayo (i-FET), kufuneka zifake ikopi yesatifiketi sobhaliso esikhutshwe nguGunyaziwe obandakanyekayo weMfundo.
Ifom egcwalisiweyo, ikunye nemiqulu efanelekileyo, kufuneka ibuyiselwe kule adresi ilandelayo:
Entla
 [UMthetho wokuLungisa weMithetho yokuRhafa, njengoko ilungisiwe liCandelo 78, neCandelo 63, neCandelo 198]

Inkampani/Iqumrhu elingavulelekanga/Iqumrhu lokugcina ngentembeko, lilele.
Umrhafi umkile wayokuhlala kwelinye ilizwe.
Ingxelo yomrhafi iphawulwe njengelifa, umzekelo, ukubhubha, ukungakwazi ukuhlawula amatyala, ukupheliswa kwenkampani.
Kukhutshwe isigunyaziso okanye umyalelo wokubizwa wonyaka werhafu ongqalileyo.
Ifom yeli xesha okanye yalo nyaka khange ikhutshwe.
Umrhafi akanaxanduva lemfaneleko kulo nyaka werhafu umiyo.
Isicelo sokongezelwa ixesha ligqitha ngaphaya kwethuba ekufikelelwa kulo elivumeleke kwicandelo lomrhafi.
Ingxelo yomrhafi ikwinkqubo yokuba isuswe komnye ummandla itshintshelwe komnye.

Inkcazelo
Le nkonzo isebenziseka kumntu ozakubangumhlali wesigxina onqwenela ukwenza isicelo sokuhlala isigxina ngenxa yokuba eyifemeli yommi okanye yomhlali osisigxina waseMzantsi Afrika kwinqanaba lokuqala lokuzalana. Ngeenjongo zokuhlala isigxina, amalungu efemeli akwinqanaba lokuqala lokuzalana amiselwa njengamalungu enzalelwane kunye nabantwana abamkelwe ngabantu abangabazelanga njengababo ngokwasemthethweni okanye abazali abamkele abantwana abangabazelanga njengababo ngokwasemthethweni kunye nabazali bomnye umtshato .
Izicelo zingenziwa kuyo nayiphina i-ofisi yezeKhaya okanye kwindlu yozakuzo yaseMzantsi Afrika okanye kwiziko elimele uMzantsi Afrika ukubangaba wenza isicelo ukwilizwe langaphandle.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ummi okanye umhlali osisigxina waseMzantsi Afrika makahambise isibhengezo sesithembiso malunga noxanduva lwezemali, unyango kunye nesiqu somenzi-sicelo. Kodwa ke, xa isihlobo ingumzali womntwana ongekabinalungelo lokuzithabathela izigqibo ngokwasemthethweni, akukho mfuneko yesibhengezo sesithembiso.

Iinkonzo zabantu
Isicelo senkxaso yokunakekela omnye umntu
Isicelo senkxaso yokunakekela omnye umntu
Inkcazelo
Inkxaso yokunakekela omnye umntu (maintenance) luxanduva lokunika omnye umntu, umzekelo umntwana ongekabinamalungelo okuzithabathela izigqibo ngokwasemthethweni, ukutya, indlu, impahla yokunxiba, imfundo kunye nonakekelo lonyango, okanye ukulungiselela omnye umntu iindlela nezinto eziyimfuneko ukuze anikwe ezi zinto zidingekayo kwimpilo yakhe. Olu xanduva lwasemthethweni lokunika inkxaso lubizwa ngokuba 'luxanduva lokuxhasa okanye 'luxanduva lokusapota'.
Ngubani ekufuneka akhuphe inkxaso yokunakekela omnye umntu (isapoti)?
Uxanduva lokusapota lusekelwe kubudlelwane begazi, ukwamkelwa komntwana abengowomnye umntu okanye abantu ngokusemthethweni okanye kwimeko yokokuba aba bantu batshatile.
Umntwana kufuneka asapotwe okanye axhaswe
Ngabazali bakhe, nokuba batshatile, bayahlalisana, bohlukene okanye baqhawule umtshato (badivosile), kubandakanywa abazali abamkele umntwana wabangowabo ngokusemthethweni; kunye/okanye
Ungabanga isapoti eqiqileyo eyimfuneko ukuze unike umntwana okanye omnye umntu onelungelo lokusapotwa indlela yokuphila nokukhula okufanelekileyo. Oku kubandakanya ukunika izinto ezidingekayo empilweni ezifana nokutya, impahla yokunxiba kunye nendlu, ndawonye nokuhlawuwulela imfundo efanelekileyo. Inkundla ingayalela nokuba utata womntwana enze igalelo kwintlawulo yeendleko zokulungiselelwa komntwana kunye nenkxaso ukusukela kumhla wokuzalwa komntwana ukuyakutsho kumhla wokunikwa komyalelo wesapoti. Inkundla inganika nomyalelo wokuhlawulwa kweendleko zonyango okanye ingayalela ukuba umntwana abhaliswe phantsi kwesikim sonyango somnye wabazali njengomntu oxhomekekileyo. Ukwenzela ukuba inkundla ikwazi ukukhupha umyalelo wesapoti ofanelekileyo, bobabini abazali mabanike inkundla ubungqina beendleko zabo.
Imbono yakho ngokuziphatha komnye umzali ayilichaphazeli ilungelo labantwana bakho lokufumana isapoti. Kukwafuneka uyihlawule isapoti, nokubangaba omnye lo umzali uphinde watshata;
uhambisana (unobudlelwane) nomnye umntu;
Uxanduva lwakho lokuhlawula isapoti kunye nelungelo lakho lokufikelela ebantwaneni bakho yimibandela emibini eyahlukene kakhulu kwaye ayingqamananga tu. Ngaphezu koko, abantwana bakhe nawuphina umzali abaluchaphazeli uxanduva lokusapota. Kodwa ke, nangona kunjalo, imali yesapoti ingalungiswa ukubangaba omnye umbandakanyeki uzisa isicelo esinjalo.
Ukuze ufumane inkcazelo ebanzi, yiya kwiSebe lezoBulungisa noPhuhliso loMgaqo-siseko.
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Yenza isicelo sesapoti kwinkundla kamantyi ekwisithili ohlala kuso.
Igosa lesapoti kunye nomphandi bayakuphanda isibango sakho kwaye bajonge iimeko zakho.
Inkundla iyakukhuphela umphenduli (lo mntu kwenziwa kuye isibango) isamani (incwadi eyalela umntu ukuba aye enkundleni) ukuze aye kuvela enkundleni ngomhla ochaziweyo ukuze kuxoxwe ngalo mbandela.
Umphenduli ke angakhetha ukuba avume ukuhlawula le sapoti ngale ndlela ibangwa ngayo, okanye aye kuphikisana nalo mba enkundleni.
Ukubangaba umphenduli uyavuma ukuhlawula isapoti njengoko ibangwa, umantyi uyakuphonononga imiqulu efanelekileyo. Uyakuthi ke akhuphe umyalelo, kwaye angagqiba ekubeni enze njalo ngaphandle kokufuna ukuba ababandakanyeki bavele enkundleni.
Inkundla ingayalela ukuba imali yesapoti ihlawulwe ngenye yezi ndlela zilandelayo:
Kwi-ofisi kamantyi ekwindawo umntu ahlala kuyo okanye kuyo nayiphina enye i-ofisi karhulumente echongelwe le meko
Kwi-akhawunti yebhanki okanye yequmrhu lokwakha echongwe ngulo mntu ubandakanyekayo
Nqo kulo mntu ufaneleke afumane le mali
Imithetho esetyenziswayo
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Izikhalazo ziyakuphathwa ngokukhawuleza nangobunono kangangoko kunokwenzeka
Akukho xesha libekiweyo kule nkonzo. Inkqubo iyonke, ukusukela ekuhambiseni isicelo ukuya kutsho ekufumaneni intlawulo yakho yokuqala yesapoti, ingathabatha iiveki ezininzi, kuxhomekeke kwintsebenziswano yabo bobabini ababandakanyeki.
Amangqina ahamba inkqubo, kubandakanywa umntu obanga isapoti, bavumelekile bafumane izibonelelo ezimiselweyo zenkxaso nohambo. Kodwa ke, inkundla iyakwenza isigqibo, ngokubona kwayo, malunga nokuba eso sibonelelo siyakuhlawulwa na kumntu onganikwa umyalelo wokuba ahlawule isapoti.
Umntu obanga isapoti makenze isicelo kwigosa lesapoti ukuze ahlawulwe iimali zamangqina.
Iindleko
Le nkonzo ayihlawulelwa.

Inkcazelo
Nawuphina umntu onepemethe yokuhlala isigxina eMzantsi Afrika uyavumeleka enze isicelo sobumi baseMzantsi Afrika ngokwenkqubo yokwamkelwa njengommi emva kweminyaka emihlanu engumhlali osisigxina.
Nawuphina umntu otshate ummi waseMzantsi Afrika uyavumeleka amkelwe njengommi kwiminyaka emibini emva kokuba efumene ipemethe yokuhlala isigxina ekhutshwe ngexesha lomtshato.
Umntwana oneminyaka yobudala engaphantsi kwama 21, onepemethe yokuhlala isigxina, uyavumeleka amkelwe njengommi kwamsinyane nje emva kokuba ikhutshiwe ipemethe.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Umzali onoxanduva angenza isicelo egameni lomntwana ongekabinalungelo lokuzenzela izigqibo ngokusemthethweni, ukubangaba phofu lo mntwana uhlala isigxina nangokusemthethweni eMzantsi Afrika.
Kuyakukhutshwa incwadi yesazisi kwaye ithunyelwe kumenzi-sicelo.
Abenzi-zicelo abalelwe izicelo bayakuxelelwa ngokunjalo.

Ishishini
Isicelo sepemethe umntu oneshishini lakhe
Isicelo sepemethe yokuhlala isigxina - umntu oneshishini lakhe
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Le nkonzo isebenziseka kumntu welizwe langaphandle ojonge ukuseka ishishini eMzantsi Afrika; okanye osele enepemethe yeshishini ukuze aqhube ishishini kweli lizwe; okanye ojonge ukutyala imali kwishishini esele likhona kweli lizwe.
Izicelo zingathunyelwa kuyo nayiphina i-ofisi yezeKhaya kwiphondo ojonge ukuqhubela kulo ishishini. Yenza isicelo kwindlu yozakuzo yaseMzantsi Afrika okanye kwiziko elimele uMzantsi Afrika ukubangaba ukwilizwe langaphandle.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Umgcini nomhloli wee-akhawunti zemali olilungu lequmrhu labagcini nabahloli bee-akhawunti zemali (chartered accountant), omele indawo yakho, kufuneka ahambise uqinisekiso lokuba igalelo lemali emiselweyo kwixabiso lempahla nezinto (ekujongwe kulo) elikwiincwadi zeshishini, lityaliwe. Igalelo lemali emiselweyo liyi R2,5 million kwaye lingabekelwa bucala okanye lincitshiswe kuphela xangaba oko kuthathwa ngokuba kungumnqweno welizwe okanye xangaba oko kucelwe liSebe lezoRhwebo naMashishini.

Isicelo sokuqonda udidi lwesityalo
Isicelo sokuqonda udidi lwesityalo (ukubhalisa udidi)
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
ISebe lezoLimo ligcina izintlu zeendidi ngokuphathelele kwezolimo, imifuno nezityalo zeziqhamo. Ubhengezo lwezityalo ngeenjongo zomThetho kwakunye nokuquka iindidi kwizintlu kwenziwa ngokulandela isicelo. Isizathu sokufikelela isigqibo sixhomekeke ekubalulekeni kohlobo lwesityalo kuqoqosho lwaseMzantsi Afrika.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
o intlawulo emiselweyo yesicelo novavanyo o imbewu okanye izixhobo zokumilisa o ugunyaziso olubhaliweyo oluvela kumnini-sityalo, ukuba awusimilisanga, wasikhetha okanye waqhubela phambili udidi.
Bonisa ngokucacileyo kuthotho lwemibuzo yobuchwepheshe ukuba zeziphi ezinye iindidi ezaziwayo eMzantsi Afrika, ekufuneka udidi olutsha luthelekiswe nazo ukumisela ukuzibalula.
Kukho iintsuku ezimiselweyo ekufuneka kuthunyelwe ngazo amaxwebhu nezixhobo zokumilisa kuMbhalisi. Iinkcukacha zezi ntsuku, inani lezixhobo zokumilisa ekufuneka zithunyelwe nalapho kufuneka zithunyelwe khona, ziyafumaneka kuMbhalisi.
Xa ukhuselo ngokwemiqathango yamalungelo ommilisi wezityalo nalo lufuneka, abenzi bezicelo bakhuthazwa ukuthumela izicelo ngaxeshanye ukulondoloza ixesha nemali.
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Inkqubo yokufaka udidi kuluhlu iya kuthatha ithuba elinye lokulima ubuncinane.

Iindleko
Intlawulo yesicelo malunga nokuqonda udidi: R790
Intlawulo yovavanyo malunga nokuqonda udidi:
o ihlelo A (ezolimo, imifuno, izityalo zamadlelo nombona): R900
o ihlelo B (umbona omhlophe nobomvu): R1 100
Isicelo sokuguqula okanye ukongeza igama lodidi olusele lufakwe kuluhlu lweendidi: R1 500

Isicelo sokubhalisa njengomnikazi-fektri eyenza izinto ezithile phantsi kwe-AGOA

Inkcazelo
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Le fom yesicelo kufuneka igcwaliswe ngumenzi-sicelo, hayi umntu wesithathu, kungenjalo isicelo asiyi kuqwalaselwa.
Nceda ubhekise kwisikhokelo sesicelo ukuze sikuncede ngenkqubo yelayisensi.
o igama lokurhweba leshishini lakho o indawo elimi kuyo elishishini (umzekelo: Plot 10)
o igama lesitalato kunye nenombolo yeshishini o ummandla wedolophu elimi kuwo ishishini o isixeko okanye idolophu elimi kuyo ishishini; kunye o nekhowudi yesitalato sommandla wedolophu elimi kuwo ishishini.
Icandelo elithi Authority to Apply (Igunya lokwenza isicelo) maligcwaliswe ngumnikazi-shishini ozimele yedwa, umqondisi, oogxa bentsebenziswano, ilungu, ilungu eliphathiswe iqumrhu ngentembeko, okanye umntu ophethe ishishini xa usenza isicelo sokubhalisela ukubangumnikazi-fektri ochongekileyo malunga nemirhumo yempahla engena elizweni kunye nerhafu yempahla nezinto kunye neelayisensi ezithile phantsi kwe-AGOA .
Igama lomenzi-sicelo okanye igama lobhaliso lweshishini, hayi igama lorhwebo, kufuneka liboniswe kweli candela.
o apho kubonakala khona inkwenkwezana ekuthiwa yi-asterisk (*), susa nayiphina efaneleke njalo.
Kwicandelo le Declaration (ISibhengezo), faka oku kulandelayo:
o oonobumba bamagama okuqala kunye nefani yomntu owenza isicelo sokunikwa ilayisensi o isikhundla somntu owenza isicelo, umzekelo, uMqondisi, uManejala, uMnikazi o lo mntu wenza isicelo kufuneka atyikitye (asayine) ifom yesicelo o umhla esisayinwe ngawo esi sicelo o indawo esisayinelwe kuyo esi sicelo.
Faka kwifom yesicelo iikopi eziluqobo lwazo okanye eziqinisekisiweyo zale miqulu ilandelayo:
o isatifiketi sobhaliso lweshishini njengoko sikhutshwe nguMphathi woBhaliso lweeNkampani okanye iNqununu yeNkundla ePhezulu kwimeko yeQumrhu lokuGcina ngeNtembeko.
o isindululo okanye imvume okanye elinye igunya elibandakanyekayo.
o iincwadi zezazisi xa umntu engummi waseMzantsi Afrika
Yomntu ongahlali kweli lizwe iqumrhu elingavulelekanga kunye nequmrhu lokugcina ngentembeko - onke amalungu, ogxa bentsebenziswano okanye amalungu aphathiswe iqumrhu ngentembeko inkampani - bonke abaqondisi, kubandakanywa umqondisi olawulayo kunye nomqondisi wezemali.

Le fom yesicelo kufuneka igcwaliswe ngumenzi-sicelo, hayi umntu wesithathu - kungenjalo isicelo asiyi kuqwalaselwa.
Nceda ubhekise kwisikhokelo sesicelo ukuze sikuncede ngenkqubo yelayisensi.
o khangela ibhokisi yokuhlola yoMngenisi wempahla, phantsi kobhaliso.
Kwicandelo elithi Importer Particulars IiNkcukacha zoMngenisi wempahla nezinto ezithile eLizweni, chaza o igama lokurhweba leshishini lakho o igama nenombolo yesitalato seshishini o igama kunye nenombolo yomgangatho wesakhiwo eliqhutyelwa kuso eli shishini o ummandla wedolophu elimi kuwo ishishini o isixeko okanye idolophu elimi kuyo ishishini; kunye o ikhowudi yesitalato sommandla wedolophu elimi kuwo ishishini o ngubani oyakubanoxanduva lokubhala nokuthumela imiqulu kwi-South African Revenue Service; kunye nokuba o ingaba nguwe oyakubhala kwaye athumele le miqulu, okanye ingaba kuyakutyunjwa i-eyijenti ukuze yenze oku, na.
Icandelo elithi Authority to Apply (Igunya lokwenza isicelo) maligcwaliswe ngumntu (ongumnikazi-shishini ozimele yedwa, umqondisi, oogxa bentsebenziswano, ilungu, ilungu eliphathiswe iqumrhu ngentembeko, okanye umntu ophethe ishishini) owenza isicelo sokubhalisela ukubangumngenisi wempahla nezinto ezithile elizweni.

o isindululo okanye imvume okanye elinye igunya elibandakanyekayo.

Inkcazelo
Le nkonzo inika inkcazelo malunga nendlela yokubhalisela ukubuyiselwa imali yi-South African Revenue Service. Le mali ibuyiswayo sisaphulelo kwintlawulo yokungenisa impahla nezinto ehlawuleka xa ungenisa impahla nezinto ezithile kweli lizwe.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Umenzi-sicelo, hayi umntu wesithathu, kufuneka ibenguye ogcwalise ifom yesicelo (DA 185), kungenjalo isicelo asiyi kuqwalaselwa.
o igama lokurhweba leshishini lakho o igama nenombolo yesitalato seshishini elibuyiselwayo o igama kunye nenombolo yomgangatho wesakhiwo ekuqhutyelwa kuso eli shishini o ummandla wedolophu elimi kuwo ishishini o isixeko okanye idolophu elimi kuyo ishishini o ikhowudi yesitalato sommandla wedolophu elimi kuwo ishishini.
Icandelo elithi Authority to apply (Igunya lokwenza isicelo), maligcwaliswe ngumenzi-sicelo (UMnikazi-shishini oZimele Yedwa, UMqondisi, Oogxa beNtsebenziswano, iLungu, iLungu eliPhathiswe iQumrhu ngeNtembeko okanye umntu ophethe naliphina elinye iqumrhu) xa usenza isicelo sokuba ngumsebenzisi wokubuyiswa kwemali.
Igama lomenzi-sicelo okanye igama lobhaliso lweshishini, hayi igama lorhwebo, kufuneka liboniswe kweli candelo.
Apho kubonakala khona inkwenkwezana ekuthiwa yi-asterisk (*), susa nayiphina efaneleke njalo.
o inkcazelo yempahla nezinto eziyakugcinwa kwishishini lokubuyiselwa imali o izinga lemirhumo yentlawulo okanye imiba yempahla nezinto ezingeniswayo eziyakugcinwa kwishishini lokubuyiselwa imali o imiba yokubuyiselwa imali phantsi kwamanani oludwe lwenkqubo yesi 3, 4, 5 kunye neyesi 6
o inkcazelo yemveliso engeniswa kweli lizwe okanye impahla nezinto ezingeniswa kweli lizwe.
Kwicandelo le Declaration (Isibhengezo), kufuneka ufake:
o oonobumba bamagama okuqala kunye nefani yomntu owenza isicelo sokunikwa ilayisensi o isikhundla somntu owenza isicelo, umzekelo, UMqondisi, uManejala, uMnikazi o lo mntu wenza isicelo kufuneka atyikitye (asayine) ifom yesicelo o umhla esisayinwe ngawo esi sicelo o indawo esisayinelwe kuyo esi sicelo.
Nceda ufake iikopi eziluqobo lwazo okanye eziqinisekisiweyo zale miqulu ilandelayo:
o isatifiketi sobhaliso lweshishini njengoko sikhutshwe nguMphathi woBhaliso lweeNkampani okanye iNqununu yeNkundla ePhezulu kwimeko yeQumrhu lokuGcina ngeNtembeko o isindululo okanye imvume okanye elinye igunya njengoko kubandakanyeka o iphepha lemvume (ipemethe) yeSebe lezoRhwebo naMashishini ukuba iyabandakanyeka o iindlela zokubala ukubangaba wenza isicelo phantsi komba wokubuyiselwa imali ku 607.04.10 , 607.04.10 , 607.04.10 naku 607.04.10 
o iincwadi zezazisi xa umntu enguMmi waseMzantsi Afrika okanye iincwadi zePaspoti xa umntu engahlali kweli lizwe:
kumntu ubuqu bakhe kooGxa beNtsebenziswano kwiQumrhu eliNgavulelekanga neQumrhu lokuGcina ngeNtembeko - Onke aMalungu/ooGxa beNtsebenziswano/ aMalungu aPhathiswe iQumrhu ngeNtembeko
KwiNkampani - Bonke abaqondisi, kubandakanywa uMqondisi oLawulayo kunye noMqondisi weZemali.

Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Inkampani yelizwe laphesheya ayinakwenza sicelo sokubhalisa eMzantsi Afrika. Isicelo sokubhalisa izichumisi singenziwa kuphela yinkampani ebhaliswe kweli lizwe, ummi weRiphabhlikhi yaseMzantsi Afrika, okanye iqumrhu elisemthethweni elibhaliswe eMzantsi Afrika.
Ubhaliso luyakwenziwa xa ngaba ngexesha lokubhaliswa kwenzeka ezi zinto zilandelayo:
izinto eziqulathwe sisichumisi esibandakanyekayo azohlukanga kweziya sele zibhalisiwe iinkcukacha kunye namagama asetyenzisiweyo avunyiweyo wemibhalo yokuphawula okuqulathiweyo okanye inkonkxa akayi kutshintshwa ngaphandle kokuba kuqale kufunyanwe imvume ebhaliweyo esuka kuMphathi woBhaliso (Registrar)
imiqathango ebekwe ngexesha lobhaliso iyalandelwa ubhaliso olubandakanyekayo aluyi kugqithiselwa ubungakanani beebhegi neenkonkxa abunakuguqulwa ngaphandle kokuba kuqale kufunyanwe imvume ebhaliweyo esuka kuMphathi woBhaliso.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Isicelo sokubhaliswa kokutya kwemfuyo yasefama kunye nezichumisi siqulathe ezi zinto zilandelayo incwadi yangaphezulu esuka kumntu obhalisileyo okanye ummeli otyunjiweyo. Incwadi yangaphezulu kufuneka ibandakanye ezi zinto zilandelayo:
o igama lemveliso o inombolo yobhaliso ukubangaba imveliso seyibhalisiwe o isizathu sokufaka isicelo (nokuba sisicelo esitsha, isicelo sokulungisa, isicelo sokubhalisa ufakelo ekuthiwa yi-daughter registration)
o iincwadi zokuvuma ukubangaba kufuneka imvume ephuma kumntu obhalisileyo (imvume yokubhalisa ufakelo ekuthiwa yi-daughter registration okanye imvume yokusebenzisa igama lemveliso yenye inkampani kumbhalo wokuphawula okuqulathiweyo)
Umntu otyunjwe ngokwasemthethweni, ekufuneka ngokukhethekayo abengumntu wonxulumano loMphathi woBhaliso kwinkampani, makasayine iifom zesicelo.
Igama nenombolo yobhaliso yemveliso mayisetyenziswe njengoko kungqaliwe kwisatifiketi sobhaliso. Naluphina utshintsho kwigama, nokuba luncinane kangakanani na, luyakuthathwa ngokuba sisilungiso.

Inkcazelo
Nawuphina umntu owayeke wabangummi, ngokuzalwa okanye ngokomnombo, owathi wabuyeka ubumi baseMzantsi Afrika okanye obu bumi baseMzantsi Afrika baziphelela ngokwabo, angenza isicelo sokuphinda abengummi waseMzansti Afrika.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Hambisa incwadi engqina ukuba umenzi-sicelo ngoku uhlala eMzantsi Afrika.
Hambisa ikopi yencwadi yesazisi yomenzi-sicelo.
Hambisa ikopi yesatifiketi somtshato, ukuba oko kuyabandakanyeka.

Isicelo soMhlaba weZolimo woMbuso

Iindleko
Inkcazelo
UMhlaba weZolimo oleleyo woMbuso uyaqeshiswa ngeenjongo zolimo ngokunika okanye ngokunganiki ithuba lokukhetha ukuwuthenga, kuxhomekeke kubume balo mhlaba (ngaba kukho isibango na kulo mhlaba). Izivumelwano zokuqeshisa ezinika ithuba lokuthenga ziyahlaziyeka qho emva kweminyaka emithathu.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Xa umhlaba wezolimo woMbuso ulungele ukuqeshiswa, iSebe leZolimo liyazisa ngawo ngokuwu-advethayiza ngokwezaziso kwiindawo ezibonakala kakuhle kwingingqi, ezifana nee-ofisi zoomantyi, izikhululo zamapolisa nakumaphephandaba.
Yenza isicelo kulo mntu uxelwe kwisaziso.

Isicelo sokuphinda unikwe incwadi yesazisi
Isicelo sokuphinda unikwe incwadi yesazisi
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Incwadi yesazisi (ID) yincwadi eyazisa nengqina ngomntu. Inikwa abemi baseMzantsi Afrika okanye abantu abaneepemethe zokuhlala isigxina kweli lizwe abaneminyaka eli 16 nangaphezulu.
Incwadi yesazisi iyaphinda inikwe kwaba bantu balandelayo:
Abantu abaguqukelwe ziimeko zobumi.
Abasetyhini abangene kubume bomtshato okanye abangathanda ukubuyela kuyo nayiphina kwiifani zabo zangaphambili.
Abantu abahlala kumazwe angaphandle ixeshana elifutshane kodwa ababekade benayo incwadi yesazisi ngaphambili.
Abangeni kweli lizwe abanepemethe esebenzisekayo yokuhlala isigxina kweli lizwe.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Hambisa iifoto ezimbini ezilingana kwincwadi yesazisi.
Nyathelisa iminwe (iifingaprinti) ukuze ifakwe kuvimba woBhaliso lweNani neeNkcukacha zaBantu.
Khupha isatifiketi somtshato ukubangaba utshatile.
Owasetyhini owenza isicelo sencwadi yesazisi kwaye enqwenela ukuphinda abuyele kuyo nayiphina ifani kwiifani awayekade ezibiza ngazo, makathi thaca ubungqina bokuba uvumelekile asebenzise loo fani.
Umntu ongumngeni kweli lizwe owenza isicelo sencwadi yesazisi makafake kwesi sicelo ipemethe yokuhlala isigxina, isatifiketi sokwamkelwa njengommi emva kokuhlala ixesha elithile okanye isatifiketi somnyenyevu wokungafunwa pemethe.
Entla
Entla

Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
lo mntwana wazalelwa ngaphandle komtshato kwaye umama wakhe utshate omnye umntu ongenguye uyise ozele lo mntwana umtshato notata womntwana uchithiwe ngokoqhawulo lomtshato (ngokwedivosi) okanye ngenxa yokubhubha, kwaye umama uphinde watshata njengomhlolokazi okanye umntu oqhawule umtshato, umama wakhe ubuyele kwifani yaphambi komtshato okanye kwifani yomtshato wangaphambili ukuzalwa komntwana owazalelwa ngaphandle komtshato kubhaliswe phantsi kwefani yotata wakhe omzeleyo.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Veza imvume ebhaliweyo evela kulo myeni umntwana azakusebenzisa ifani yakhe.
Ukuze kuguqulwe (apho kubandakanyeka khona), iyafuneka imvume ebhaliweyo evela kubazali bobabini, ndawonye nezizathu ezaneleyo, ezibhaliweyo.
Iyafuneka imvume ebhaliweyo yotata ozele lo mntwana, ngaphandle kokuba isuselwe ecaleni yinkundla enamandla negunya lokwenza njalo.

Ubudlelwane kunye nobume beemvakalelo zesondo
Ukutshata
Ukutshata phantsi komthetho wesiko lesiqhelo
Isicelo sokutshata phantsi komthetho wesiko lesiqhelo
Inkcazelo
Umtshato wesiko lesiqhelo ungenelwa phantsi komthetho wesiko lesiqhelo. Xa umyeni etshate umfazi phantsi komthetho wentlalo yabemi, aze agqibe ekubeni atshate abanye abafazi, aba bafazi bangabanye bayakuvunywa phantsi komthetho wesiko lesiqhelo.
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Umtshato kufuneka kuthetha-thethwane ngawo, kuvuyiswane ngawo kwaye ungenelwe ngokuhambisana nomthetho wesiko lesiqhelo.
Abenzi-zicelo abahlala kwimimandla yasezilalini kufuneka bakhuphe incwadi evela kwinkokheli yemveli.
Abenzi-zicelo abahlala kwimimandla yasezidolophini kufuneka bakhuphe incwadi ebhaliweyo nefungelweyo (i-affidavit).
Ukuze umtshato uqhubeke, abatshati kunye namangqina aphuma kwifemeli nganye, kufuneka babekhona.

Isatifiketi esingafinyezwanga: iiveki ezintandathu ukuya kwezisibhozo

Iinkonzo zamabanjwa aseMzantsi Afrika abanjwe kuma
Isicelo sesatifiketi esiphuma emapoliseni esichaza

Iinkonzo zabantu
Ukumka eMzantsi Afrika
IiNkonzo zamazwe angaphandle
Inkcazelo
Isatifiketi sokubhubha ngumqulu ogunyazisiweyo okhutshelwa ifemeli yomntu obhubhileyo xa kubhaliswe ukubhubha. Xa umntu welizwe langaphandle ebhubhele eMzantsi Afrika, ingxelo igcinwa kuvimba weengxelo kwaye ifemeli yakhe inikwa isatifiketi esipheleleyo. Kungenziwa izicelo kuyo nayiphina i-ofisi yezeKhaya okanye kwiNdlu yoZakuzo yaseMzantsi Afrika okanye kwiZiko elimele uMzantsi Afrika ukubangaba wenza isicelo ukwilizwe langaphandle.
Ukuze ufumane inkcazelo ebanzi, yiya kwiSebe lezaseKhaya
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Bhala incwadi enazo zonke iinkcukacha zomfi, uze uyiposele kwi-ofisi yezeKhaya ekufuphi kuwe ukubangaba akukho ofisi yezeKhaya kummandla ohlala kuwo.
Akukho mngcwabo uyakuqhubeka ungekho umyalelo wokungcwaba. Umyalelo wokungcwaba sisatifiketi esinika igunya lomngcwabo kunye nokususwa kwesidumbu kummandla umfi abhubhele kuwo sisiwe kummandla ekuyakungcwatyelwa kuwo. Umyalelo wokungcwaba ungakhutshwa:
Liziko labangcwabi eligunyaziselwe ukukhupha imiyalelo yokungcwaba.
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Isatifiketi esifinyeziweyo: Sikhutshwa kwakube kubhaliswe ukubhubha.
Iindleko

Isatifiketi esingafinyezwanga: R45

Inkcazelo
Abemi baseMzantsi Afrika okanye abantu abaneepemethe zokuhlala isigxina kweli abafuna ukutshintsha ii-adresi zabo zokuhlala okanye zokuposa kwiNcwadi yeLizwe yokuBhalisa iNani neeNkcukacha zaBantu, bangenza izicelo kuyo nayiphina i-ofisi yezeKhaya. Izicelo zingenziwa nakwindlu yozakuzo yaseMzantsi Afrika okanye kwiziko elimele uMzantsi Afrika ukubangaba wenza isicelo ukwilizwe langaphandle.

Inkcazelo
Into ekujoliswe kuyo ngokubanzi kwixesha elide elizayo kukuthoba imirhumo yokurhafela impahla nezinto ezingena kweli, kodwa kunyuswe imirhumo engephi kwiimveliso ezichaziweyo phantsi kweemeko ezikhethekileyo nezizodwa. Ukunyuswa komrhumo kuqwalaselwa ngokuxhaswayo kuphela xangaba oko kunyuswa kuyakwenza igalelo kuphuhliso lwamashishini ngokuhambisana neenjongo zelizwe zoqoqosho.

Inkcazelo
Iimpazamo ezidla ngokufunyanwa kwiincwadi zezazisi, kwaye umenzi-sicelo anganqwenela ukuzilungisisa, zibandakanya ezi zilandelayo:
igama elingachanekanga kunye nefani okanye ifani engachanekanga ifoto engeyiyo i-adresi engachanekanga umhla wokuzalwa ongachanekanga isini (ukubayindoda okanye owasetyhini) esingesiso.

Ukutshata
Isicelo sokubhalisa umtshato wesiko lesiqhelo
Isicelo sokubhalisa umtshato wesiko lesiqhelo
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Umtshato wesiko lesiqhelo ungabhaliswa ngokoMthetho wokuVunywa kweMitshato yeSiko leSiqhelo (Recognition of Customary Marriages Act, 1998). Akukhathaliseki nokuba wawutshate ninina. Kwiimeko apho omnye omlingane ebhubhile, lo mlingane usaphilayo angawubhalisa lo mtshato. Ubhaliso lungenziwa kuyo nayiphina i-ofisi yezeKhaya. Kufuneka kubekho amangqina amabini akwaziyo nanegunya lokungqina.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Abatshati kunye namangqina kufuneka bakhuphe iincwadi ezisebenzisekayo zezazisi.
Hambisa ubungqina bothetha-thethwano ngomtshato (ukuba oko kunokwenzeka).
Kwiimeko apho ugxa oyindoda kumtshato wesiko lesiqhelo enqwenela ukungenela omnye umtshato wesiko lesiqhelo, kufuneka anxulumane neNkundla ePhakamileyo ukuze afumane umyalelo oyakugqalisela inkqubo yakhe yempahla nezinto zasemtshatweni.
Entla
Entla

Isatifiketi somtshato esifinyeziweyo: Sikhutshwa kwangoko.
Isatifiketi somtshato esingafinyezwanga: Sithabatha iiveki ezi 6 ukuya kwezisi 8.

Iindleko

Isatifiketi somtshato esingafinyezwanga: R53

Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Xa unikezela iscelo,fumana I risithi uyilondoloze njengesiqinisekiso sokufaka isicelo.
Faka isibheno zingekapheli intsuku ezingamashumi alithoba usakuba ufumenene iziphumo zesicelo.
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Kungathabatha iiveki ezine ukuphonononga isicelo.
Unontlalontle umema bonke abadla indima kuphononongo lwezicelo njengo nempilo nabaseburhulumenteni apha ekuhlaleni ukuba baphande ngendawo abazakuhlaliswa abantu abadala.
Ngamnye ngamnye Kwabadlala indima kuphononongo lwezicelo,uza kwenza uxwebhu le ngxelo ngakufumanisile.
Iingxelo zabo zithunyelwa e ofisini eyeCandelo lezoPhuhliso zaseKuhlaleni.

Inkqubo emayilandelwe

Iindleko
Inkcazelo
I-SITE luhlobo lwerhafu yomqeshwa ebandakanyeka kuphela kwintlawulo yomvuzo osalayo emva kokuxhuzulwa kwento yonke ukuya kufikelela kwi R60 000. I-SITE iqulungqwa ekupheleni kwethuba lerhafu, kwaye ingamela kuphela inxenye yerhafu yomqeshwa apha enyakeni.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Iinkampani nenkampani zabantu abambalwa zabucala (closed corporations) ezingabhaliswanga njengangoku kwi-SARS ukulungiselela irhafu yabaqeshwa, kufuneka zibhalise kwangexesha ukuze zihlawule irhafu yabaqeshwa  kwabo baqeshwa bakulungeleyo oku.

Isicelo sokubhalisa isiza njengeziko lwezolimo nge
Isicelo sokubhalisa isiza njengeziko lwezolimo ngenjongo yokuqokelela impahla yofuzo (genetic material)
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Isiza apho impahla yofuzo (genetic material) iqokelelwa, ihlolwe, ihlelwe, ipakwe, ifakwe iileyibhile, igcinwe yaye ithengiswe khona, singabhaliswa njengeziko xa:
amalungiselelo amiselweyo efumaneka kwisiza esinjalo imisebenzi yobuchwepheshe kwisiza esinjalo, efana nonakekelo lwezilwanyana ezigcinwe apho, ukuqokelela, ukuhlola, ukuhlela, ukupakisha, ukwenza iileyibhile nogcino lwempahla yofuzo, ilawulwa nokongamelwa ngumntu owanelisa iimfuno ezimiselweyo isiza sisanelisa ezinye iimfuno ezingamiselwa.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Izicelo ezingazaliswanga ngokupheleleyo ziya kuphindiswa kumenzi wesicelo yaye akukho xanduva luya kwamkelwa malunga nakuphi na ukuphazamiseka okunokwenzeka.
Intlawulo yesicelo ingahlawulwa kwi-akhawunti elandelayo yebhanki:

Iinkonzo zabantu bamazwe angaphandle
Ukuya kuhala okanye ukutyelela eMazantsi Afrika
Ukufunda
Isicelo sephepha lemvume yokufunda
Isicelo sephepha lemvume (ipemethe) yokufunda
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Iphepha lemvume (ipemethe) yokufunda yincwadi enika abantu abaphuma kumazwe angaphandle ilungelo lokufunda kulo naliphina iziko lemfundo ephakamileyo eMzantsi Afrika. Afake isicelo ngokwakhe kwiNdlu yoZakuzo yaseMzantsi Afrika okanye kwiZiko eliMele uMzantsi Afrika.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Aveze:
o incwadi egunyazisiweyo okanye ubungqina bokubhaliswa obusuka kwiziko lemfundo elibhalisiweyo laseMzantsi Afrika o iinkcukacha malunga nendawo yokuhlala elungisiweyo o ubungqina beemali ezaneleyo zokuhlawula iimali zokufunda, ukulungiswa kunye nezinye iindleko o isatifiketi sokubamsulwa esiphuma emapoliseni ngokuphathelelene namazwe abekade ehlala kuwo kumathuba angaphezulu konyaka. Esi satifiketi kufuneka sithiwe thaca kwisithuba seenyanga ezilishumi elinesibini kwenziwe isicelo ukubangaba asifumaneki kwamsinyane o ikopi yetikiti lomoya eliyiritheni okanye isiqinisekiso sokubuyiselwa ekhaya esiluhlobo lwedipozithi elingana nendleko yetikiti lomoya eliya kwilizwe avela kulo okanye ahlala kulo, ukuba kuyimfuneko o incwadi kagqirha engqina ukuba umenzi-sicelo usempilweni entle.
Abenzi-zicelo abanakungena eMzantsi Afrika phambi kokuba izicelo zabo zivunywe.
Abenzi-zicelo abanezicelo ezivunyiweyo banikwa i-visa evumela ukuba bangena-ngene kaninzi.
Abantu abasephantsi kwabazali mabathi thaca iinkcukacha zomntu waseMzantsi Afrika oyakubangumntu obamelayo. Ezi nkcukacha mazithiwe thaca nencwadi evumayo, ubungqina obuvela kubazali bobabini bemvume yeli xesha kujongwe ukuba lihlalwe, okanye obuvela kumzali onguye yedwa ogcina umntwana ndawonye nobungqina bokugcinwa ngumzali omnye.
Entla
Entla

Iiveki ezisibhozo.

Ukuya kuhala okanye ukutyelela eMazantsi Afrika
Ukuhlala ixeshana elifutshane
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Ipemethe yemvumelwano (i-treaty permit) yincwadi enika abantu bangaphandle imvume yokungena eMzantsi Afrika ukuze bathabathe inxaxheba kwiinkqubo ekuvunyelwene ngazo nguMzantsi Afrika namazwe waba bantu.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Hambisa ezi ncwadi zilandelayo:
Incwadi ephuma kwiqumrhu okanye kwiziko elibandakanyeka kwesi sivumelwano engqina uhlobo lwenkqubo. Le ncwadi iyakungqina isi sivumelwano ekuyakuqhutyelwa phantsi kwaso le nkqubo, ukuthabatha inxaxheba komenzi-sicelo (umntu welizwe langaphandle) kule nkqubo ixeliweyo kunye nohlobo lwemisebenzi umenzi-sicelo alindeleke ukuba ayenze phantsi kwesi sivumelwano.
Isatifiketi sokugabulwa esiphuma kumapolisa kuwo onke amazwe umenzi-sicelo nomlingane wakhe abake bahlala kuwo ukusukela kwiminyaka yobudala eli 18 kunye nezabo bonke abantwana abaxhomekeke kuye abaneminyaka yobudala eli 18 okanye nangaphezulu abayakubanaye ngelixa eseMzantsi Afrika.
o o Isithembiso esibhaliweyo esivela kumqashi, apho amkela uxanduva lweendleko ezayamene nokufuduswa komenzi-sicelo kunye nabo baxhomekeke kuye ukuba kuyimfuneko. Ukubangaba umqashi lisebe likarhulumente kwaye akanako ukuthi thaca esi sithembiso sibhaliweyo sixeliweyo, ilizwe elithumelayo lingathi thaca eso sithembiso egameni lalo mqashi.
o o Iincwadi eziphathelelene nobume bomtshato, ingxelo ebhaliweyo nefungelweyo yobulingane okanye abantwana abasaxhomekeke kubazali ngokwasemthethweni ukubangaba umenzi-sicelo uyakukhatshwa ngumlingane kunye nabantwana abaxhomekeke kubo.

Khetha ulwimi
Isiqinisekiso sokuhambisa isiselo esinxilisayo esi
Isicelo sokuxuba isiselo esinxilisayo
Isicelo semvume yokuthengisa isiselo esinxilisayo
Shicilela eli phepha/Printa eli phepha
Yongeza kwimiba ethandwayo
Beka njengephepha lokuqala
Nxulumana nathi
Imephu yesiza
Ikhasi lokuqala
Iinkonzo zemibutho
Ukufaka isicelo sesiqinisekiso sokungenisa elizweni isiselo esinxilisayo
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Kufuneka isiqinisekiso sokungenisa elizweni ukuze ukwazi ukungenisa isiselo esinxilisayo (ngaphandle kwebhiya) apha eMzantsi Afrika. Isiqinisekiso sokungenisa elizweni okanye ikopi siya kufuneka phambi kokuba umthwalo ukhululwe kwizibuko lokungena.
Umngenisi elizweni wenza isicelo sesiqinisekiso sokungenisa elizweni kube kanye kubomi bemveliso. Emva koko loo nombolo inye yesiqinisekiso sokungenisa elizweni ingasetyenziswa xa isakhiwo, iziqulatho, ubukhulu bebhotile neleyibhile yemveliso ingaguqukanga.
Isiqinisekiso sokungenisa elizweni asinakufuneka malunga nemveliso engeniswa elizweni equlathe isiselo esinxilisayo esingaphezulu kwesinye ekhulwini ngenjongo yokusela yaye iyinxalenye yomthwalo wobuyena yomntu ofikayo eMzantsi Afrika, ngokuxhomekeke ekubeni iimveliso ezinjalo:
o isambuku sazo asigqithi kumthamo weelitha ezili-12 yaye o injongo yeyokuba isetyenziswe kuphela nguloo mntu, usapho lwakhe neendwendwe zakhe ezingahlawuliyo.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Zalisa ifomu yesicelo.
Thumela isampuli yesiselo esinxilisayo esingeniswe elizweni ngobuninzi ngebhotile eqhelekileyo yama-750 ml.
Malunga nemveliso engeniswa ngobuninzi iziqulatho ziya kuhlolwa. Ileyibhile ihlolwa ukuze kufakwe isicelo semvume yesiqinisekiso sokuthengisa.
Kufuneka iCandelo lifumane imali (eziinkozo) phambi kokuba kukhutshwe isiqinisekiso sokungenisa elizweni.
Isiqinisekiso sokungenisa elizweni siya kukhutshwa xa iziqulatho neleyibhile, kwimo yemveliso engeniswa isebhotileni, yaye kwimeko yemveliso engeniswa ngobuninzi, xa iziqulatho zemveliso zanelisa iimfuno ze-Liquor Products Act, 1989 (umThetho weeMveliso eziNxilisayo). Emva koko umthwalo wemveliso ungangeniswa elizweni.

Entla

Imephu yesiza
Ikhasi lokuqala
Iinkonzo zabantu
Isicelo senkxaso yokunakekela omnye umntu isapoti
Isicelo senkxaso yokunakekela omnye umntu
Inkcazelo
Inkxaso yokunakekela omnye umntu (maintenance) luxanduva lokunika omnye umntu, umzekelo umntwana ongekabinamalungelo okuzithabathela izigqibo ngokwasemthethweni, ukutya, indlu, impahla yokunxiba, imfundo kunye nonakekelo lonyango, okanye ukulungiselela omnye umntu iindlela nezinto eziyimfuneko ukuze anikwe ezi zinto zidingekayo kwimpilo yakhe. Olu xanduva lwasemthethweni lokunika inkxaso lubizwa ngokuba 'luxanduva lokuxhasa okanye 'luxanduva lokusapota'.
Ngubani ekufuneka akhuphe inkxaso yokunakekela omnye umntu (isapoti)?
Uxanduva lokusapota lusekelwe kubudlelwane begazi, ukwamkelwa komntwana abengowomnye umntu okanye abantu ngokusemthethweni okanye kwimeko yokokuba aba bantu batshatile.
Umntwana kufuneka asapotwe okanye axhaswe
Ngabazali bakhe, nokuba batshatile, bayahlalisana, bohlukene okanye baqhawule umtshato (badivosile), kubandakanywa abazali abamkele umntwana wabangowabo ngokusemthethweni; kunye/okanye
Ungabanga isapoti eqiqileyo eyimfuneko ukuze unike umntwana okanye omnye umntu onelungelo lokusapotwa indlela yokuphila nokukhula okufanelekileyo. Oku kubandakanya ukunika izinto ezidingekayo empilweni ezifana nokutya, impahla yokunxiba kunye nendlu, ndawonye nokuhlawuwulela imfundo efanelekileyo. Inkundla ingayalela nokuba utata womntwana enze igalelo kwintlawulo yeendleko zokulungiselelwa komntwana kunye nenkxaso ukusukela kumhla wokuzalwa komntwana ukuyakutsho kumhla wokunikwa komyalelo wesapoti. Inkundla inganika nomyalelo wokuhlawulwa kweendleko zonyango okanye ingayalela ukuba umntwana abhaliswe phantsi kwesikim sonyango somnye wabazali njengomntu oxhomekekileyo. Ukwenzela ukuba inkundla ikwazi ukukhupha umyalelo wesapoti ofanelekileyo, bobabini abazali mabanike inkundla ubungqina beendleko zabo.
Imbono yakho ngokuziphatha komnye umzali ayilichaphazeli ilungelo labantwana bakho lokufumana isapoti. Kukwafuneka uyihlawule isapoti, nokubangaba omnye lo umzali uphinde watshata;
uhambisana (unobudlelwane) nomnye umntu;
Uxanduva lwakho lokuhlawula isapoti kunye nelungelo lakho lokufikelela ebantwaneni bakho yimibandela emibini eyahlukene kakhulu kwaye ayingqamananga tu. Ngaphezu koko, abantwana bakhe nawuphina umzali abaluchaphazeli uxanduva lokusapota. Kodwa ke, nangona kunjalo, imali yesapoti ingalungiswa ukubangaba omnye umbandakanyeki uzisa isicelo esinjalo.
Ukuze ufumane inkcazelo ebanzi, yiya kwiSebe lezoBulungisa noPhuhliso loMgaqo-siseko.
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Yenza isicelo sesapoti kwinkundla kamantyi ekwisithili ohlala kuso.
Igosa lesapoti kunye nomphandi bayakuphanda isibango sakho kwaye bajonge iimeko zakho.
Inkundla iyakukhuphela umphenduli (lo mntu kwenziwa kuye isibango) isamani (incwadi eyalela umntu ukuba aye enkundleni) ukuze aye kuvela enkundleni ngomhla ochaziweyo ukuze kuxoxwe ngalo mbandela.
Umphenduli ke angakhetha ukuba avume ukuhlawula le sapoti ngale ndlela ibangwa ngayo, okanye aye kuphikisana nalo mba enkundleni.
Ukubangaba umphenduli uyavuma ukuhlawula isapoti njengoko ibangwa, umantyi uyakuphonononga imiqulu efanelekileyo. Uyakuthi ke akhuphe umyalelo, kwaye angagqiba ekubeni enze njalo ngaphandle kokufuna ukuba ababandakanyeki bavele enkundleni.
Inkundla ingayalela ukuba imali yesapoti ihlawulwe ngenye yezi ndlela zilandelayo:
Kwi-ofisi kamantyi ekwindawo umntu ahlala kuyo okanye kuyo nayiphina enye i-ofisi karhulumente echongelwe le meko
Kwi-akhawunti yebhanki okanye yequmrhu lokwakha echongwe ngulo mntu ubandakanyekayo
Nqo kulo mntu ufaneleke afumane le mali
Imithetho esetyenziswayo
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Izikhalazo ziyakuphathwa ngokukhawuleza nangobunono kangangoko kunokwenzeka
Akukho xesha libekiweyo kule nkonzo. Inkqubo iyonke, ukusukela ekuhambiseni isicelo ukuya kutsho ekufumaneni intlawulo yakho yokuqala yesapoti, ingathabatha iiveki ezininzi, kuxhomekeke kwintsebenziswano yabo bobabini ababandakanyeki.
Amangqina ahamba inkqubo, kubandakanywa umntu obanga isapoti, bavumelekile bafumane izibonelelo ezimiselweyo zenkxaso nohambo. Kodwa ke, inkundla iyakwenza isigqibo, ngokubona kwayo, malunga nokuba eso sibonelelo siyakuhlawulwa na kumntu onganikwa umyalelo wokuba ahlawule isapoti.
Umntu obanga isapoti makenze isicelo kwigosa lesapoti ukuze ahlawulwe iimali zamangqina.
Iindleko
Le nkonzo ayihlawulelwa.

Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Le nkonzo isebenziseka kumntu ovunyiweyo njengembacu eMzantsi Afrika. Izicelo zingenziwa kwi-ofisi ekufuphi yezeKhaya kwiphondo ohlala kulo. Kufuneka ube ubunobume obuqhubekayo bobumbacu iminyaka emihlanu ukuze wenze isicelo.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Fumana uqinisekiso kwiKomiti eMiyo yeMibandela yeeMbacu oluchaza ukuba ngahle uhlale uyimbacu okokoko.
Hambisa incwadi ebhaliweyo nefungelweyo (i-affidavit) malunga nawo onke amagama asetyenziswa nguwe.
