Isicelo samalungelo okumilisa izityalo
Isicelo samalungelo okumilisa izityalo
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Umbhalisi wamaLungelo abaMilisi beziTyalo unokuthatha uhlobo oluthile njengohlobo olutsha aze anikele ngamalungelo abamilisi bezityalo xa:
Izixhobo zokumilisa olo hlobo zingekathengiswa apha eMzantsi Afrika kwithuba elingaphaya konyaka.
Kwimeko yohlobo lomthi okanye umdiliya, apho izixhobo zokumilisa zingekafumaneki kwelinye ilizwe, kwezoshishino okanye kuluntu kwithuba elingaphaya kweminyaka emithandathu, okanye kwimeko yesityalo nasiphi na esinye, kwithuba elingaphaya kweminyaka emine.
o kufuneka sahluke ngokucacileyo kuhlobo naluphi na olunye lomnombo ofanayo o kufuneka sifane, kukuthi, zonke izityalo kulimo kufuneka zikhangeleke zifana yaye zibe neempawu ezifanayo o kufuneka sizinze, kukuthi, kufuneka izityalo zohlobo oluthile, emva kokulinywa amatyeli aliqela, zisoloko zikhangeleka zifana nezityalo zentsusa o kufuneka sibe negama elamkelekileyo.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Xa uhlobo lwesityalo lungabonakali kuluhlu, thumela isicelo ngokuphathelele kupapasho kwakunye nenkxaso ebhaliweyo kuMbhalisi wamLungelo abaMilisi beziTyalo.
Ukuba uhlobo lwesityalo lukhona kuluhlu, kufuneka kuthunyelwe izinto ezilandelayo:
o intlawulo emiselweyo yesicelo novavanyo o imbewu okanye izixhobo zokumilisa o ugunyaziso olubhaliweyo oluvela kumnini-sityalo, ukuba awusimilisanga, wasikhetha okanye waqhubela phambili udidi.
Bonakalisa ngendlela ecacileyo kuthotho lwemibuzo ukuba udidi olutsha kufuneka luthelekiswa neziphi ezinye iindidi ezaziwayo ukumisela ukuzibalula.
Ungenza isicelo sokhuselo lwethutyana lodidi. Oku kuxela ukuthi udidi lukhuselwe ngethuba lovavanyo. Kufuneka unikezele ngokuzibophelela okubhaliweyo ukuthi ungathengisi (ngaphandle kwenjongo yokumilisa okanye uvavanyo) nayiphi na into yokumilisa yodidi okujoliswe kulo kude kube zonke iimvavanyo zigqityiwe yaye kunikelwe ngamalungelo abamilisi. Luyakhuthazwa ukhuselo lwethutyana ngokuphathelele kwizityalo apho iimvavanyo zithatha ixesha elingaphaya konyaka ukuze zigqitywe.
Kukho iintsuku ezimiselweyo ekufuneka kuthunyelwe ngazo amaxwebhu nezixhobo zokumilisa kuMbhalisi. Iinkcukacha zezi ntsuku, inani lezixhobo zokumilisa ekufuneka zithunyelwe nalapho kufuneka zithunyelwe khona, ziyafumaneka kuMbhalisi.
Xa uluhlu lodidi lukhona ngokuphathelele kolo hlobo olwenzelwa isicelo samalungelo abamilisi bezityalo, thumela izicelo ngaxeshanye ukulondoloza ixesha nemali.
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Inkqubo yokuhlola amalungelo abamilisi bezityalo ithatha ithuba lolimo elinye ubuncinane.

Isicelo semvume yelungelo lokumilisa izityalo: R1 300 inye
Intlawulo yovavanyo lwelungelo lokumilisa izityalo zeHlelo A (ezolimo, imifuno, izityalo zamadlelo nezihombiso zaminyaka le): R2 200 inye
Intlawulo yovavanyo lwelungelo lokumilisa izityalo zeHlelo B (iziqhamo, imidiliya, ezesitrasi nezihombiso zaminyaka le): R3 000 inye
Intlawulo yovavanyo lwelungelo lokumilisa izityalo zeHlelo B (umbona omhlophe nobomvu): R2 600 inye
Impikiso yemvume yelungelo lokumilisa izityalo: R4 500 inye
Intlawulo yonyaka nonyaka yemvume yelungelo lokumilisa izityalo: R250 inye
Isicelo sokukhutshwa kwelayisensi ebophelelayo malunga nelungelo lommilisi wezityalo: R3 600 inye
Isicelo sokuguqula okanye ukufakelela kwigama elamkelweyo ngokuphathelele kudidi: R1 500 inye
Impikiso echasene nokwamkelwa okucetywayo kokuguqula okanye ukufakelela kwigama elamkelweyo ngokuphathelele kudidi: R650 inye
Isaziso sokurhoxisa ngokuzithandela ilungelo lommilisi wezityalo: Simahla

Iinkonzo zemibutho
Isicelo sokubhalisa ukutya kwasefama
Isicelo sokubhalisa ukutya kwasefama okanye ukutya kwezilwanyana zobuhlobo
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Inkampani ya phesheya ayifanelanga ukwenza isicelo sokungenisa elizweni apha eMzantsi Afrika. Isicelo sokubhalisa ukutya kwasefama nezichumisi singenziwa kuphela yinkampani yasekhaya ebhalisiweyo, ummi waseMzantsi Afrika okanye umbutho osemthethweni obhalisiweyo apha eMzantsi Afrika.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Isicelo sokubhalisa ukutya kwasefama siqulethe:
Incwadi echazayo evela kumnini wobhaliso okanye ummeli otyunjiweyo. Ileta echazayo kufuneka iquke:
o igama lemveliso o inombolo yobhaliso xa imveliso sele ibhalisiwe o isizathu sokuthumela isicelo (ukuthi sisicelo esitsha, isicelo sokulungisa, isicelo sokubhalisa imveliso ezalwa lubhaliso olukhoyo)
o iileta zesivumelwano xa kufuneka imvume yominini wobhaliso (imvume yokubhalisa imveliso ezalwa lubhaliso olukhoyo okanye imvume yokusebenzisa igama lemveliso yenye inkampani kwileyibhile)
Thumela iifomu (iikopi ezimbini) zesicelo zezicelo ezintsha nezilungiso kubhaliso olukhoyo, kuquka neenguqu zokwakheka.
Zalisa ngokupheleleyo, ngaphandle kokubhekisa kwizicelo zexesha elidlulileyo, iinombolo zamaphepha okanye ezinye iimveliso (okungenani ikopi enye yeefomu zesicelo kufuneka ibe nentsayino yentsusa. Enye inokuba yikopi).
Iifomu zesicelo kufuneka zisayinwe ngumntu otyunjiweyo ngokusemthethweni yaye lona kunqweneleka kube ngumntu wenkampani onoqhagamshelwano noMbhalisi.
Igama nenombolo yobhaliso yemveliso kufuneka lisetyenziswe njengoko kuchaziwe kwisiqinisekiso sobhaliso. Nayiphi na inguqu egameni, nokuba incinci kangakanani, iya kuthathwa njengesilungiso.
o thumela iikopi ezimbini o nikela ngesiNgesi nesiBhulu. Akukho mfuneko yokuba iileyibhile zishicilelwe ngeelwimi ezimbini o kufuneka ibhalwe ngendlela ecacileyo nefundekayo, ngendlela echanekileyo o ungabhali iinombolo kwizilumkiso neziqapheliso o onke amanqaku akwileyibhile kufuneka ahambelane ngako konke nalawo akwifomu yesicelo.
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Kungathatha iinyanga ezintathu kuya kwezine ukuba ukutya kwasefama nokutya kwezilwanyana zobuhlobo kubhaliswe.

Iinkonzo zemibutho
Isicelo sesikhokelo serhafu intlawulo yomvuzo womq
Isicelo sesikhokelo serhafu: intlawulo yomvuzo womqondisi
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
UMthetho weRhafu yeNgeniso-mali, wango 1962 (Income Tax Act, 1962), ulungiselela iimeko apho kungenziwa khona isicelo sesikhokelo serhafu.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Xa usenza isicelo sesikhokelo serhafu, qinisekisa ukuba imibandela yakho yerhafu ime kakuhle. I-SARS ayidli ngokusikhupha isikhokelo serhafu ukubangaba kukho iincwadi zokubuyisa zerhafu ongekazifaki okanye unemali ongekayihlawuli yerhafu.
Kufuneka kufakwe kwifom yesicelo le nkcazelo isisiseko ilandelayo:
Intlawulo yomvuzo egqityelwe ukufunyanwa kubandakanywa izibonelelo ezisecaleni, umzekelo i50% yesibonelelo sohambo kodwa ingabandakanyi izixa zezambuku kunye neengeniso ezenziwe ngabaqondisi okanye abaqeshwa ngokuphathelelene namalungelo okufumana izibambiso ezithengisekayo.
Unyaka wovavanyo ekufunyenwe ngawo intlawulo yomvuzo.
Inani leenyanga ezigqityiweyo ekwagqityelwa ngazo ukufunyanwa intlawulo eyaziwayo yomvuzo.
Intlawulo yomvuzo eqikelelwayo okanye eyiyo nqo kunyaka omiyo. (le nkcazelo mayinikwe xa isizathu somyalelo iyinzima).
Isicelo masiqulathe izizathu zesikhokelo. Xhasa ezi zizathu ngeencwadi ezibandakanyekayo, umzekelo, iingxelo zemali zethutyana kunye nemizuzu yeentlanganiso ezibanjwe ngabaqondisi, ebonisa ukuba iintlawulo zemivuzo eyakuhlawulwa abaqondisi iyakubangaphantsi kwaleyo yonyaka wovavanyo ophelileyo.
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Akukho xesha elisisigxina.
Entla
Iindleko
Le nkonzo ayihlawulelwa.

Entla

Iindleko
Inkcazelo
UMthetho weRhafu yeNgeniso-mali, wango 1962 (Income Tax Act, 1962), ulungiselela iimeko apho kungenziwa khona isicelo sesikhokelo serhafu.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Xa usenza isicelo sesikhokelo serhafu, qinisekisa ukuba imibandela yakho yerhafu ime kakuhle. I-SARS ayidli ngokusikhupha isikhokelo serhafu ukubangaba kukho iincwadi zokubuyisa zerhafu ongekazifaki okanye unemali ongekayihlawuli yerhafu.
Kufuneka kufakwe kwifom yesicelo le nkcazelo isisiseko ilandelayo:
Intlawulo yomvuzo egqityelwe ukufunyanwa kubandakanywa izibonelelo ezisecaleni, umzekelo i50% yesibonelelo sohambo kodwa ingabandakanyi izixa zezambuku kunye neengeniso ezenziwe ngabaqondisi okanye abaqeshwa ngokuphathelelene namalungelo okufumana izibambiso ezithengisekayo.
Unyaka wovavanyo ekufunyenwe ngawo intlawulo yomvuzo.
Inani leenyanga ezigqityiweyo ekwagqityelwa ngazo ukufunyanwa intlawulo eyaziwayo yomvuzo.
Intlawulo yomvuzo eqikelelwayo okanye eyiyo nqo kunyaka omiyo. (le nkcazelo mayinikwe xa isizathu somyalelo iyinzima).
Isicelo masiqulathe izizathu zesikhokelo. Xhasa ezi zizathu ngeencwadi ezibandakanyekayo, umzekelo, iingxelo zemali zethutyana kunye nemizuzu yeentlanganiso ezibanjwe ngabaqondisi, ebonisa ukuba iintlawulo zemivuzo eyakuhlawulwa abaqondisi iyakubangaphantsi kwaleyo yonyaka wovavanyo ophelileyo.

Isicelo somyalelo werhafu - imali esisigxina

Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo

Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Qinisekisa ukuba imibandela yakho yerhafu ime kakuhle phambi kokuba wenze isicelo somyalelo werhafu. I-SARS ayidli ngokuwukhupha umyalelo werhafu ukubangaba kukho iincwadi zokubuyisa zerhafu ongekazifaki okanye unemali ongekayihlawuli yerhafu.
Khupha ezi zinto zilandelayo ukuze uncedise i-SARS ekuvumeni isicelo sakho somyalelo werhafu:
Sakuba sivunyiwe isicelo yi-SARS, uyakunikwa ubungqina bokuvunywa kwiintsukwana ezimbalwa, kodwa wona umyalelo werhafu ogunyazisiweyo ungathatha ixesha elinokuya kuthi ga kwiiveki ezine.

Entla

Lingaya kutsho kwiiveki ezine.

Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Esi sikhokelo sithunyelwa xa kwenziwe isicelo sokuba umvuzo womrhafi uxhuzulelwe irhafu ngepesenti esisigxina. Umqashi nguye ekufuneka athumele esi sicelo egameni lomqeshwa.
Izikhokelo azitshintsheleki, kwaye xa umqeshwa ethe watshintsha imo yakhe yengqesho, kufuneka kwenziwe isicelo esitsha. Ukubangaba usebenzela abaqashi abaninzi, yenza izicelo zezikhokelo ezohlukeneyo ngokomqashi ngamnye.
Kufuneka iikopi zeencwadi zengqesho, izivumelwano ezizikhontrakthi zenkonzo kunye neminye imiqulu ebandakanyekayo, ukuze kungqinisiswe iimeko nemigaqo yengqesho.
Isikhokelo sokuxhuzula irhafu ngepesenti esisigxina siyakukhutshelwa ixesha elithi ga kwiinyanga ezili 12, kwaye kufuneka sivuselelwe emva koko.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Qinisekisa ukuba imibandela yakho yerhafu ime kakuhle phambi kokuba wenze isicelo sesikhokelo serhafu. I-SARS ayidli ngokusikhupha isikhokelo serhafu ukubangaba kukho iincwadi zokubuyisa zerhafu ongekazibuyisi okanye kukho iintlawulo ongekazenzi.
Faka ezi zinto zilandelayo kwisicelo sakho sesikhokelo serhafu:
Faka le miqulu ilandelayo kwisicelo sakho:
o ikopi yesivumelwano esiyikhontrakthi yenkonzo (apho kuboniswa khona iinkcukacha zokunikwa kwenkonzo kunye nemigaqo)
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Sakube sivunyiwe isicelo yi-SARS, kuyakuthunyelwa ubungqina kwisithuba seentsuku ezimbalwa. Kodwa ke, sona isikhokelo esigunyazisiweyo serhafu singathabatha ukuyakutsho kwiiveki ezine.

Inkcazelo
NgokoMthetho wokuLawulwa koRhwebo lwaMazwe eHlabathi (International Trade Administration Act, Act 71 of 2002), uMphathiswa wezoRhwebo naMashishini, naninina xa ebona ukuba kuyimfuneko okanye kuluncedo kwiminqweno neemfuno zoluntu, angamisela ngesaziso kwiGazethi kaRhulumente, ukuba kungabikho zimpahla nezinto zodidi okanye zohlobo olungqalileyo ezingangeniswa eMzantsi Afrika; okanye ezingangeniswa eMzantsi Afrika ngaphandle kwaphantsi kwegunya lepemethe kunye nangokuhambisana nemiqathango exelwe kwipemethe ekhutshwe nguye okanye ngumntu ogunyaziswe nguye.
Izicelo zeepemethe zokungeniswa kwempahla nezinto, eziphantsi kwamanyathelo olawulo lokungeniswa kwempahla nezinto elizweni, kufuneka zenziwe kwifom emiselwe oku.

Udidi lwelungelo lokuloba:
Inkqubo yokusingathwa kwesicelo ingathatha inyanga enye ukuya kwezi-3 okanye ngaphezulu ngokuxhomekeke kumthamo wezicelo kunye/okanye ngexesha lonyaka lecandelo lokuloba (fishing sector season).
Inkqubo yokusingathwa kwesicelo ingathatha inyanga enye ukuya kwezi-3 okanye ngaphezulu ngokuxhomekeke kumthamo wezicelo kunye/okanye ngexesha lonyaka lecandelo lokuloba (fishing sector season).

Iindleko
Udidi lwelungelo lokuloba
Ukubamba (ukusebenzisa/ukuvuna ) iintlanzi
Njengoko imiselwe nguMphathiswa okanye umntu onegunya lokwenza oko ngokwecandelo lokuloba nesimemo esikhutshwe kwigazethi karhulumente sokucela ilungelo lokuloba
Ukuloba i-line fish (yemveli) ngabalobi abangekho ngaphezu kwabane
Ukubamba (ukusebenzisa/ukuvuna) iintlanzi, kuquka nengca yolwandle (seaweed)

Inkcazelo
IiPemithi zokungenisa iintlanzi zamazwe angaphandle ngenjongo yolonwabo ezikhutshelwa ukulungiselela ukusetyenziswa ngabantu okanye ukutyiwa ziya kuba semthethweni kangangethuba lolo hambo lokuya nokubuya kwilizwe ekuyiwa kulo.

Isicelo sepemethe yokuthumela impahla nezinto kuma
Ukuthumela iintlanzi kumazwi angaphandle
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Ukulobela ukurhweba Commercial fishing kukwenza umsebenzi onxulumene nokuloba ofana nokuthumela iintlanzi zolwandle kumazwe angaphandle ngenjongo yokuzithengisa. Ukuze uthumele iintlanzi zolwandle marine fish kumazwe angaphandle okanye ngaphandle kwemida yeRiphabliki yoMzantsi Afrika, kufuneka wenze isicelo sepemithi yokuthumela kumazwe angaphandle nesivunywa nguMphathiswa weSebe leMicimbi yokusiNgqongileyo noKhenketho Minister of Environmental Affairs and Tourism okanye omnye umntu onegunya lokwenza oko. Akukho mntu uya kuthumela iintlanzi zolwandle kumazwe angaphandle ngaphandle kwepemithi. Xa ipemithi yokuthumela kumazwe angaphandle ebikho iphelelelwe emva kweenyanga ezintathu, kufuneka wenze isicelo sepemithi entsha. Ukungaphumeleli ukubambelela kwimiqathango yepemithi kunganeziphumo zokunqunyanyiswa okanye ukurhoxiswa kwepemithi.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Yenza isicelo sepemithi yokuthumela iintlanzi kumazwe angaphandle.
Nikezela ngale ngcaciso ilandelayo:
o ubungakanani beentlobo eziza kuthunyelwa kumazwe angaphandle o kwimeko yaxa kukho i-arhente ebandakanyekayo, kufuneka kuqhotyoshelwe isivumelwano phakathi kwamaqela achaphazelekayo amabini kunye neekopi zezazisi zabo banelungelo lokusayina (ID copies of signatories)
Intlawulo yokwenza isicelo eyi- R225 (equka konke) iyafuneka.
Izicelo zentsusa mazithunyelwe ngeposi, ukuze ingakhutshwa ipemithi xa ungakwenzanga oko.
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Inkqubo yokwenza isicelo ingathatha iintsuku ezisi-7 kwezomsebenzi okanye ngaphezulu ngokuxhomekeke ekufakweni kwesicelo ngokufanelekileyo.

Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Ukungenisa iintlanzi zamazwe angaphandle ngenjongo yokurhweba kuthetha ukuba wenza imisebenzi efana nokungenisa iintlanzi zolwandle zamazwe angaphandle ngenjongo yokurhweba ngazo. Ukuze ungenise iintlanzi zolwandle zamazwe angaphandle (marine fish), kufuneka wenze isicelo sepemithi yokungenisa iintlanzi zamazwe angaphandle nesivunywa nguMphathiswa weMicimbi yokusiNgqongileyo noKhenketho (Minister of Environmental Affairs and Tourism) okanye umntu onegunya lokwenza oko (delegated authority). Akukho mntu uya kurhweba angenise iintlanzi zolwandle zamazwe angaphandle ngaphandle kwepemithi. Yenza isicelo sepemithi entsha yokungenisa iintlanzi zolwandle zamazwe angaphandle xa leyo ubunayo iphelelwe lixesha. Ukungaphumeleli ukubambelela kwimiqathango yepemithi kunganeziphumo zokunqunyanyiswa okanye ukurhoxiswa kwayo.
Akukho nonkala uhleliyo welizwe langaphandle unokungeniswa kweli lizwe.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Funda ifom yokwenza isicelo ngononophelo uze uqinisekise ukuba uyazanelisa iimfuneko nemiqathango.
Nikezela ngale ngcaciso ilandelayo:
o ubungakanani beentlobo eziza kungeniswa zamazwe angaphandle.
Ngenisa isicelo sakho kunye nala maxwebhu alandelayo:
Iifom eziyintsusa mazithunyelwe ngeposi, kwaye ukungakwenzi oko, kuya kubangela ukuba ipemithi ingakhutshwa.

Entla

Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Isilwanyana singavunyelwa ukuba ngumnikeli wempahla yofuzo xa ugqirha wezilwanyana engqina ukuba isilwanyana esinjalo samkelekile ngokuphathelele:
kwimo yempilo ngokubanzi ukungabinazo izifo kudidi lwencindi yobudoda (isidoda)
kwiimpawu ezinye ezinokumiselwa.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Khupha ifomu yesicelo kwi-inthanethi uze uzalise ifomu yesicelo ngokwahlukanisa oonombumba usebenzisa oonobumba abakhulu. Ifomu kananjalo ingacelwa kuMbhalisi wokuPhucula iziLwanyana.
Isicelo kufuneka senziwe ngegama leziko elibhalisiweyo apho isilwanyana siya kugcinwa khona.
Kufuneka isicelo sithunyelwe kumbutho ofanelekileyo wabazalisi.
Amaxwebhu alandelayo kufuneka akhaphe isicelo:
DNA/ isiqinisekiso sohlobo lwegazi o iirekhodi zokusebenza kwesilwanyana o intlawulo emiselweyo yesicelo.
Isicelo kufuneka siqinisekiswe ngugqirha wezilwanyana wangasese size singqinwe ngugqirha wezilwanyana osemthethweni.
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Xa umbhalisi engavumi ukwamkela isicelo, umenzi wesicelo uya kwaziswa ngeleta malunga nesigqibo nezizathu ekusekelwe phezu kwazo.
Xa umbhalisi esamkela isicelo malunga nemvume yesilwanyana esichaphazelekayo esifana nesilwanyana esingumnikeli, kuya kukhutshwa isiqinisekiso semvume.

Iinkonzo zemibutho
Inkcazelo
I-learnership (inkqubo yokufunda nokuqeqeshela umsebenzi) yindlela eyenye yokuqeqesha egxininisa kumava okwenza umsebenzi.
Ii-Learnerships zibandakanya ukufunda kwigumbi lokufundela, kwiziko loqeqesho okanye kwikholeji, kunye nokuqeqeshelwa emsebenzini nqo kwindawo yokusebenza.
Ukuze ufumane inkcazelo ebanzi, yiya kwiSebe leZabasebenzi.
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Khangela umntu kwinkampani okanye kwiziko lakho akhokele abafundi kwaye abancede ngengxaki abangajongana nazo mhlawumbi kule nkampani yakho.
Khangela umntu wokuncedisa umfundi ngenxenye yezifundo zengqondo ze-learnership ngokukhetha umniki-nkonzo zoqeqesho. Lo mniki-nkonzo zoqeqesho kufuneka abe unikwe uqinisekiso lokuvunywa nokwamkelwa yi-SETA.
Abaqeshi bangakhetha abafundi kwalapha kubasebenzi babo okanye bangakhetha abantu abangaphangeliyo bangenele i-learnership. Ukubangaba abaqeshi bafuna abantu abangaphangeliyo kwii-learnerships, banganxulumana neziko lezabasebenzi elikufuphi kubo ukuze bafumane uluhlu lwamagama akhoyo abantu abangaphangeliyo. Akunyanzelekanga ukuba abaqeshi babaqeshe aba bafundi bangaphangeliyo emva kwee-learnership.
Abaqeshi, abaniki-nkonzo zoqeqesho kunye nabafundi kufuneka basayine isivumelwano se-learnership.
Akuba egqityiwe wonke la manyathelo, abaqeshi bangayiqhuba i-learnership.
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo

Inkcazelo
I-visa luphawu olugunyazisiweyo olubekwa kwipaspoti esebenzisekayo yomntu welizwe langaphandle, olunika loo mntu welizwe langaphandle igunya lokungena eMzantsi Afrika.
ifunyanwe phambi kokuba umenzi-sicelo alishiye ilizwe lakhe endulukela eMzantsi Afrika ifunyanwe kwilizwe langaphandle, kwaye akunakwenziwa isicelo sayo kumasango okungena aseMzantsi Afrika kwenziwe isicelo sayo kwelo lizwe, kwindlu yozakuzo yaseMzantsi Afrika okanye kwiziko elimele uMzantsi Afrika, kumazwe apho uMzantsi Afrika umelweyo kuwo kwenziwe isicelo sayo kwindlu yozakuzo yaseMzantsi Afrika ekufuphi okanye kwiziko elimele uMzantsi Afrika elikufuphi, ukubangaba uMzantsi Afrika awumelwanga elizweni lakho. Oku kuyabandakanyeka nakubantu abaneepaspoti zozakuzelwano lwamazwe nezigunyazisiweyo abafuna iipemethe zozakuzelwano phakathi kwamazwe.

Iinkonzo zemibutho
Yenza isicelo sepemethe okanye selayisensi ukuthutha okanye ukuphatha ukutya
Isicelo sesatifiketi sokwamkeleka ekubeni uthuthe okanye uphathe ukutya
Inkcazelo
Nawuphi na umntu onqwenela ukubanendawo yokutya okanye ukuthutha ukutya kufanele abenesatifiketi sokwamkeleka. Esi satifiketi sikhutshwa emva kokuba abahloli abaphuma koogunyaziwe bendawo beyihlolile le ndawo okanye esi sithuthi.
Ukuze ufumane inkcazelo ebanzi, yiya kwiSebe lezeMpilo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Yenza isicelo semvume okanye sesatifiketi sokuthutha okanye sokuphatha ukutya kugunyaziwe wendawo ohlala kuyo.
Lungisa indawo efanelekileyo esetyenziselwa kuphela ukuphatha ukutya okanye isithuthi esisetyenziselwa kuphela ukuthutha ukutya.
Gcina isithuthi okanye indawo icocekile ngamaxesha onke, ukuze uqinisekise ukuba ukutya okuthuthwayo okanye okuphathwayo akungcoliswa ziimpukane, ukungcola, ubunyhukunyhuku, ubumdaka okanye nayiphi na enye into engcolisayo.
Isithuthi okanye indawo iya kuhlolwa ngabahloli abaphuma kugunyaziwe wendawo ohlala kuyo ukuze ivumeleke ukuba ithuthe okanye iphathe ukutya.
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Umgangatho ofikelelwayo uxhomekeka kubahloli abaphuma kugunyaziwe wendawo ohlala kuyo.
Iindleko
Le nkonzo ayihlawulelwa, kodwa oogunyaziwe bendawo ohlala kuyo bangabiza intlawulo ethile.

Yenza isicelo sepemethe okanye selayisensi
Ukuphathwa nokuthuthwa kobisi
Isicelo sesatifiketi sokwamkeleka kokuphathwa nokuthuthwa kobisi
Inkcazelo
Iishedi ekusengelwa kuzo ziindawo ezisetyenziselwa ukukhutshwa nokuphathwa kobisi ngokucocekileyo nangokunempilo. Isicelo sesatifiketi sokwamkeleka kweshedi yokusengela kufuneka sifakwe ngencwadi ebhaliweyo. Esi sicelo kufuneka sibandakanye inkcazelo exelwe apha ngezantsi.
Ukuze ufumane inkcazelo ebanzi, yiya kwiSebe lezeMpilo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Thumela isicelo esibhaliweyo kugunyaziwe wendawo kummandla apho ikhoyo okanye izakwakhiwa khona ishedi yokusengela.
Nika le nkcazelo ilandelayo:
Igama lakho (lomenzi-sicelo), idilesi kunye nenombolo yomnxeba
Inkcazo yegama lendawo
Isicwangciso sesiza ekuboniswe kuso umntla, ndawonye nazo zonke izakhiwo ezisecaleni nezikumda wale ndawo, kunye nento ezisetyenziselwa yona.
Umzobo obonisa uyilo lwale ndawo ngokweqondo lokulinganisa le 1:100 kuwo wonke amaziko eshedi yokusengela, abandakanya isicwangciso somgangatho, imbonakaliso ngokwamacandelo kunye nokunyuka okuthe nkqo.
Zilungiselele ukunika nayiphi na inkcazelo engacelwa ngugunyaziwe wendawo.
Umhloli ophuma kugunyaziwe wendawo uhlola le ndawo ineshedi ngokupheleleyo. Umhloli uthumela ingxelo kunye nesiphakamiso kugunyaziwe wendawo.
Kukhutshwa isatifiketi sokwamkeleka ukubangaba ingxelo yomhloli ithetha kakuhle ngale shedi.
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Le nkonzo ayihlawulelwa.
Isicelo sesatifiketi sokwamkeleka kweshedi yokusengela. Elifom lifumaneka kugunyaziwe wendawo okanye kwiSebe lezeMpilo.

Ubudlelwane bezabasebenzi
Inkcazelo
Naliphi na ibhunga leengxoxo nezigqibo ezihlanganelweyo okanye i-arhente yabucala lingenza isicelo kwiqumrhu elilawulayo sokunikwa uqinisekiso lokuvunywa nokwamkelwa (accreditation) ukuze :
Lisombulule iimpikiswano ngoxolelwaniso; kwaye
Iqumrhu elilawulayo lingadinga inkcazelo eyongezelelweyo yokuxhasa isicelo, kwaye, ngokwaloo njongo, lingafuna ukuba umenzi-sicelo aye kwintlanganiso okanye kwiintlanganiso ezithile zequmrhu elilawulayo.
Ukuze ufumane inkcazelo ebanzi, yiya kwiSebe leZabasebenzi..
Inkqubo emayilandelwe

Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Umngenisi elizweni uswela isiqinisekiso sokuhambisa iimveliso zeziselo ezinxilisayo ezisezibhotileni ukusuka ezibukweni lokungena ukuza kuthengiswa apha eMzantsi Afrika. Umngenisi wezinto elizweni uswela isiqinisekiso ngokubhekiselele kumnthwalo ngamnye.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Khulula umthwalo wesiselo esinxilisayo ezibukweni lokungena xeshikweni umhloli weSebe lezoLimo ekhangele.
Nika umhloli isicelo sesiqinisekiso sokuhambisa.
Zalisa ifomu yesicelo ehlukileyo malunga nemveliso nganye ehlukileyo ngokweziqulatho, isakhiwo, ileyibhile, igama loshishino okanye ubukhulu bebhotile kwiimveliso ezinye zeziselo ezinxilisayo ezisemthwalweni.
Isicelo kufuneka sikhatshwe zizinto ezilandelayo:
o iziqinisekiso zentsusa, zobudala beminyaka, isakhiwo nohlobo ezikhutshwe ngumbutho osemthethweni welizwe lentsusa.

Ukusebenza eMzantsi Afrika
INgqesho
Isicelo sepemethe yokusebenza enqanaweni (elwandle)
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Ipemethe yokusebenza enqanaweni inikwa umntu welizwe langaphandle ongomnye wabasebenzi basenqanaweni. Ipemethe yokusebenza enqanaweni ikhutshelwa ithuba elingagqithiyo kwiinyanga ezintathu ngexesha. Izicelo zingenziwa kwisango lokungena eMzantsi Afrika.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Veza incwadi yesicelo esuka kumnikazi wenqanawa, kwaye ibandakanye isibhengezo sesithembiso sokuthabatha uxanduva lokuhambisana kwaloo mntu noMthetho wokuNgena eLizweni (Immigration Act, 2002).
Hambisa ubungqina bokubanako ngokwaneleyo komnikazi wenqanawa ngokuphathelelene nemali yokujongana neemfuno zemihla ngemihla kunye neendleko zonyango.
Hlawula idipozithi ukubangaba oko kubonwe kuyimfuneko liSebe lezeKhaya, ukuze uqinisekise ukuhambisana neemeko nemiqathango yepemethe yokusebenza enqanaweni. Loo dipozithi iyakubuyiselwa kuwe emva kokuba umke umphelo okanye emva kokuba unikwe ipemethe. Intlawulo yedipozithi ingenziwa ngetshekhi eqinisekiswe yibhanki okanye ngekhadi lemboleko yekhredithi kwindawo eneziko elilungiselelwe loo ndlela yokuhlawula.
Hambisa ubungqina bentlawulo ebingekakhutshwa yayo nayiphina intlawuliso yesohlwayo (ifayini) esiwiselwe isithuthi.
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Izicelo zithabatha ixesha elingagqithanga kwiintsuku ezingama 30.

Xa kuphela iminyaka emine imoto ingena phepha-mvume, amagosa endlela akhupha isitifiketi sokuyicima lo moto endleleni.

o incwadi yesaziso eqinisekisiweyo o ikopi eqinisekisiweyo yobunini moto o isitifiketi sobhaliso semoto.

Isicelo sokucima ubhaliso okanye sokuphelisa iqumr
Isicelo sokucima ubhaliso okanye sokuphelisa iqumrhu elingavulelekanga
Inkcazelo
I-CC ingayeka ukusebenza kwaye inqwenele ukucinywa kubhaliso, okanye ingapheliswa. Ezi meko zinganzima kwaye zibenobuchwepheshe, kwaye uMphathi woBhaliso lweeNkampani kufanele anikwe inkcazelo yobuchule.
alinako ukuhlawula amatyala ayo;
liyekile ukusebenza (kudla ngokuba ngenxa yeengxaki zemali); okanye amalungu anqwenela ukuzobela impah la nezinto ze-CC.
Ukucinywa kobhaliso kuthetha ukuba i-CC isusiwe kuvimba wokubhalisa nokugcina inkcazelo ngeenkampani kwaye i-CC ayisekho. Ishishini lingaqhuba ngenye indlela eyahlukileyo, umzekelo, njengeshishini eliqhutywa ngumntu omnye, emva kokuba ukucinywa kobhaliso kugqityiwe.
Isitetimenti esibhalwe nguye nawuphina umntu onomnqweno (umzekelo, i-SARS, umbolekisi i-CC enetyala kuye, umphathi wobhaliso okanye ilungu) kufanele isiwe kuMphathi woBhaliso lweeNkampani.
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Hambisa iikopi eziqinisekisiweyo zeencwadi zezazisi zamalungu e-CC.
Ixesha elithatyyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Kungathabatha phakathi kosuku olunye neentsuku ezimbini ukuze kugqitywe inkqubo yokucima ubhaliso.

Inkcazelo
Iphepha-mvume lokuqhuba linika umntu igunya lokuqhuba imoto. Eli phepha-mvume liqulethe: Inkcukacha ezixela ukba umqhubi ukulungele ukuhamba endleleni. Kufuneka ukuba ube neminyaka elishumi elinesibhozo nangaphezulu ukze ukwazi ukwenza esi sicelo.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
o iphepha-mvume lokufunda ukuqhuba o incwadi yesaziso sakho okanye incwadi yokundwendwela o ifoto ezine ezimnyama namhlophe.
Uvavanyo lwamehlo luzakwenziwa ngaphambi kokubhaliswa kosuku lokuvavanyelwa iphepha-mvume lokuqhuba (Luthathele ingqalelo usuku lovavanyo).
Bhatala imali emisiweyo.

Inkcazelo
Ummi waseMzantsi Afrika ofuna ukubangummi welinye ilizwe kufanele enze isicelo kwiSebe lezeKhaya ukuze agcine ubumi bakhe baseMzantsi Afrika phambi kokuba afumane ubumi belinye ilizwe. Ubuzwe okanye ubumi bamazwe amabini buthetha ukuba lo mntu uthathwa ngokuba ungummi wawo omabini la mazwe.
Ubumi bamazwe amabini bunikwa abantu abaneminyaka yobudala engaphezulu kwama 21.
Yenza isicelo kwindlu yozakuzo yaseMzantsi Afrika okanye kwiziko elimele uMzantsi Afrika ukuba wenza isicelo ukwilizwe langaphandle.

Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
I-SARS ifake imigangatho yokunika iinkonzo eyakungeniswa ngokwezigaba kwisithuba seminyaka emibini (2005 ukuya kutsho ku 2007). Xa ubhalisa okanye uhlawula, i-SARS ijolisa ekubeni iqhubekise ubhaliso lwakho ngokuchanekileyo kwisithuba seentsuku zokusebenza ezili 10.

Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Okwangoku, kufumaneka ezi fom zerhafu zilandelayo:
Abarhafi banikwa ithuba lokufumana, ukugcwalisa, ukuthumela nokuhlawula irhafu ngeendlela zokuhlawula ezithembekileyo nezikhuselekileyo, ngamaxesha onke ngemini.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Khetha iqhosha lokubhalisa elingasekhohlo, uze ukhethe uhlobo lobhaliso olubandakanyeka kuwe.
Uphawu olusisitshixo sokuvula kunye negama lokungena eliyimfihlo yakho ziyakukhutshwa kuphela xa umrhafi okanye ummeli womrhafi, eqondiwe ukuba nguye nyhani na, ngokuhambisana namanyathelo ogqaliselo losayino lwe-website.
Akuba umrhafi eyigcwalisile ifom yerhafu, inkcazelo efakwe kwifom iphononongwa ngokugqibeleleyo ukuze kuqinisekwe ukuba ifanelekile. Lonke ubalo lwenziwa yile nkqubo yomatshini ukuze kususwe naliphina ithuba lokufakeka kwenkcazelo engachanekanga.
Umrhafi angakhetha ukuhlawula xa ebuyisa ifom yerhafu kwaye angayenza loo ntlawulo naninina phambi komhla ekufanele ingene ngawo.
Nangona nje le nkqubo ivakala ngathi inzima, eneneni, xa uyisebenzisa, ilula kwaye iyakhawuleza. Uncedo ulufumana nje ngokutsalela umnxeba kwiZiko lokuTsalela uMnxeba nakwiCandelo leNkxaso elinesitafu esaneleyo ukuze ukhokelwe kule nkqubo.
Entla
Entla

Ubudlelwane bezabasebenzi
Ukucela ikomiti yeenkonzo eziyimfuneko engundoqo i
Ukucela ikomiti yeenkonzo eziyimfuneko engundoqo iqhube uphando lokuqonda ukuba ingaba inkonzo ethile iyonke okanye inxenye yayo, iyinkonzo eyimfuneko engundoqo na
Inkcazelo
Xa kuthethwa ngenkonzo eyimfuneko engundoqo (essential service) kubhekiswa kwinkonzo, eyakuthi, xangaba iphazamisekile, yenze ingozi okanye idale umonakalo kubomi okanye kwimpilo yabantu.
ingaba inkonzo iyinkonzo eyimfuneko engundoqo na okanye hayi;
ingaba umqeshwa okanye umqashi ubandakanyeka kwinkonzo echongwe nejngenkonzo eyimfuneko engundoqo na okanye hayi.
Iqela elithumela le mbambano kwikomiti yeenkonzo eziyimfuneko engundoqo kufuneka libonise ubungqina kwikomiti bokuba ikopi yesicelo sokuthumela imbambano ithunyelwe kuwo onke amanye amaqela abandakanyeka kwimbambano. Ikomiti yeenkonzo eziyimfuneko engundoqo kufuneka yenze isigqibo ngale mbambano kwamsinyane kangangoko inako.
Iinkonzo zePalamente, iNkonzo yaMapolisa aseMzantsi Afrika kunye nenkonzo yezeMpilo, ziinkonzo eziyimfuneko engundoqo.
Ukuze ufumane inkcazelo ebanzi, yiya kwiSebe leZabasebenzi.
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Thumela ikopi yale fom kwelinye iqela elibandakanyeka kwimbambano.
Nika ubungqina bokuba ikopi yale fom isiwe kwelinye iqela eli libandakanyeka kwimbambano, ngokufaka:
Ikopi yesiliphu serejista esiphuma ePosini; okanye
Ingxelo esayiniweyo yalo mntu uhambise ikopi yefom; okanye
Ikopi yesiliphu esingqinayo sefeksi okanye nabuphina obunye ubungqina obanelisayo benkonzo.
Ixesha elithatyyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iyakuxhomekeka kumaqela abhengeza iinkonzo njengeenkonzo eziyimfuneko engundoqo.
Iindleko
Le nkonzo ayihlawulelwa

Ubudlelwane bezabasebenzi
Isicelo esiya kwikomiti yeenkonzo eziyimfuneko engundoqo sokuba iqulunqe ukuba ingaba ishishini lomqeshi lilonke, okanye inxenye yalo, liyinkonzo yokuxhasa nokugcina indawo ethile yokusebenza, ifektri okanye oomatshini, ingatshabalali na
Inkcazelo
Umqeshi angenza isicelo ngencwadi ebhaliweyo kwikomiti yeenkonzo eziyimfuneko engundoqo sokuba iqulunqe ukuba ingaba ishishini lomqeshi lilonke, okanye inxenye yalo, liyinkonzo yokuxhasa nokugcina indawo ethile yokusebenza, ifektri, okanye oomatshini, ingatshabalali na.
Inkonzo iyinkonzo yokuxhasa nokulondoloza ukubangaba ukuphazamiseka kwaloo nkonzo kungadala ukutshabalala okunembonakalo nokubambekayo kuyo nayiphi na indawo yokusebenza, ifektri okanye oomatshini.
Nabaphi na abanye ababandakanyeki abanomnqweno, bangathumela impendulo kwiNkonzo eyiMfuneko eNgundoqo, kwisithuba seentsuku ezingama- 21 befumene esi sicelo.
Ukuze ufumane inkcazelo ebanzi yiya kwiSebe lezaBasebenzi
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ikopi yale fom kufuneka ithunyelwe komnye umbandakanyeki kwaye kufuneka kunikwe ubungqina bokuba ikopi yale fom isiwe komnye umbandakanyeki, ngokufaka ezi zinto zilandelayo:
Makufakwe ikopi yesiliphu serejista esiphuma ePosini.
Ingxelo esayiniweyo engqina ukuhanjiswa kwekopi ngulo mntu uhambise ifom kufuneka ihambe nesicelo.
Makufakwe ikopi yesiliphu esingqinayo sefeksi okanye nabuphi na obunye ubungqina obanelisayo.
Imithetho esetyenziswayo
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Akukho xesha libekiweyo; kuxhomekeka kumbandakanyeki owenza isicelo seenkonzo eziyimfuneko engundoqo.
Iindleko
Le nkonzo ayihlawulelwa.

Ukusebenza eMzantsi Afrika
INgqesho
Isicelo sepemethe yokusebenza yezakhono ezikhetheke zodwa
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Ipemethe yokusebenza yezakhono ezikhetheke zodwa inikwa umntu welizwe langaphandle onezakhono okanye iikhwalifikheyshini ezikhetheke zodwa. Inganikwa namalungu efemeli esondele nqo kuloo mntu. Izicelo zingenziwa kwindlu yozakuzo yaseMzantsi Afrika okanye kwiziko elimele uMzantsi Afrika.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ubungqina bokubanako ngokwemali, ngohlobo lwezitetimenti zebhanki, iincwadi ezibonisa umvuzo, isibhengezo sesithembiso esenziwe liziko oza kulo okanye izibhengezo zezithembiso ezenziwe ngamaziko oza kuwo, eMzantsi Afrika, iibhasari, izicwangciso zonyango, okanye imali ekhoyo, kubandakanywa amakhadi emboleko yekhredithi okanye iitshekhi zomhambi, eyakujongana neendleko ezicingelwayo zentlalo nokuphila ngexesha lokuhlala eMzantsi Afrika.
Veza incwadi ephuma kwiziko lombuso welizwe langaphandle okanye waseMzantsi Afrika okanye ephuma kwiqumrhu elimiyo laseMzantsi Afrika lezemfundo, lenkcubeko okanye lezoshishino, engqina izakhono okanye iikhwalifikheyshini zakho ezikhetheke zodwa.
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Le nkonzo ithabatha ixesha elingagqithiyo kwiintsuku ezingama 30.

Isicelo sokutshintshela ilayisensi yomqhubi yelizwe langaphandle
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Iilayisensi zabaqhubi ezikhutshwe kwamanye amazwe kwaye ezamkelweyo eMzantsi Afrika ziya kuguqulelwa kwiilayisensi zabaqhubi eziluhlobo lwekhadi lekhredithi xa abantu abanezi layisensi befuneka befumene iilayisensi zaseMzantsi Afrika ngokoMthetho weLizwe weZithuthi zeNdlela (National Road Traffic Act, 1996).
Isicelo sokutshintshela imvumelo yomqhubi yamazwe ngamazwe kufanele sikhatshwe yilayisensi yomqhubi esegunyeni, eyakhutshelwa yona le mvumelo.
Ilayisensi yomqhubi yelizwe langaphandle okanye iMvumelo yoMqhubi yaMazwe ngaMazwe ingatshintshelwa kwilayisensi yaseMzantsi Afrika kuphela akube umenzi-sicelo engummi waseMzantsi Afrika, okanye akube efumene imvume yokuhlala isigxina kweli lizwe (oko kukuthi, hayi abantu abaneemvumelo zozakuzelwano okanye zezivumelwano phakathi kwamazwe).
Ilayisensi yomqhubi yelizwe langaphandle kufuneka ibe isemthethweni ngomhla wokutshintshela kwaye kufuneka ibekwelinye leelwimi ezigunyazisiweyo zaseMzantsi Afrika. Ukuba akunjalo, isicelo masikhatshwe yinguqulelo ekhutshwe ngugunyaziwe onelungelo noxanduva lokwenza njalo.
Xa umntu onelayisensi yokuqhuba yelizwe langaphandle ephinda eqalisa ukubangumhlali osisigxina, okanye efumana imvume yokuhlala isigxina eMzantsi Afrika, ilayisensi yelizwe langaphandle iya kuphelelwa ukuba semthethweni kunyaka omnye ukusukela kumhla loo mntu athabathe ngawo okanye aphinde waqalisa ngawo ukuhlala isigxina.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
o khupha incwadi eyamkelekileyo yokuzazisa njengoko kumiselwe ngumthetho waseMzantsi Afrika (umzekelo, iNcwadi yeSazisi (ID), i-ID yexeshana, ipaspoti esemthethweni yaseMzantsi Afrika, okanye ipaspoti yelizwe langaphandle ehamba nemvumelo yokuhlala isigxina).
o hambisa incwadi ephuma kugunyaziwe onelungelo noxanduva lokukhupha loo ncwadi, engqina ukuba semthethweni kwelayisensi yakho yokuqhuba yelizwe langaphandle, futhi echaza udidi lwelayisensi (uhlobo lwesithuthi esingasetyenziswa)
o hambisa ilayisensi yakho yokuqhuba yelizwe langaphandle o hambisa iifoto ezine ze-ID, zombala omnyama nomhlophe.
Hlawula imali ebandakanyekayo njengoko imiselwe ngumthetho waseMzantsi Afrika.
Uya kuhlolwa amehlo kweli ziko phambi kokuba kugqitywe ukutshintshelwa.
Qaphela: Awuyikungenela zimviwo zelayisensi yomqhubi. Ilayisensi yomqhubi yexeshana isemthethweni iinyanga ezintandathu kwaye ikhutshwa kwangoko, ngaphandle kwendleko.

Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Ipemethe yotshintshiselwano inganikwa umntu welizwe langaphandle othabatha inxaxheba kwinkqubo yenkcubeko, yezoqoqosho okanye yentlalo, eququzelelwa okanye ephethwe liziko lombuso wakweli okanye welizwe langaphandle, okanye liziko loluntu lemfundo ephakamileyo, ngokusebenzisana neziko lombuso welizwe langaphandle. Yenza isicelo sepemethe yotshintshiselwano kwindlu yozakuzo yaseMzantsi Afrika okanye kwiziko elimele uMzantsi Afrika elikufuphi kuwe.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Hambisa ipaspoti yakho esebenzisekayo ikunye nesicelo.
Khupha incwadi ephuma kwiziko, umbutho okanye kwifemeli ojonge ukuqhubela kuyo le nkqubo eMzantsi Afrika, ungqine ubume okanye ubukho benkqubo yotshintshiselwano. Incwadi kufuneka ingqine ukuba uyavumeleka ubhalisele le nkqubo okanye uthabathe inxaxheba kuyo kwaye kukwafuneka ichaze ukuba eli ziko, umbutho okanye ifemeli, iyakubanoxanduva lwakho ngelixa ukweli laseMzantsi Afrika.
Fumana incwadi esuka kwiziko elifanelekileyo lombuso okanye kwiqumrhu elixhasayo kwilizwe lakowenu, ingqine ubume okanye ubukho benkqubo yotshintshiselwano noMzantsi Afrika, ndawonye nomba wokuba wamkelwe ukuze ubhalisele le nkqubo.
Entla
Entla

Ukuhlala eMzantsi Afrika
Imfundo
Isicelo sepemethe yenkqubo yokutshintshiselana ngabafundi
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Ipemethe yenkqubo yokutshintshiselana ngabafundi yipemethe enikwa umfundi welizwe langaphandle ekufanele athabathe inxaxheba kwiprojekthi okanye kwinkqubo ethile kwiziko lemfundo laseMzantsi Afrika elikwinqanaba lesithathu (imfundo ephakamileyo, umzekelo, iyunivesiti okanye iyunivesiti yobuchwepheshe.)
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Yenza isicelo kwindlu yozakuzo yaseMzantsi Afrika okanye kwiziko elimele uMzantsi Afrika.
Hambisa incwadi esuka kwiSebe leMfundo okanye kwiziko loluntu lemfundo ephakamileyo eMzantsi Afrika:
o engqina ukuba eli ziko lilo eliququzelela okanye eliphethe le nkqubo o echaza imisebenzi yale nkqubo kunye nexesha eliyakuthatyathwa yile nkqubo o engqina ukuba eli ziko liyakuthabatha uxanduva olupheleleyo malunga nalo mfundi ngelixa ekwiRiphabhlikhi kwaye umfundi wamkelelwe ukuba abhaliswe.
Hambisa incwadi esuka kwiziko elithile lelizwe langaphandle:
o engqina iinkcukacha zomfundi, kubandakanywa ubhaliso lomfundi kwiziko lemfundo ekwinqanaba lesithathu kwilizwe langaphandle o engqina umhla eyakuqala ngawo le nkqubo eMzantsi Afrika.

Isicelo sepemethe yokuthumela impahla nezinto kuma
Isicelo sokuncediswa kwiinkqubo zokuphuhlisa iimarike zokuthumela iimveliso neenkonzo kumazwe angaphandle kunye notyalo-mali
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Ukunika imbuyekezo eyinxalenye yeendleko ezithile ezifumaneke ngokwemisebenzi ejongene nokuphuhlisa iimarike zokuthumela iimveliso neenkonzo zaseMzantsi Afrika kumazwe angaphandle, kunye nokugaya utyalo-mali lwamazwe angaphandle olutsha noluza nqo eMzantsi Afrika.
I-EMIA inika abathumeli-ngaphandle uncediso lwemali ukuze babonise ngeemveliso neenkonzo zabo kumazwe ehlabathi kwaye iyancedisa kwiinkqubo zabo zokwakha ubudlelwane ukuze bafumane iimarike zokuthumela iimveliso neenkonzo kumazwe angaphandle kunye notyalo-mali lwamazwe angaphandle oluza nqo. Ikwancedisa ekulinganiseleni iindleko zemarike zomthumeli-ngaphandle.
Le nkonzo ijoliswe kwezi klayenti zilandelayo:
Amashishini eenkonzo ngokweeprojekthi, ngokusekelwe kubungqina obuvela kwiBhunga lokuThumela iiMveliso neeNkonzo kuMazwe aNgaphandle okanye kwi-Ofisi yeCandelo le-TISA, bokuba le projekthi yenkonzo ethile iyakubayinzuzo kwicandelo kwaye yongeze ixabiso.
Inkqubo
Ukuze ufumane inkcazelo ebanzi, yiya KwiSebe le zoRhwebo naMashishini
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Inkonzo nganye ye-EMIA inencwadana yayo yezikhokelo, equlathe inkcazelo malunga nendlela yokuvumeleka, amaxesha abekiweyo kunye neenzuzo ezibandakanyeka kwiinkqubo ezahlukeneyo zamacandelo.
Inyathelo lokuqala: Sebenzisa incwadana yezikhokelo
Funda le miqulu ngocoselelo ukuze uyazi kakuhle imigaqo neenkqubo.
Lunikiwe uluhlu oluphangaleleyo lwemiqulu ekufuneka ithunyelwe nesicelo. Incwadana yezikhokelo nayo iyakubonisa ukubangaba kukho eminye imiqulu efunekayo.
Inyathelo lesithathu: Hambisa isicelo
Amashishini angathumela izicelo eziphelela kwisithandathu enyakeni, kwaye baqingqelwe izicelo ezine kwicebo lesicwangciso ngasinye. Nawuphina umnyenyevu womahluko kufuneka ugunyaziswe nguManejala oMkhulu we-EMIA.
Izicelo ezifike emva kwexesha nezingagcwaliswanga ngokupheleleyo aziyi kuqwalaselwa.
Inyathelo lesine: Ukuqhubekiswa kwesicelo
I-EMIA iyakuthumela incwadi yokuvuma ukufunyanwa kwesicelo kwisithuba seeyure zokusebenza ezingama 48 emva kokuba ifumene isicelo sakho. Le ncwadi yokuvuma ukufunyanwa kwesicelo kufuneka ibandakanywe kuyo yonke imbalelwano nonxulumano lwexesha elizayo ne-EMIA.
Inyathelo lesihlanu: Ukuvunywa okanye ukwaliwa kwesicelo
I-EMIA iyakukwazisa ngokuba isicelo siphumelele na okanye saliwe kwisithuba seeyure ezingama 48 emva kokuba kuthatyathwe isigqibo sokugqibela.
Izicelo azinakuvunywa ngomlomo. Kufuneka uqinisekise ukuba isicelo sivunywe ngencwadi ebhaliweyo phambi kokuba unduluke.
Ikopi yesaziso sokuvunywa kufuneka ikhaphe yonke imbalelwano nonxulumano lwexesha elizayo kunye nokuthunyelwa okanye ukuthunyelwa kweminye imiqulu kwi-EMIA. Ukubangaba i-EMIA ifumana enye imbalelwano nonxulumano okanye imiqulu engasibandakanyiyo isaziso sokuvunywa, i-EMIA ayinakuthwaliswa uxanduva ukubangaba le miqulu ilahlekile okanye ibekwe kwiindawo ezingachanekanga. Ukubangaba le miqulu ilahlekile, loo nto ingathintela okanye ilibazise inkqubo yokuqhubekiswa kwesicelo.
Sakuba sivunyiwe isicelo soncediso, kufuneka kugcwaliswe ifom yesibango ye-EMIA, yonke imiqulu yokuxhasa kunye noxwebhu olufanelekileyo lwemibuzo, kwaye le miqulu ithunyelwe kwi-EMIA kwisithuba seenyanga ezintathu zomhla wokubuya kwindawo evunyiweyo obuye kuyo yoshishino.
Ukubangaba kukho imiba okanye imiqulu engekhoyo malunga nesibango emva kweenyanga ezintathu, isibango siyakwaliwa.

Iinkonzo zokungenisa impahla nezinto kweli lizwe k
Isicelo sepemethe yokuthumela impahla nezinto kuma
Isicelo sepemethe yokuthumela impahla nezinto kuma
Isicelo sepemethe yokuthumela impahla nezinto kumazwe angaphandle
Inkcazelo
Ipemethe yokuthumela impahla nezinto kumazwe angaphandle iyafuneka ukuze kuqinisekiswe ukuba umntu okanye umbutho oneenjongo zokuthumela impahla nezinto kumazwe angaphandle uhambisana nemiyalelo yokuthumela impahla nezinto kumazwe angaphandle kwaye uyahambisana nemimiselo yezivumelwano zamazwe ehlabathi. Iipemethe zokuthumela impahla nezinto kumazwe angaphandle zikwanceda ekulawuleni ukuphuma kwempahla nezinto ezinobaluleko oluthile okanye ukuphuma kwempahla nezinto ezirhubuluziswa ngomgunyathi okanye ezibiweyo.
Umgaqo osebenziseka ekungeniseni impahla nezinto kweli lizwe, nasekuthumeleni impahla nezinto kumazwe angaphandle, wahluka ngokwamacandelo eli shishini. Kwakhona, uninzi lwempahla nezinto ezintsha zinomnyenyevu wokungabandakanywa kumanyathelo okulawula ukungena kwempahla nezinto kweli lizwe. Ngoko ke, ukubangaba udinga inkcazelo yomgaqo malunga nokungeniswa nokukhutshwa kwempahla nezinto ezichaziweyo, nceda unike i-ofisi yoLawulo lweMpahla neZinto eziNgena kweli Lizwe kunye neziThunyelwa kuMazwe aNgaphandle (Import and Export Control), ekwiSebe lezoRhwebo naMashishini.
Ayizizo zonke impahla nezinto okanye iimveliso eziphantsi kwamanyathelo olawulo lokungena nokuthunyelwa ngaphandle okanye lokuthunyelwa ngaphandle. Nangona kunjalo, zonke impahla nezinto esele zisetyenzisiwe, impahla nezinto ezingamasekendi, izinto ezichithwayo nezilahlwayo, ziphantsi kwamanyathelo olawulo lokungena kweli lizwe. Luyafumaneka uluhlu lwamagama empahla nezinto eziphantsi kwamanyathelo olawulo lwempahla nezinto ezingena kweli lizwe kunye nezithunyelwa kumazwe angaphandle. Ukubangaba unika iinkcukacha zonxulumano, olu luhlu ungaluthunyelwa ngeposi, ngefeksi okanye nge e-mail.
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Nxulumana neZiko loLawulo lweMpahla neZinto eziNgena kweli Lizwe kunye neziThunyelwa kuMazwe aNgaphandle, leSebe lezoRhwebo naMashishini.
Ixesha elithatyyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Kungathabatha ixesha elifikelela kwiintsuku ezintathu ukuze kuqhubekiswe isicelo sakho sepemethe yokuthumela impahla nezinto kumazwe angaphandle.
Indleko
Le nkonzo ayihlawulelwa.

Abaqashi kufuneka batyikitye (basayine) isibhengezo kwaye bagximfize isitampu senkampani.
Ukubangaba asikho isitampu, ingqesho kufuneka ingqinwe ngencwadi esecaleni ekwisihloko esigunyazisiweyo senkampani.
Hambisa isatifiketi esiphuma emapoliseni esiqinisekisa ubume obumsulwa (ukubangaba zange usihambise ngokuya wawufaka isicelo sokuqala).
Hambisa ikopi yekhontrakthi egunyazisiweyo yengqesho.
Ukubangaba kuyabandakanyeka, hambisa ubungqina bobhaliso kwiqumrhu elifanelekileyo lobuchule boqeqesho.
Veza imiba ebonisa izicwangciso zomenzi-sicelo zexesha elizayo.
Hambisa ingxelo yenkqubela engqina ukuba abemi baseMzantsi Afrika okanye abahlali abasisigxina baqeqeshiwe okanye bayaqeqeshwa.

Inkcazelo
Abantu abanqwenela ukubangabanikazi bemipu kufuneka baqale baphumelele uvavanyo loqeqesho oluqingqiweyo kwiziko loqeqesho elinoqinisekiso lokuvunywa nokwamkelwa (accredited) kwaye bafumane isatifiketi sokuphumelela uqeqesho. Uluhlu lwamagama wamaziko oqeqesho anoqinisekiso lokuvunywa nokwamkelwa lugcinwa kwi-website ye-SAPS okanye ungatsalela umnxeba kwiZiko laMapolisa lokuTsalela uMnxeba leMipu yeLizwe kwinombolo ethi: +27 12 353 6111 okanye uthumele ifeksi e: +27 12 353 6036 ukuze ufumane inkcazelo.

Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Phatha le miqulu ilandelayo xa usiya kwiGosa eliSebenza ngeMipu:
o iSatifiketi soLwazi neZakhono esiluqobo lwaso (ukuba sesikhutshiwe)
Faka iziphakamiso zokuxhasa isicelo sakho ngokugcweleyo kwaye ufake imiqulu yokuxhasa esi sicelo.
IGosa eliSebenza ngeMipu liyakukunika isiqwengana sephepha lokuhlawula kwaye likuthumele kwi-Ofisi yezeMali kwisikhululo samapolisa ukuze uhlawule le mali ichaziweyo. Le ntlawulo mayenziwe ngekhetshi okanye ngetshekhi eqinisekiswe yibhanki. Uyakunikwa irisiti yenkcitho (Z263) njengobungqina bentlawulo kwaye kufuneka uyise kwiGosa eliSebenza ngeMipu ukuze likwazi ukuqhubeka ngesicelo sakho.
Uyakufumana incwadi esayiniweyo evuma ukufunyanwa kwesicelo (SAPS 523), njengobungqina bokuba ufake isicelo selayisensi yokubanompu.

ILayisensi yoMpu: R140

Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ungenza izicelo ngexesha elinye zokuvuselela ilayisensi okanye iilayisensi ezahlukeneyo onazo zemipu. Kusetyenziswa la maxesha alandelayo, ngokwemihla yokuzalwa:
Umhla wokuzalwa
Ixesha lokuvuselela
Phatha le miqulu ilandelayo uyise kwiGosa eliSebenza ngeMipu kwisikhululo samapolisa esikufuphi kwindawo ohlala kuyo:
o incwadi yakho yesazisi egunyazisiweyo o ilayisensi okanye iilayisensi eziluqobo lwazo, ipemethe okanye ugunyaziso lompu okanye lwemipu onqwenela ukuyivuselela o isatifiketi soqeqesho esiluqobo lwaso esifunyenwe kumniki-nkonzo zoqeqesho onoqinisekiso lokuvunywa nokwamkelwa o iSatifiketi soLwazi neZakhono esiluqobo lwaso (ukuba sesikhutshiwe)
o iifoto zombala eziphume ngokucacileyo, ezilingana kwipaspoti kwaye ezingagqibanga iinyanga ezintathu zifotiwe (kufuneka iifoto ezimbini kuzo zonke iilayisensi onqwenela ukuzivuselela kunye neefoto ezimbini zesicelo sesatifiketi solwazi nezakhono).
IGosa eliSebenza ngeMipu liyakukunika isiqwengana sephepha lokuhlawula SAPS 523a kwaye likuthumele kwi-ofisi yezemali kwisikhululo samapolisa ukuze uhlawule iR70 yesatifiketi solwazi nezakhono kunye ne R70 yelayisensi nganye yemipu ofuna ukuyivuselela. Le ntlawulo mayenziwe ngekhetshi okanye ngetshekhi eqinisekiswe yibhanki. Uyakunikwa irisiti yenkcitho Z263 njengobungqina bentlawulo. Yisa le Z263 kwiGosa eliSebenza ngeMipu ukuze liqhubeke ngesicelo sakho.
Uyakufumana incwadi esayiniweyo evuma ukufunyanwa kwesicelo (SAPS 523), njengobungqina bokuba uzifakile izicelo zokuvuselela ilayisensi okanye iilayisensi zemipu.
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
IGosa eliSebenza ngeMipu liyakuqhuba uphengululo lokukujonga ukuba ingaba ungumntu ofanelekileyo nokulungeleyo na ukubanompu. IGosa eliSebenza ngeMipu liyakuya kuhlola nqo indawo yakho ukuze liqonde amanyathelo ezokhuseleko kwindawo yakho nakwiindawo ezijikeleze le ndawo, lijonge ibhokisi yokugcina umpu ngokukhuselekileyo (iseyifu), lingqine ukuhambisana nemigangatho yoGunyaziwe weMigangatho waseMzantsi Afrika ekuthiwa yi-South African Bureau of Standards (SABS). Ukubangaba ufumene ilayisensi yompu phambi komhla we 1 Julayi 2004 kwaye kufuneka uvuselele loo layisensi, akukho mfuneko yokuthenga ibhokisi entsha yokugcina umpu ngokhuseleko. Iimfuneko ezikhoyo ngokweMigqaliselo yeZixhobo neeMbumbulu zokuDubula, zika 1994, zithathwa ngokuba ziyamkeleka. Ukubangaba nayiphina ibhokisi yokugcina umpu ngokhuseleko ayihambisani nezo mfuneko, kufuneka uthenge entsha ehambisana nemigangatho ye-SABS.
Sakube isicelo okanye izicelo zakho ziqwalaselwe ngempumelelo, iGosa eliSebenza ngeMipu liyakunxulumana nawe nqo ngobuqu bakho ukuze uyokuthatha isatifiketi sakho solwazi nezakhono (ukubangaba asikakhutshwa) kunye nelayisensi okanye iilayisensi zakho zemipu.
Entla

Isicelo sakho sobhaliso kufuneka siqulathe le nkcazelo ilandelayo:
o iinkcukacha zequmrhu lokukhusela umlilo elingumgqatswa o iinkcukacha zomntu oqalisa inyathelo lobhaliso lwequmrhu lokukhusela umlilo elingumgqatswa o isibhengezo sokuba akukho mnikazi okhethwe ngabom kubandakanyo kwiintlanganiso neengxoxo malunga nokusekwa kweli qumrhu lokukhusela umlilo o iinkcukacha zommandla elinegunya lokusebenza kuwo eli qumrhu lokukhusela umlilo lingumgqatswa o isibhengezo sokuba alikho elinye iqumrhu lokukhusela umlilo elijongiweyo okanye elikhoyo ngaphakathi kulo mmandla wequmrhu lokukhusela umlilo elingumgqatswa o isibhengezo esenziwe ngumntu oqalisa inyathelo lokusekwa kwequmrhu lokukhusela umlilo o isiphakamiso esenziwe ngummeli ofanelekileyo worhulumente wendawo yabahlali o isiphakamiso esenziwe ngummeli wengingqi wesebe lezamanzi namahlathi o isibhengezo esenziwe ngumqondisi oyintloko wengingqi weSebe lezaManzi naMahlathi.

Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Isaziso sokuzalwa kufuneka sifakwe ngomnye wabazali okanye ngumntu ongumlondolozi ngokwasemthethweni, kwaye ukubangaba abazali okanye umntu ongumlondolozi ngokwasemthethweni abakwazi ukwenza njalo, umntu ocelwe ngomnye wabazali okanye ngumntu ongumlondolozi ngokwasemthethweni, angasifaka isaziso.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Umntu ocelwe ukuba afake isaziso kufuneka abenomyalelo obhaliweyo wokwenza njalo, ekufuneka ubandakanye izizathu zokuba kutheni abazali bengenako ukufaka isaziso ngokwabo.
Ukubangaba umntwana uzalelwe ngaphandle koMzantsi Afrika, kwaye omnye wabazali ungummi waseMzantsi Afrika ngexesha lokuzalwa komntwana, oku kuzalwa kungaziswa kwiNdlu yoZakuzo yaseMzantsi Afrika, kwiZiko loNxulumano noMzantsi Afrika, okanye kuyo nayiphina i-ofisi yezeKhaya eMzantsi Afrika.
Kwisaziso esenziwe emva kweentsuku ezingama 30 zokuzalwa, kodwa phambi konyaka emva kokuzalwa, abazali okanye umntu ongumlondolozi ngokwasemthethweni, mabanike izizathu zokuba kutheni ukuzalwa kungabhaliswanga kwisithuba seentsuku ezingama 30 njengoko kuyimfuneko ngokoMthetho.
Ukubangaba abazali abatshatanga kwaye banqwenela ukubhalisa umntwana ngefani kayise, uyise womntwana makavume ukubanguyise walo mntwana kwisithuba esilungiselelwe oko kwifom yeSaziso sokuZalwa. Utata womntwana makabekhona xa kubhaliswa ukuzalwa.

Entla

Inkcazelo
Ukuze uvumeleke, kufuneka ube ungumntu owayekade edlelwa indlala (oko kukuthi uNtsundu, uliKhaladi okanye uliNdiya)
ubeneminyaka yobudala eli 18 okanye ngaphezulu ube ujonge ukusebenzisa umhlaba ngeenjongo zezolimo kuphela ube ujonge ukubangumfama ngokupheleleyo ube awunasikhundla osibambileyo kumacandelo karhulumente uzimisele ukuthabatha inxaxheba kwinkqubo yoqeqesho emva kokuba ufumene umhlaba ubekwimeko yokuba ungenza igalelo ubeliqumrhu elakhiwe ngokwamacandelo ukubangaba nenza isicelo ningumbutho, kwaye ubene-akhawunti yebhanki.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Chaza umhlaba ofuna ukuwuthenga. Kungenjalo, mhlawumbi sele unawo umhlaba, ofana nomhlala onabanikazi abawudibaneleyo.
Nxulumana neSebe lezeMihlaba okanye igosa lendawo ohlala kuyo lesihlomelo sezolimo (agricultural extension) ukuze wenze isicelo segranti.
Hambisa le miqulu ilandelayo nesicelo sakho:
o indlela yokukhetha ukuthengisa ngexabiso ekuvunyelwene ngalo ukubangaba ungenela isivumelwano sengqeshiso esinendlela yokukhetha ukuthenga o uluhlu lwamalungu ekhaya okanye amalungu ombutho, ukubangaba umpoposho ngowombutho o ubungqina bokuba itayitile kulo mhlaba icacile, ayinazibango zomhlaba, ibhaliswe ngegama lomthengisi kwaye ixabiso ekuthetha-thethwane ngalo alikho ngaphezulu kwexabiso eliphakanyiswe yimarike o ubungqina bokuba le mali iseleyo ikhona (iimali ezizezo-menzi-sicelo okanye ikhontrakthi yemali-mboleko elungiselelayo)
o ingxelo yokuphonononga ixabiso

Isicelo sokufumana incwadi yesazisi okokuqala
Isicelo sokufumana incwadi yesazisi okokuqala
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Incwadi yesazisi (ID) yincwadi eyazisa nengqina ngomntu. Iincwadi zezazisi zinikwa abemi baseMzantsi Afrika okanye abantu abaneepemethe zokuhlala isigxina kweli lizwe abaneminyaka eli 16 okanye nangaphezulu. Inganikwa nakubani osebenzela urhulumente okanye iqumrhu lasembusweni elingaphandle koMzantsi Afrika okanye umntu othunyelwe kwisikhundla sokusebenzela elinye ilizwe. Oku kugqithiselwa nakumlingane nabantwana balo mntu.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Uyakunyatheliswa iminwe (fingerprints) ukuze ishicilelwe kwiNcwadi eBhale iNani neeNkcukacha zaBantu belizwe.
Abenzi-zicelo abatshatileyo mabakhuphe ikopi yesatifiketi somtshato.
Owasetyhini owenza isicelo sencwadi yesazisi kwaye enqwenela ukuphinda abuyele kuyo nayiphina ifani kwiifani awayekade esaziwa ngazo, makathi thaca ubungqina bokuba uvumelekile kuloo fani.
Umntu ongumngeni kweli lizwe owenza isicelo sencwadi yesazisi makafake kwesi sicelo ipemethe yokuhlala isigxina, isatifiketi sokwenziwa ummi weli lizwe okanye sokunikwa umnyenyevu, isatifiketi somtshato, kunye nefom ekuthiwa yi BI-529.

Isicelo sokungenisa elizweni iimveliso zezilwanyan
Isicelo sokungenisa elizweni iimveliso zezilwanyana ngenjongo yokuzisebenzisa ngokwakho okanye ukuzihambisa ukugqitha eMzantsi Afrika
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Kudingeka iphepha lemvume (ipemethe) yokungenisa izilwanyana xa ungenisa izilwanyana okanye iimveliso zezilwanyana kwiRiphabhlikhi yaseMzantsi Afrika.
Zikho izivumelwano zokungenisa izilwanyana kunye neemveliso zezilwanyana kweli lizwe. Njengoko izinto eziyimfuneko zempilo ziguquka rhoqo, nceda unxulumane neCandelo loBuqondisi beMpilo yeZilwanyana (Directorate Animal Health) ukuze uqonde ngezinto eziyimfuneko zakutshanje.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Isebe: 010845
Iintlawulo zingenziwa kananjalo kwiiofisi zeSebe lezoLimo ezikuluhlu lwee-Iindawo zoqhagamshelwano.
Ukuba wenzela omnye umntu isicelo, nceda uqinisekise ukuba uhlawula phantsi kwegama laloo mntu okanye laloo nkampani.
Pretoria okanye uzithumele kwifeksi ethi 012 329 8292
Kwiimeko apho izilwanyana kufuneka zivalelwe, umntu ozingenisa kweli makanxulumane neGosa lokuValelwa kwezilwanyana kwisango lokungena.
Isikhululo sokuvalela esise Durban asisebenzi okwangoku, kodwa inkcazelo ingafunyanwa kuloo ofisi kwinombolo yomnxeba ethi: 031 368 6011 okanye ngefeksi ethi: 031 337 7469
Kufuneka kugcwaliswe ifom yeSibhengezo soKhuseleko ekubekweni ityala (ngokuphathelelene nezilwanyana okanye iintaka ezivalelweyo ezingeniswa kweli lizwe) kwaye sifakwe apha kwifom yesicelo. Le fom yeSibhengezo soKhuseleko ekubekweni ityala ingafumaneka nakwi-Ofisi yeePemethe.
Kufuneka kugcwaliswe nge-English, ngugqirha wezilwanyana ogunyaziselwe ukwenza njalo liZiko loLawulo lwemibandela yeZilwanyana lelizwe elithumela ngaphandle, kwisithuba seentsuku ezili 10 zokumka kwazo.
Ukuba kukho inkcazelo edingekayo malunga neemfuneko nqo zesilwanyana esithile okanye imveliso ethile yesilwanyana, iikopi zokubonisa zePemethe yokuNgenisa iZilwanyana kweli kunye nezeSatifiketi seMpilo yeZilwanyana, zingafumaneka kwi-Ofisi yeePemethe.
Kufuneka kuvezwe ezi zinto zilandelayo kwiGosa eliLawula ukuNgeniswa kweZilwanyana eMzantsi Afrika kwiSango lokuNgena:
o iPemethe eluqobo lwayo yokuNgenisa iZilwanyana kweli o iSatifiketi esiluqobo lwaso seMpilo yeZilwanyana o nayiphina enye incwadi echaziweyo, umzekelo, iSibhengezo soKhuseleko ekubekweni ityala, iSatifiketi sokuGonyelwa uMgada, njalo-njalo.
Xa ungenisa izilwanyana eziphilileyo zasefama, ezifana neenkomo, iigusha, iibhokhwe, amahashe (ingezizo iikati nezinja), kufuneka ufumane ipemethe yokuphucula izilwanyana phambi kokuba kukhutshwe ipemethe yokungenisa izilwanyana.
Zombini ezi pemethe ziluqobo lwazo kufuneka zithiwe thaca kwiGosa leZilwanyana kwisango lokungena, ndawonye neSatifiketi esiluqobo lwaso seMpilo yeZilwanyana esikhutshwe lilizwe elithumela ngaphandle.
Intlawulo okanye ubungqina bentlawulo kufuneka bukhaphe ifomu yesicelo. Akukho sicelo siya kulungiswa ngaphandle kobungqina bentlawulo.

Isicelo sephepha lemvume yokungenisa amayeza okuto
Isicelo sephepha lemvume (sepemethe) yokungenisa amayeza okutofa izilwanyana, eMzantsi Afrika
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Kwimeko yonxunguphalo, apho kuqhambuke isifo kwaye kungekho yeza libhalisiweyo elifumanekayo eMzantsi Afrika, kungayimfuneko ukuba kusetyenziswe iyeza elingabhaliswanga. Ngoko ke, wena, njengomntu onqwenela ukungenisa iyeza kweli lizwe, kufuneka wenze isicelo kwiBhunga lokuLawula aMayeza (Medicines Control Council) ukuze ufumane umnyenyevu weCandelo 21 ngokoMthetho woLawulo lwaMayeza neeMveliso ezaYamene nawo (uMthetho 101 ka 1965, njengoko ulungisiwe nguMthetho 90 ka 1997).
Ukwadinga ipemethe yokungenisa, kwiCandelo loBuqondisi beMpilo yeZilwanyana, ukuze eli yeza lingene kweli lizwe. Eli Candelo likhupha le pemethe yokungenisa kuphela wakube ufumene imvume kwiBhunga lokuLawula aMayeza yaye ubuthumele ubungqina kweli candela. Kule meko ke, eli yeza lingabhaliswanga lingathengiswa ixesha eliqingqiweyo kude kufunyanwe ubhaliso.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
o ubungakanani bomthamo o igama lemveliso o isithako okanye izithako ezisebenzayo, kubandakanywa nentlanganisela yezithako o ilizwe eliphuma kulo o umenzi weyeza o inombolo yombhumbuthu womthwalo oyakungeniswa o iphepha lenkcazelo yobuchule okanye umbhalo wokuphawula okuqulathiweyo (nge-English), onenombolo yobhaliso yequmrhu lokugqalisela lelizwe ebhaliswe kulo le mveliso o isango lokungena o inkcazelo yokuba ifuneka nini na le mveliso o umba wokuba le mveliso ingeniselwa iinjongo zokulingelwa ubhaliso lweemveliso zokunceda imfuyo o ubume bobhaliso lwemveliso kwezinye iindawo (oko kukuthi, apho ibhaliswe khona)
o iSivumelwano soLingo esineenkcukacha (ngokweemfuno ze-VICH GCP), kubandakanywa imihla ekulindeleke ukuqaliswa ngayo uqwalaselo olulodwa lekamva lokutya okuphuma kwizilwanyana ezivelisa ukutya (umzekelo, iyakulahlwa) kunye nokuthabatha uxanduva lokulandela iimfuno zamachiza.
Ukubangaba iyeza sele libhaliselwe ukusetyenziswa eMzantsi Afrika ngokoMthetho 36 ka 1947, udinga kuphela ipemethe enye yokungenisa, kwiCandelo loBuqondisi beMpilo yeZilwanyana. Thumela ikopi yobhaliso ngokoMthetho 36 ka 1947 nesicelo sakho.
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Nceda wenze isicelo sepemethe yokungenisa izilwanyana okungenani kwiiveki ezintandathu phambi kokuba uthumele kweli. Akuba ugqirha wezilwanyana wombuso esivumile isicelo, kuthabatha iintsuku zokusebenza ezimbini ukuyakutsho kwezintathu ukuze i-ofisi yeepemethe iqhubekise kwaye ikhuphe ipemethe.

Isicelo sokungenisa eMzantsi Afrika isithuthi esil

Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Ukubangaba ufuna ukungenisa eMzantsi Afrika izithuthi ezingamasekendi okanye esele zisetyenzisiwe, kufuneka ubenemvume elungiselelwe le meko esuka kwiCandelo loBuphathiswa bezoRhwebo naMashishini okanye kubanxulumanisi balo. ICandelo loBuphathiswa liyakwenza isigqibo sokuba ingaba kungowona mnqweno ungcono woluntu na ukuba kungeniswe kweli lizwe ezi zithuthi zingamasekendi okanye sele zisetyenzisiwe.
Kufuneka uhambise ifom eqingqiweyo yesicelo ukuze wenze isicelo sepemethe yokungenisa impahla nezinto kweli lizwe. Iipemethe zokungenisa impahla nezinto kweli ziyafuneka kuzo zonke impahla nezinto eziphantsi kwamanyathelo olawulo lwempahla nezinto ezingena kweli.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Nika iSebe ikopi eqinisekisiweyo yencwadi yakho yesazisi.
Nika iSebe ikopi eqinisekisiweyo yesatifiketi sobhaliso lwesithuthi.

Inkcazelo
Abantu abafezekisa ezi mfuno zilandelayo bangenza izicelo:
ummi waseMzantsi Afrika okanye umntu onephepha lemvume (onepemethe) yokuhlala isigxina eMzantsi Afrika umntu otshatileyo okanye ohlala nesinqandamathe sethuba elide abantu abangatshatanga abangaphezulu kweminyaka engama 21 ubudala kwaye abanabantu abaxhomekeke kubo ingeniso-mali yekhaya liphelele yi R3 500 okanye ngaphantsi zange ngaphambili wabangumnikazi wepropati yokuhlala (iimeko ezingaqhelekanga ezizodwa ziyaqwalaselwa)
abenzi-zicelo abakhubazekileyo abenza izicelo zeenguqulo ezizodwa (siyafuneka isatifiketi sonyango).
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Gcwalisa ifom yesicelo efumaneka kuphela kwiSebe lezeZindlu kwiPhondo, ezibhankini nakoomasipala.
Faka zonke iincwadi zobungqina, umzekelo:
o incwadi yesazisi o isatifiketi somtshato o isatifiketi sokuzalwa o ubungqina bengeniso-mali, kunye o nencwadi yesigqibo sentengiso.

Ukusebenza eMzantsi Afrika
INgqesho
Isicelo sepemethe yokusebenza yokutshintshelwa kwinkampani enxulumeneyo
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Ipemethe yokutshintshelwa kwinkampani enxulumeneyo ikhutshelwa umntu welizwe langaphandle otshintshelwa yinkampani yakhe ukuze ayokusebenza kwinkampani enxulumene naleyo eMzantsi Afrika. Ixesha elithatyathwa yile pemethe yokusebenza yokutshintshelwa kwinkampani enxulumeneyo aligqithi kwiminyaka emibini. Izicelo zingenziwa kwindlu yozakuzo yaseMzantsi Afrika okanye kwiziko elimele uMzantsi Afrika.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Hambisa isiqinisekiso esenziwe ngumgcini nomhloli wee-akhawunti zemali olilungu lequmrhu labagcini nabahloli bee-akhawunti zemali, omele indawo yomqashi, esichaza imfuneko yokukuqasha kwaye esibonisa inkcazelo yezinto ozakuzenza kumsebenzi wakho.
Hambisa isiqinisekiso esenziwe ngumgcini nomhloli wee-akhawunti zemali olilungu lequmrhu labagcini nabahloli bee-akhawunti zemali, esichaza ukuba awuyikuqashwa phantsi kweemeko nemiqathango engaphantsi kwaleyo ibandakanyeka kubemi nabahlali, futhi sichaze ukuba unazo iikhwalifikheyshini ezisemthethweni ezifuneka kulo msebenzi.
Veza ubungqina bobhaliso kwiqumrhu lobuchule boqeqesho okanye kwibhodi yobuchule boqeqesho, ukubangaba oko kuyabandakanyeka.

Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Le nkonzo ithabatha ixesha elingagqithanga kwiintsuku ezingama 30.

Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo

Inkcazelo
IZatifiketi ezi-Orenji neziLuhlaza zisebenziseka kumthwalo wembewu ezithathwe kuwo, kodwa sona iSatifiketi esiBlu sisebenziseka kuphela kwibinza elifunyanelwe ukuvavanya.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Cela ukunikwa amanani agunyazisiweyo wemithwalo yembewu.
Lungisa imithwalo yembewu ukuze kukhiwe amabinza. Oku kubandakanya ukuphawula imithwalo ngamanani anikiweyo emithwalo. Inkonkxa nganye kufuneka iphawulwe (ifundeke ngokucacileyo) okanye incanyatheliswe iphetshana ekubhalwe kulo okuqulathiweyo nelichaza amanani anikiweyo embewu.
Xa imithwalo yembewu ilungele ukukhiwa kwamabinza, biza umphengululi azokukha ibinza.
Amabinza athunyelwa kwi-OSTS kwaye avavanyelwa umgangatho, kuze ke kukhutshwe isatifiketi esibandakanyekayo.
Hlawula umlinganiselo wentlawulo yokuvavanya imbewu. Kwakube kufunyenwe amabinza, kukhutshwa i-invoice. Nazi iinkcukacha zebhanki:
Yenza isicelo seSatifiketi esiLuhlaza ngencwadi ebhalelwe kwisihloko esigunyazisiweyo sombutho wakho, kuba akwenziwa ukuphawulwa komthwalo wembewu nokukhiwa kwebinza okugunyazisiweyo.
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
ISikhululo esiGunyazisiweyo sokuVavanya iMbewu sibeka phambili ukuvavanywa kwamabinza embewu alungiselelwe ukuthunyelwa kumazwe angaphandle. Iintlobo-ntlobo ezahlukeneyo zeemveliso zezityalo zivavanyelwa phantsi kweemeko ezahlukeneyo kwaye ixesha elithatyathwa luvavanyo lungahluka ukusukela kwiintsuku ezimbalwa ukuya kutsho kwiiveki ezimbalwa.
I-OSTS iyazama ukuntshulisa amabinza embewu kumthwalo omnye phantsi kweemeko zokuvavanya ezifanayo. Kwakhona, iindidi ezahlukeneyo zovavanyo zingacelwa yiklayenti. Ngoko ke, akukho nkcazelo inganikwa malunga nomgangatho wenkonzo ofikelelwayo. Buza kwiziko ngokwalo (jonga iinkcukacha zonxulumano).

Iinkonzo zabantu
Inkcazelo
I-learnership (ukufundela umsebenzi) yinkqubo yokufunda ekhokelela kwisiqinisekiso solwazi lomsebenzi. Ii-Learnership zibandakanya ukufunda kwigumbi lokufundela, kwiziko loqeqesho okanye kwikholeji, kunye nokuqeqeshelwa emsebenzini ngqo kwindawo yokusebenza. Ukuze uthabathe inxaxheba kwi-learnership, umqeshi kufuneka avume kwaye abenako ukunika i-learnership.
Ngubani ongenza isicelo?
Nabani na ogqibe esikolweni, kwikholeji okanye eyunivesiti kwaye ongasebenziyo. Abantu abangasebenziyo kufuneka babhalise njengabantu abafuna umsebenzi kwiSebe leZabasebenzi.
Ubude be-learnership buxhomekeka kwicandelo ngecandelo, kodwa budla ngokungabi ngaphantsi konyaka omnye.
Ukuze ufumane inkcazelo ebanzi, yiya kwiSebe leZabasebenzi.
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Cinga ngohlobo loqeqesho nomsebenzi owufunayo. Ngamanye amazwi, ukubangaba uthanda ukuba phandle, ungenzi sicelo somsebenzi wase-ofisini.
Zoba i-CV eneenkcukacha zobuqu ezifana nezi zilandelayo:
Igama lakho kunye nomhla wakho wokuzalwa
Imfundo; isikolo ofunde kuso kunye neziqinisekiso zemfundo
Amava omsebenzi; amagama abaqeshi bangaphambili nomsebenzi owawuwenza.
Ezinye izakhono ezifana nezakhono zekhompyutha; ingaba unelayisensi yokuqhuba na, njalo-njalo.
Abantu abakwaziyo (amagama kunye neenkcukacha zokunxulumana zabantu abakwazi kakuhle ngokwasemsebenzini okanye ngokwasemfundweni)
Bhalisa njengomntu ofuna umsebenzi kwiziko lezabasebenzi elikufuphi kuwe. Oku kuya kunceda ekubeni abaqeshi bakufumane xa befuna ukuqalisa i-learnership.
Cela abahlobo nosapho bakujongele izithuba kwaye ujonge nezaziso kumaphephandaba.
Mana uvela kwiziko lezabasebenzi kwaye ulungise iinkcukacha zakho xa zitshintshile.
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Ubude benkqubo yee-learnership abufani, kodwa budla ngokungabi ngaphantsi konyaka omnye.
Iindleko
Le nkonzo ayihlawulelwa.
Yenza isicelo kwiSebe leZabasebenzi okanye kwiziko lezabasebenzi elikufuphi kuwe.

Ukumka eMzantsi Afrika
IiNkonzo zamazwe angaphandle
Ukumisa ngokusemthethweni amaxwebhu asemthethweni kunye neziqinisekiso zomsebenzisi wokugqibela
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Okokuqala, qonda ukuba loluphi uxwebhu ofuna ukulumisa ngokusemthethweni.
ICandelo lokuMisa ngokuseMthethweni lingakhupha isigunyaziso esifanelekileyo okanye isiQinisekiso seApostille ngokwale migaqo ilandelayo:
Uxwebhu olo alukho ngaphezu konyaka ubudala.
Kufuneka ulicebise iCandelo lokuMisa ngokusemThethweni malunga nelizwe apho luya kusetyenziswa khona olo xwebhu, ukuze libe nakho ukufumanisa ukuba kufuneka iApostille okanye isiQinisekiso soGunyaziso na.
Phambi kokuba iCandelo lokuMisa ngokuseMthethweni likhuphe isiGunyaziso okanye isiQinisekiso seApostlle esifanelekileyo, olo xwebhu kufuneka lumiswe ngokomthethweni:
nguMantyi, uMantyi owoNgezelelweyo okanye uMantyi oNcedisayo nguMgcini-zincwadi okanye uMgcini-zincwadi oNcedisayo weNkundla ePhezulu yoMzantsi Afrika.
Makungeniswe amaxwebhu kwiCandelo lokuMisa ngokusemThethweni ngokusebenzisa enye yezi ndlela zilandelayo:
Asiwe ngumntu - Amaxwebhu angeniswe ngumntu angalandwa kuphela xa kukho ubungqina bokwamkelwa. Isiqinisekiso sokwamkelwa sinikwa wena emva kokunikezela amaxwebhu akho.
Asiwe sisigidimi - Isigidimi siya kunikwa iphetshana lokuza kulanda, eliya kufunwa xa kulandwa amaxwebhu. Kufuneka usihlawule isigidimi xa sibuyisela amaxwebhu akho.
Athunyelwe ngeposi ebhalisiweyo okanye ekhawulezayo - Kufuneka ufake imvulophu ebhalwe igama nedilesi yakho, ehlawulelweyo (akwamkelwa mali) nebukhulu bayo buyi-A4 ukuze iCandelo lokuMisa ngokusemThethweni likwazi ukuwabuyisa amaxwebhu. Ileta esisiqinisekiso, exela inani lamaxwebhu afuna ukumiswa ngokwasemthethweni, ilizwe ekufunelwa lona oku, kwakunye neenkcukacha zakho ezipheleleyo, kufuneka ihanjiswe kunye namaxwebhu.
Amaxwebhu afinyeziweyo okanye okubhalwe ngekhompyutha
Iikopi eziqinisekisiweyo zomtshato, zokuzalwa, zokufa okanye iziqinisekiso ezikhululayo zasemapoliseni
Iikopi eziqinisekisiweyo zeziqinisekiso zoBume boMtshato (akukho sithintelo) okanye ubuNgqina bobuZwe
Iikopi eziqinisekisiweyo zamaxwebhu okundwendwela okanye iincwadi zezazisi
Amaxwebhu aqinisekiswe ngabaKhomishinala beziFungo ukuba ziikopi zokwenyani zamaxwebhu akuqala. Umntu wasebuRhulumenteni onesiGunyaziso sokusayina kufuneka aqinisekise. 
La maxwebhu alandelayo akunyanzelekanga ukuba amiswe ngokusemthethweni yinkundla kuqala njengoko kuchaziwe ngentla apha, ngaphandle kokuba ebesayinwe ngumntu onegunya lokunikeza:
Iziqinisekiso ezingafinyezwanga okanye ezipheleleyo zokuzalwa, zomtshato kunye/okanye ezokufa kunye neeleta eziqinisekisa ubume bobuzwe bomntu, ezisayiniwe zagximfizwa isitampu ngumqeshwa ogunyazisiweyo weSebe lemiCimbi yezeKhaya.
Iimpepha zokuthathela kuwe umntwana umkhulise ezisayiniweyo zaze zagximfizwa isitampu nguMgcini-zincwadi wemicimbi yokuThathwa kwabantwana bakhuliswe ngabanye abazali kwiSebe lezoBulungisa.
Amaxwebhu okuthumela ngaphandle kwelizwe asayiniweyo aze agximfizwa isitampu yiNdlu yezoRhwebo.
Iziqinisekiso zokukhulula zamaPolisa ezisayinwe zagximfizwa isitampu liZiko leNgxelo yoLawphulo-mthetho leNkonzo yamaPolisa oMzantsi Afrika (isiqinisekiso sokuKhulula samaPolisa sisemthethweni kwithuba leenyanga ezintathu kuphela).
Ileta exela ukuba Akukho siThintelo (ileta yobume bomtshato) esayinwe yagximfizwa isitampu ngumqeshwa weSebe lemiCimbi yaseKhaya.
Iziqinisekiso zakwagqirha ezisayinwe zagximfizwa isitampu ligosa eligunyazisiweyo kwiBhunga lemiSebenzi yezeMpilo.
Amaxwebhu aphathelele kuthutho lwemfuyo, kuquka izilwanyana zasekhaya, kufuneka egximfizwe asayinwa nguGqirha weziLwanyana kaRhulumente.
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iiyure zikawonke-wonke zimi ngolu hlobo : ngoMvulo - ngoLwesihlanu, 08:30 - 12:30 (ngaphandle kweentsuku zeholide zikaRhulumente).
ICandelo lokuMisa ngoksemThethweni liya kunika isibhengezo sethuba leentsuku ezisixhenxe sokuvala xa olo suku ingelulo olweholide kaRhulumente.

Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
ibenobunikazi kwaye ilawulwe ngokupheleleyo ngumntu okanye abantu baseMzantsi Afrika, okanye ibenobunikazi kwaye ilawulwe ngokupheleleyo lilo naliphi na iqumrhu leenkampani, umbutho okanye naliphi na iqumrhu labantu elifakwe okanye elisekwe phantsi kwemithetho yeRiphabhlikhi yaseMzantsi Afrika, kwaye apho isininzi sezabelo kunye namalungelo okuvota alawulwa ngabantu baseMzantsi Afrika.
Inqanawa yokuloba yeli lizwe idla ngokuxhotyiselwa ukuloba kunye neminye imisebenzi eyayamene nokuloba. Le nqanawa ibandakanya zonke izixhobo eziyimfuneko, izixhobo zokuloba, iindawo zokugcina imithwalo, umthwalo okanye iimpahla zorhwebo kunye namafutha alayishwe kuyo. Inqanawa yokuloba yeli lizwe ingabandakanya nayiphi na inqanawa encedisa enye okanye ezinye iinqanawa eziselwandle ekwenzeni nawuphi na umsebenzi owayamene nokuloba. Oku kungabandakanya ezi zinto zilandelayo, kodwa kungapheleli kuzo kuphela:
amalungiselelo ukunika nokukhupha izinto eziyimfuneko indawo yokugcina imithwalo indawo yomkhenkce nokubandisa ukuthutha, okanye ukukhupha imveliso; kunye/okanye nokwenza ngqo imisebenzi yokuloba kuMmandla oKhethekileyo wezoQoqosho ekuthiwa yi-Exclusive Economic Zone (EEZ) okanye kumanzi olwandle lwehlabathi phantsi kweflegi yeRiphabhlikhi yaseMzantsi Afrika.
Akukho mntu unokusebenzisa inqanawa yokuloba okanye nayiphi na inqanawa ukuze asebenzise ilungelo lofikelelo, ngaphandle kokuba ikhutshiwe ilayisensi, enepemethe efanelekileyo ukubangaba umnikazi wenqanawa ngumntu onelungelo lokuloba. Kwimeko apho umnikazi wenqanawa engenalungelo lokuloba, kufuneka kubekho isivumelwano sekhontrakthi yokusebenzisa le nqanawa.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Inqanawa yokuloba kufuneka iyokuvavanyelwa ukufanelana nolwandle (yi-SAMSA) kwaye i-SAMSA ingakhupha iSatifiketi soKhuseleko.
Fumana ifom yesicelo kwiSebe lezokuSingqongileyo kunye noKhenketho.
Kufuneka ubengumntu onelungelo lokuloba (ube wasenza isicelo selungelo lokuloba waze walinikwa elo lungelo). Ukubangaba awunalungelo lokuloba elingumnikazi wenqanawa, thumela okanye bandakanya isivumelwano sekhontrakthi, osingenele nomnikazi wenqanawa ukuze usebenzise le nqanawa kuthethwa ngayo, xa ufaka isicelo selayisensi yenqanawa.
Thumela ifom yesicelo kwiSebe lezokuSingqongileyo kunye noKhenketho nale nkcazelo ilandelayo:
o igama lenqanawa o igama lomnikazi wale nqanawa o uhlobo lwamandla, ubude benqanawa o umlinganiselo wamandla e-injini kunye nomlinganiselo womthwalo ongalingana kule nqanawa o icandelo lokuloba ekujongwe ukuba le nqanawa isetyenziswe kulo o uMbuso weFlegi ebhaliswe phantsi kwawo xakungoku le nqanawa (ukubangaba iqeshwe okanye kuvunyelwene ngayo ngekhontrakthi noMntu waseMzantsi Afrika oneLungelo lokuLoba).
Zalisa le fom ngoonobumba abangadityaniswanga kwaye usebenzise oonobumba abakhulu kuphela, ufake nesiphakamiso esibhaliweyo esixhasa iimfuno zakho apho kuyimfuneko.
Bonisa ixesha eya kulichitha le nqanawa kunye nendlela eya kusetyenziswa ngayo kwicandelo lokuloba eya kusebenza kulo.
Entla
Entla

Isicelo singathabatha iintsuku zokusebenza ezi- 3, kuxhomekeke ekufakweni kwesicelo ngokufanelekileyo.

Izikhalazo
Isicelo sokufaka isikhalazo
Isicelo sokufaka isikhalazo sokungaphumeleli kweNkonzo yaMapolisa aseMzantsi Afrika ukunceda okanye ukukhusela amaxhoba obundlobongela basekhaya
Inkcazelo
Ukubamba ummangalelwa;
Ukunceda umkhalazi amangale, afumane indawo yokusithela efanelekileyo, afumane unyango, ukukhapha umkhalazi ayokuqokelela impahla yakhe kunye nokoxutha izixhobo eziyingozi kumxhaphazi;
Ukucebisa umkhalazi ngezinto angakhetha ukuzenza, okufana nokungaphumeleli ukucebisa umkhalazi afake ityala lobugebenga okanye enze isicelo somyalelo wokukhusela, okanye zombini ezi zinto kunye
Nokungakwazi ukubiza ummangalelwa ngomyalelo wokumnyanzela aye enkundleni.
Ubundlobongela basekhaya benzeka xa umntu obandakanyekana naye kubudlelwane basekhaya esenza ezi zinto zilandelayo:
Ekuxhaphaza ngokwasemzimbeni okanye ngokwesondo, umzekelo, akubethe okanye akudlwengule.
Ekuhlelele ngokukuhlupha, umzekelo, athi gqolo ukukutsalela umnxeba oku kucaphukisayo, akubhalele okanye athumele izinto kuwe, okanye agade iindlela zakho.
Engena kwakho ngaphandle kwemvume yakho.
Ekuxhaphaza ngokwezoqoqosho nangokwemali, umzekelo, xa indoda okanye isinqandamathe sinyanzelisa ukwenza zonke izigqibo ngemali okanye sisala ukuhlawulela ukutya, iimali zesikolo, njalo-njalo.
Ekugrogrisa, umzekelo, esoyikisa ngokukubulala xa ufuna ukuya emapoliseni.
Esonakalisa impahla yakho, umzekelo, etshisa impahla yakho yokunxiba, esophula ifenitshala okanye egqabhuza amatayari emoto yakho.
Esaphula umyalelo wokukhusela okhoyo nosebenzayo.
Eziphatha ngayo nayiphina indlela yokuxhaphaza ebeka esichengeni ukhuseleko lwakho, impilo yakho okanye intlalontle yakho.
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Nika i-ICD le nkcazelo ilandelayo:
Igama kunye neenkcukacha zokunxulumana nexhoba kunye nomkhalazi okanye zokunxulumana nomkhalazi.
Igama kunye nesikhundla sepolisa okanye samapolisa akrokrelwayo
Inombolo yetyala yamapolisa, ukuba ikhona
Iinkcukacha zamangqina, ukuba akhona.
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Ixesha lokulinda udliwano-ndlebe - imizuzu engama 30
Incwadi ebhaliweyo engqina ukuba isikhalazo sifunyenwe - kwisithuba seentsuku ezingama 30
Ingxelo yenkqubela - kwisithuba seentsuku ezingama 30
Ingxelo yokugqibela - kwisithuba seentsuku ezingama 90
