Izikhalazo
Isicelo sokufaka isikhalazo sezenzo ezigwenxa
Isicelo sokufaka isikhalazo sokuziphatha kakubi okanye sezenzo ezigwenxa zamalungu eNkonzo yaMapolisa aseMzantsi Afrika okanye eeNkonzo zaMapolisa kaMasipala
Inkcazelo
Isikhalazo soDidi III: Isikhalazo esityhola ukuba ipolisa okanye amapolisa abandakanyeka kwisenzo esigwenxa esikhokelele kulwenzakalo lomzimba olumasikizi oludinge unyango olungenisa isigulane esibhedlele. Oko kuziphatha kakubi okanye eso senzo sigwenxa kufuneka sibe senzeke ngexesha umntu eselugcinweni lwamapolisa. Le miba ilandelayo ludweliso lwezikhalazo zoDidi III:
Ukusebenzisa kakubi amandla okunochaphazelo olubonakalayo kubahlali malunga nolwenzakalo olwenziweyo, inani labantu abachaphazelekayo, ubungakanani bemali ebandakanyekayo, isithuba sexesha eyenzeke ngalo.
Ukutshisa ngabom
Ukubetha ngeenjongo zokulimaza umzimba kanobom, okanye ukuzama ukubulala
Ukuthwala okanye ukuba umntu
Ukuthintela inkqubo yomthetho
Ubuqhetseba
Ukuxoka uphantsi kwesifungo
Ubundlobongela esidlangalaleni
Ukugrogrisa
Ukuxhwila umntu (ngeenjongo zokuzuza into)
Ukonakalisa impahla (ipropati) ngabom
Ukuthabatha inxaxheba kumbutho wobugebenga.
Ukudlwengula
Ukwamkela impahla ebiweyo
Ukuphanga
Ubuqhophololo
Ukwabelana ngesondo kwendoda nenye indoda (Sodomy)
Ubusela
Ukungcungcuthekisa
Ukucudusela umntu ukuze akunike into
Ukuxhokonkxa, ukwenza iyelenqe okanye ukuzama ukwenza nasiphina isenzo esigwenxa kwezi zixelwe ngasentla
Isikhalazo soDidi IV: Isikhalazo esityhola ukuba ipolisa leNkonzo yaMapolisa aseMzantsi Afrika okanye ipolisa leeNkonzo zaMapolisa kaMasipala, libandakanyeke kwisenzo esigwenxa okanye kwisenzo sokuziphatha kakubi esingekhoyo kwezi zidweliswe ngasentla okanye esingakhokelelanga ekubhubheni komntu okanye ekulimaleni komzimba ngokumasikizi.
Isikhalazo soDidi V: isikhalazo esingaphandle komda womsebenzi okanye womgaqo we-ICD.
Izikhalazo zezehlo ezenzeke phambi kokusekwa kwe-ICD, oko kukuthi, zonke izehlo ezenzeke phambi kuka Epreli 1997. Nazo izehlo ezenzeke kwisithuba esingaphezulu konyaka phambi kokuba zixelwe kwi-ICD, ngaphandle kokuba kukho iimeko ezingaqhelekanga ezizodwa.
Ukuze ufumane inkcazelo ebanzi, yiya the ICandelo eliZimeleyo leZikhalazo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
I-ICD ingakucela ukuba unike inkcazelo eyongeziweyo phambi kokuba kuphandwe ngesikhalazo.
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Ukuqhubekiswa kwezikhalazo:
Ukwamkelwa kotyelelo lweklayenti kungathabatha imizuzu emihlanu.
Ixesha lokulinda udliwano-ndlebe nomsebenzi ojongene nezikhalazo okanye umcazululi, kungathabatha imizuzu engama 30.
Ukungqinwa kokufunyanwa kwesikhalazo ngencwadi ebhaliweyo kungathabatha iintsuku ezingama 30.
Ingxelo ngenkqubela yesikhalazo ingathabatha iintsuku ezingama 30
Ingxelo yokugqibela ingathabatha iintsuku ezingama 90

Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Nika i-ICD le nkcazelo ilandelayo:
Igama kunye neenkcukacha zokunxulumana nexhoba kunye nomkhalazi okanye zokunxulumana nomkhalazi.
Igama kunye nesikhundla sepolisa elikrokrelwayo.
Igama lesikhululo samapolisa okanye umasipala apho ipolisa elikrokrelwayo lisebenza khona.
Inombolo yetyala yamapolisa, ukuba ikhona.
Umhla, ixesha kunye nohlobo lokungakwazi ukunceda ixhoba.
Iinkcukacha zamangqina, ukuba akhona.
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Uphando lungathabatha iintsuku ezingama 30 okanye nangaphezulu, kuxhomekeke kubunzulu betyala.
Ukukhutshwa kweengxelo zokugqibela zentshayelelo kungathabatha iintsuku ezingama 180.
Zonke iingxelo ezifakwe kuvimba wenkcazelo zingathabatha iiyure ezingama 48.
Ukukhutshwa kweengxelo zokugqibela zeziphakamiso kungathabatha iintsuku ezili 14 emva kokufunyanwa kweengxelo zobuchule.

Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
ukunabisa umba 'wofikelelo' ukusukela kwilungelo lokufumana inkcazelo ukuya kutsho ekubandakanyeni ufikelelo olwandileyo kwizinto neendlela zemveliso yosasazo.
Ilungelo lenkululeko yamaphephandaba kunye nezinye iinkonzo zosasazo lweendaba, inkululeko yokufumana nokukhupha inkcazelo kunye nemibono, inkululeko yemveliso enobugcisa kunye nenkululeko yemfundo, kunye nenkululeko yophando lwenzululwazi.
ngokwembono yophuhliso, umba wokulingana ubalulekile ekulungelelaniseni amacandelo okudlala indima kwishishini losasazo, ngokukhuthaza abangeni abatsha kule marike.
ILayisensi yoSasazo lweZandi olukhupha imitha yaMandla akwizinga eliPhantsi inganikwa kula macandelo alandelayo:
Iinkonzo zorhwebo zosasazo lwezandi ezikhupha imitha yamandla akwizinga eliphantsi - iinkonzo ezisebenzela, kwaye ezisasazela, kwimimandla emikhulu yoobhazabhaza beevenkile okanye kumaziko eevenkile, kumabala emidlalo, kumabala emiboniso kunye nakumaqonga emiboniso yeebhanyabhanya okanye nayiphina inkonzo efana nezi iGunya elingayibona ifanelekile.
Iinkonzo zoluntu zosasazo lwezandi ezikhupha imitha yamandla akwizinga eliphantsi - iinkonzo ezisebenzela, kwaye ezisasaza, kumakhaya wabantu abadala, unxulumano phakathi kweendawo zokunqula, unxibelelwano phakathi kweendawo zokunqula namakhaya wabantu abadala, okanye nayiphina enye inkonzo efana nezi iGunya elingayibona ifanelekile.
Iilayisensi zabahlali kunye nezorhwebo, zosasazo lwezandi olukhupha imitha yamandla akwizinga eliphantsi, ziya kusebenziseka iminyaka emithathu kwaye ilayisensi yosasazo lwezandi ekhupha imitha yamandla ekwizinga eliphantsi yezenzeko zexeshana iya kusebenziseka iintsuku ezingamashumi amathathu.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Chonga intshukumo efanelekileyo yamaza okusetyenziswa kwemitha yamandla akwizinga eliphantsi.
Seka itim (iqela) yabantu abasebenza ngesicelo ukuze le tim ithabathe uxanduva lwenkqubo yesicelo kwaye ibengumenzi-sicelo egameni labaququzeleli bezenzeko.
Qinisekisa ukuba le tim yenza ezi zinto zilandelayo:
Ibhala isicwangciso seshishini
Iphembelela ukonyulwa kwamalungu eBhodi ngenkqubo yedemokhrasi.
Cela ikopi yenkonzo yosasazo kunye nefom yesicelo sokuhambisa iintshukumiso zemitha yosasazo.

Umntu ovelisa, akhe, aguqule okanye angenise iimoto zangaphandle eMzantsi Afrika ngenjongo zorhwebo, okanye ukuthengisa kufuneka abhalise KwiCandelo leZothutho.

Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Dibana neCandelo leZothutho kwiphondo lakho.
o ikopi eqinisekisiweyo yencwadi yesazisi o ikopi eqinisekisiweyo yesatifiketi soshishino o incwadi yelungelo lokumela xa umele inkampani o inani lengqokelela lomthetho wekxaso ophuma kuNcedo laBabuti beRhafu eMzantsi Afrika, xa ungenisa impahla yangaphandle eMzantsi Afrika o isatifiketi esisusa ukuthandabuzeka kwemoto esiphuma kuNcedo laMapolisa ase Mzantsi Afrika.

Ukungena eMzantsi Afrika
Ukufika eMzantsi Afrika
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Ipemethe yokufumana unyango inikwa umntu welizwe langaphandle oneenjongo zokufumana unyango eMzantsi Afrika. Loo pemethe yonyango ihlala isebenziseka iinyanga eziphelela kwisithandathu ngexesha. Yenza isicelo sepemethe yotshintshiselwano kwindlu yozakuzo yaseMzantsi Afrika okanye kwiziko elimele uMzantsi Afrika elikufuphi kuwe.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Hambisa ipaspoti yakho ekufuneka ibe iyasebenziseka iintsuku ezingekho ngaphantsi kwama 30 emva kokuphelelwa kotyelelo olucetywayo.
Hambisa ubungqina bokubanako ngokwemali ukuze umelane nezidingo zemihla ngemihla zabo bonke abantu abakhapha umntu onepemethe yonyango (ukuba bakhona), ngokwezitetimenti, iimpepha ezibonisa umvuzo, ukuba zikhona, okanye iitshekhi zabahambi.
Hambisa incwadi evela kwingcaphephe yezonyango okanye kwiziko lezonyango, ebonisa izizathu okanye imfuneko yonyango, ixesha ekulindeleke ukuba lithatyathwe lunyango kunye neenkcukacha zezicwangciso zokunyangwa eMzantsi Afrika.
Khupha omnye okanye nangaphezulu koko, kule miqulu ilandelayo, ikhaphe isicelo sakho sepemethe:
o isatifiketi sonyango esipheleleyo o isatifiketi sokuzalwa esipheleleyo o isatifiketi somtshato esipheleleyo (ukuba siyabandakanyeka)
o incwadi ebhaliweyo nefungelweyo ekuthiwa yi-affidavit BI-1712A ukubangaba kubandakanyeka ubudlelwane bobulingane obungengomtshato, ihambe nobungqina bokuhlalisana o isivumelwano esizotywe ngumntu oqeqeshelwe ukwenza njalo ngokomthetho, kwiimeko zokuhlalisana o ubungqina bomtshato wesintu, ukubangaba oko kuyabandakanyeka o umyalelo woqhawulo-mtshato, ukubangaba oko kuyabandakanyeka o ubungqina bomyalelo wenkundla onika ilungelo lokugcina abantwana, ukubangaba oko kuyabandakanyeka o isatifiketi sokubhubha, ngokuphathelelene nomlingane ongasekhoyo, ukubangaba oko kuyabandakanyeka o imvume ebhaliweyo esuka kubo bobabini abazali, okanye kumzali omnye onguye yedwa ogcina abantwana, ukuba oko kuyabandakanyeka, ihambe nobungqina bokubanguye yedwa ogcina abantwana o ubungqina bokwamkelwa komntwana ngumntu ongamzelanga ibengowakhe (adoption) ngokwasemthethweni, ukuba oko kuyabandakanyeka o umyalelo wokwahlukana ngokwasemthethweni, ukuba oko kuyabandakanyeka o isatifiketi esiphuma emapoliseni esiqinisekisa ubume obumsulwa, ukubangaba wena, menzi-sicelo, uneminyaka yobudala engama 21 nangaphezulu, ngokuphathelelene nawo onke amazwe ohleli kuwo unyaka okanye ngaphezulu konyaka o isatifiketi sokugonywa, ukuba oko kuyabandakanyeka.
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Izicelo zingathabatha ixesha elifikelela kwiintsuku ezingama 30.

Inkcazelo
Ilungelo lokwemba umgodi yimvume enikwa nguMbuso ngokweSebe leZimbiwa naMandla, ekunika igunya lokwemba izimbiwa emgodini kummandla othile.
Esi simbiwa singembiwa ngokugqibeleleyo
Umenzi-sicelo unayo imali kunye nobuchule bokwemba esi simbiwa ngokugqibeleleyo,
Isicwangciso sokuxhasa ngemali siyangqinelana nale nkqubo yokwembiwa komgodi kunye nexesha elizakuthatyathwa yile nkqubo.
Umenzi-sicelo wenze amalungiselelo ezemali kunye namanye amalungiselelo esicwangciso esichaziweyo sentlalo nesabasebenzi.
Ukuze ufumane inkcazelo ebanzi, yiya kwiSebe leZimbiwa naMandla.
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Yenza isicelo kwi-ofisi yoManejala weNgingqi weSebe leZimbiwa naMandla okwingingqi omi kuyo lo mhlaba.
Le fom kufuneka ikhatshwe yintlawulo yesicelo engabuyiswayo njengoko ichazwe nguManejala weNgingqi.
Uthumele isicwangciso senkqubo yokulawula imo yokusingqongileyo ukuze ivunywe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
UManejala weNgingqi uyakukwazisa ngencwadi ebhaliweyo ukubangaba isicelo samkelwe, oku kuthetha ukuba isicelo sakho sihambisene nazo zonke iimfuneko, kwisithuba seentsuku ezili 14 esifumene isicelo, kwaye akuyalele ukuba ubonisane nomnikazi-mhlaba, umntu ohlala kulo mhlaba, ndawonye nabo bonke abanye ababandakanyeki abachaphazelekayo.
Ukubangaba uMphathiswa uyala ukukhupha ilungelo lokwemba umgodi, kufuneka akwazise, kwisithuba seentsuku ezingama 30, kwaye achaze izizathu zokwala esi sicelo.
Iindleko
Iindleko ziya kuqulunqwa lisebe kwaye azibuyiswa.

Inkcazelo
esi simbiwa sibandakanyekayo singembiwa ngokugqibeleleyo iminyaka emibini ummandla womgodi awudluli kwi- 1.5mÂ² yobungakanani akukho mntu ungomnye onelungelo lokukhangela ubukho besimbiwa, ilungelo lokwemba umgodi, ipemethe yokwemba umgodi okanye ipemethe yokugcina umgodi yesimbiwa esinye nomhlaba omnye.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Yenza isicelo kwi-ofisi yoManejala weNgingqi weSebe leZimbiwa naMandla okwingingqi omi kuyo lo mhlaba.
Sakuba sivunyiwe isicelo sakho, uManejala weNgingqi uyakukucela ukuba uthumele isicwangciso sokulawula imo yokusingqongileyo kwaye ubonisane nomnikazi-mhlaba kunye nomntu ohlala ngokusemthethweni kulo mhlaba, ndawonye nawuphina omnye umbandakanyeki ochaphazelekayo.
Thumela isiphumo soku kubonisana kuManejala kwisithuba seentsuku ezingama- 30.
Entla
Entla

Ukuxela umntu olahlekileyo
Ukuxela umntu olahlekileyo
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Le nkonzo yenzelwe ukuba uluntu lukwazi ukuxela umntu olahlekileyo. Ungamxela umntu olahlekileyo kwangoko wakube ukrokrela ukuba kukho into embi eyenzekileyo kulo mntu.
Akukho xesha limisiweyo lokulinda phambi kokuba umxele umntu olahlekileyo. Ukubanga ipolisa likuxelela ngenye indlela, thetha nelinye igosa elingentla ngesikhundla kweli uthetha nalo,uqhubeka wenze njalo ude ufumane uncedo oluyimfuneko. Ukuze ufumane inkcazelo ngabantwana abalahlekileyo, yiya kwiZiko lase Mzantsi Afrika laBantwana abalahlekileyo (South African Centre for Missing Children).
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ukubangaba ukrokrela ukuba umntu ulahlekile, zama ukunxulumana naye kuqala.
Nika inkcazelo esisiseko ngalo mntu, kulicebo elihle ukukhupha ifoto esandul'ukufotwa.
Ukubangaba umntu olahlekileyo ufunyenwe, yiya kwesa sikhululo samapolisa bekuxelwe kuso ukulahleka kwalo mntu, wazise ipolisa okanye igosa eliphanda ngale nyewe.
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Ungamxela umntu olahlekileyo kuso nasiphina isikhululo samapolisa, akuyomfuneko ukuba ude uye kummandla apho lo mntu akrokreleka ukuba ulahlekele kuwo.

Inkcazelo
Olu ncedo lulungiselelwe abantu abavelisa iimoto, abenza iimoto,abathenga bathengise iimoto. Inanai lokurhweba ngeemoto linika imvume kwababantu babaliweyo yokuba baqhube endleleni kawonke-wonke iimoto ezingabhaliswanga.
abavelisi bemoto, bazise bathengise batshintshe okanye balungise iimoto abathuthi bemoto bahambise iimoto abarhwebi ngemoto ukuze bakwazi ukuhambisa iimoto nabathenga iimoto kwamanye amazwe ukuze bakwazi ukuzihambisa.

o ikopi yencwadi yesazisi okanye uxwebhu lelungelo lokumela xa umele inkampani o isatifiketi sokubhaliswa kweshishini

Inkcazelo
I-Nedlac kufuneka ixelelwe ngeli nyathelo ngefom eqingqiweyo (i-LRA 4.5). Kufuneka kuchazwe kule fom izizathu kunye nohlobo lwenyathelo elicetywayo. Oku akubandakanyi umhla wenyathelo elicetywayo, njengoko oku kungasingela phantsi inkqubo yokuzama ukufikelela kwimvisiswano.
Ukubangaba iinzame zokusombulula aziphumelelanga, umbutho wabasebenzi okanye imanyano yemibutho yabasebenzi kufuneka inike i-Nedlac isaziso sesibini esiyixelela ngeenjongo zayo zokuqhubeka ngenyathelo loqhankqalazo. Esi saziso sesibini kufuneka sisiwe kwi-Nedlac okungenani kwiintsuku ezili- 14 phambi kokuba liqalise inyathelo lokuqhankqalaza.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Yazisa i-Nedlac ngeenjongo zombutho wabasebenzi zokuqhubeka ngenyathelo lokuqhankqalaza.
Unobhala wombutho wabasebenzi okanye wemanyano yemibutho yabasebenzi kufanele azalise ifom yesicelo.
Thumela ifom ezalisiweyo kule dilesi ilandelayo:

Isaziso sokutshintsha komnini moto okanye ukuthengiswa kwemoto
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Oku kukunika isaziso kwabasemaguyeni kubhaliso lwemoto, sokutshintsha kobunini moto okanye uphatho lwamaxwebhu amalungelo. Isaziso kufuneka sithunyelwe kwabase magunyeni kubhaliso lwemoto kungaphelanga intsuku ezingamashumi amabini nanye, ukusukela ngosuku lokwenziwa kotshintsho.
Abaphathi baxwebhu amalungelo(njengee bhanki okanye amaziko asebenza ngemali) okanye abanini moto kufuneka batyikitye isatifiketi esitsha sobhaliso basinikezele kumphathi woxwebhu lamalungelo okanye umnini omtsha wemoto.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
o isatifiketi sobhaliso lwemoto o icwe-cwe lephepha-mvume elisemthethweni o incwadi yesaziso.
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Isicelo siqulunqwa kwangolo suku lwesicelo.
Entla
Iindleko
Le nkonzo ayihlawulelwa. 
Entla
Ifomu lesaziso sokutshintsha kobunini moto okanye ukuthengiswa kwemoto lifumaneka kwi ofisi yamagosa endlela.

Iinkonzo zemibutho
Isicelo sepemethe yokuseka indawo yokwenza imveliso yeentlanzi
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Indawo yokwenza imveliso yeentlanzi, ebizwa ngokuba yi-fish processing establishment (FPE), sisithuthi, inqanawa, iziko neendawo ezilingqongileyo okanye indawo apho into ethile okanye imveliso ethile yenziwa kwintlanzi. Le mveliso ingenziwa nangayiphi na indlela, efana nokunqunqa, ukusikelela, ukwaba amalungu athile, ukucoca, ukupakisha, ukukrozisa kunye nokugcina intlanzi. Eli ziko likwabandakanya indawo yokufaka intlanzi etotini, ukuyipakisha, ukuyomisa, ukuyiqhola ngetyiwa, ukuyifaka emkhenkceni, ukuyibandisa, ukuyiqinisa ngomkhenkce okanye ukwenza imveliso yayo ukuze ithengiswe eMzantsi Afrika okanye kumazwe angaphandle.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Yenza isicelo selungelo lokuloba kuphela xa kukho isimemo, esiya kupapashwa kwiGazethi kaRhulumente.
Fumana ifom yesicelo kwiSebe lezokuSingqongileyo kunye noKhenketho okanye kwiziko lokwamkela okanye lokukhupha iifom eliya kupapashwa liSebe lezokuSingqongileyo kunye noKhenketho.
Sifunde ngocoselelo futhi uyiqonde yonke into ekwisicelo, kwaye uqinisekise ukuba uyazanelisa iimfuneko kunye nemiqathango yesicelo.
Inkqubo yovavanyo iya kuqalisa emva komhla wokuvalelwa kwezicelo kwaye iziphumo ziya kupapashwa ngembalelwano yi-DEA&T. Ukubangaba unikwe ilungelo le-FPE (indawo yokwenza imveliso yeentlanzi) , kufuneka wenze isicelo sepemethe yokuqhuba i-FPE kwaye wanelise iimfuno phambi kokuba unikwe ipemethe.
Kwiimeko ezikhethekileyo nezizodwa. ungaqwalaselwa umnyenyevu wokungafunwa ndawo yokwenza imveliso yeentlanzi, ngokubona koMphathiswa weSebe lezokuSingqongileyo kunye noKhenketho.
Ukubangaba unikwe umnyenyevu wale ndawo yokwenza imveliso yeentlanzi, kufuneka usenze sona isicelo sepemethe yokuqhuba indawo yokwenza imveliso yeentlanzi.
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Isicelo selungelo le-FPE (lendawo yokwenza imveliso yeentlanzi) singathabatha inyanga enye ukuya kutsho kwiinyanga ezi- 3, ngokuqwalasela ubungakanani bezicelo. Ipemethe yokuqhuba indawo yokwenza imveliso ingathabatha usuku olunye okanye iintsuku ezingaphezulu kwesinye, kuxhomekeke ekufakweni kwesicelo ngokufanelekileyo.
Entla
Iindleko
Iimali ezihlawulwayo ziqwalaselwa ngokutsha okanye ziqulungqwa ngonyaka nguMphathiswa okanye ngugunyaziwe onikwe amandla okwenza njalo, ngokusebenzisana noMphathiswa wezeMali.
R6 000 - Isicelo selungelo lendawo yokwenza imveliso yeentlanzi okanye ilungelo lokuloba: ukuze uqhube indawo yokwenza imveliso yeentlanzi.
R1 330, kongezwe i-R125 yentlawulo yesicelo- Isicelo sepemethe yokuloba: ukuze uqhube indawo yokwenza imveliso yeentlanzi.

INcwadi yokubuyisa yokuhlawula irhafu yokubambisa
Incwadi yokubuyisa yokuhlawula irhafu yokubambisa - intlawulo yokuqala
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Xa umntu engenelwa yimali erhafelekayo engaxhuzulelwayo ngokwe-SITE okanye i-PAYE (umzekelo inzala, irenti okanye ingeniso yeshishini), kufanele ahlawule irhafu yokubambisa kule ngeniso-mali. Iintlawulo zerhafu yokubambisa zenziwa ngokweenyanga ezintandathu.
Irhafu yokubambisa yenzelwe ukunceda abarhafi bamelane noxanduva lwabo lwerhafu ngokuqhubekayo, endaweni yokuba bahlawule iimali ezinkulu kubekanye ngonyaka xa bevavanywa. Intlawulo yerhafu yokubambisa iyakungqamaniswa nerhafu yengeniso-mali yokugqibela (irhafu yesiqhelo) ekufanele umntu ayihlawule kuloo nyaka wovavanyo ubandakanyekayo.
Umhla wokungena kwentlawulo yerhafu yokubambisa kwixesha lokuqala ukwisithuba seenyanga ezintandathu ukusukela ekuqaleni konyaka wovavanyo. Intlawulo yokuqala yerhafu yokubambisa kufuneka imele isiqingatha soxanduva lokuhlawula irhafu kunyaka opheleleyo werhafu.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Bala irhafu yokubambisa ngolu hlobo lulandelayo kwixesha lesibini:
o isiqingatha serhafu epheleleyo yonyaka opheleleyo o uthabathe irhafu yomqeshwa exhuzulelwe eli xesha (iinyanga ezi 6)
Iinkcukacha zokubhankisha:
Okuya kufuneka koku kulandelayo:
uxwebhu lweSazisi salowo wenzelwa iinkonzo (beneficiary ID) okanye inombolo ye-akhawunti eqhagamshelaniswe nohlobo oluthe ngqo lwerhafu ukulungiselela intlawulo.

INcwadi yokuBuyisa yentlawulo yesibini yerhafu yokubambisa
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Xa umntu engenelwa yimali erhafelekayo engaxhuzulelwayo ngokwe-SITE okanye i-PAYE (umzekelo inzala, irenti okanye ingeniso yeshishini), kufanele ahlawule irhafu yokubambisa kule ngeniso-mali. Iintlawulo zerhafu yokubambisa zenziwa ngokweenyanga ezintandathu.
Irhafu yokubambisa yenzelwe ukunceda abarhafi bamelane noxanduva lwabo lwerhafu ngokuqhubekayo, endaweni yokuba bahlawule iimali ezinkulu kubekanye ngonyaka xa bevavanywa. Intlawulo yerhafu yokubambisa iyakungqamaniswa nerhafu yengeniso-mali yokugqibela (irhafu yesiqhelo) ekufanele umntu ayihlawule kuloo nyaka wovavanyo ubandakanyekayo.
Umhla wokungena kwentlawulo yerhafu yesibini yokubambisa awudluli kumhla wokugqibela wonyaka wokuvavanywa okanye umhla ovunyiweyo wokuphela konyaka-mali.
Qaphela: (kubhekiswa kuphela kubantu nakumaqumrhu ethrasti)
Xa ngaba uphelo lonyaka-mali wangoFebhruwari lunobunzima ngokwezemali yaye kufunyenwe imvume kwi-SARS yokusa iingxelo zemali ngomhla ongenguwo owokuphela kukaFebhruwari, abo bantu bangaphinda bacele imvume yokusa iincwadi zokubuyisa zerhafu yokubambisa ngokuhambisana nokuphela konyaka-mali ovunyiweyo. Nangona kunjalo, zonke ezinye iingeniso-mali zihlala zikulo nyaka wovavanyo ophela ngomhla wama 28/29 Febhruwari.
Bala irhafu yokubambisa ngolu hlobo lulandelayo kwixesha lesibini:
irhafu eqikelelwayo iyonke kunyaka opheleleyo uthabathe irhafu yomqeshwa ehlawulwa kunyaka opheleleyo uthabathe naziphina iikhredithi zerhafu yangaphandle zonyaka opheleleyo uthabathe imali ehlawulwe kwixesha lokuqala.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Xa iintlawulo zenziwe nge-posi, ngokusebenzisa ibhanki okanye i-ATM, ixesha elaneleyo lokuthumela ngeposi okanye lokusebenzisa le nkqubo, malithathelwe ingqalelo.
Iinkcukacha zokubhankisha:
Okuya kufuneka koku kulandelayo:
uxwebhu lweSazisi salowo wenzelwa iinkonzo (beneficiary ID) okanye inombolo ye-akhawunti eqhagamshelaniswe nohlobo oluthe ngqo lwerhafu ukulungiselela intlawulo.
Ukuba usuku lokugqibela lentlawulo liwela kumhla weholide yomntu wonke (public holiday) okanye kwimpela-veki, intlawulo mayenziwe ngosuku lokugqibela lokusebenza phambi komhla weholide yomntu wonke okanye phambi komhla weholide yomntu wonke okanye kwempelaveki.
Qaphela:
Intlawulo yesibini yerhafu yokubambisa kufanele isekelwe kwingeniso-mali erhafelekayo eqikelelwayo elingana nemali esisiseko okanye imali esekelwe kwingeniso-mali yakho eyiyo nqo erhafekelayo kuloo nyaka.

Indawo yokuhlala
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Le nkqubo iphembelela abazuzi baseke umbutho wenkxaso kwezezindlu oyakubancedisa ngokuququzelela ulwakhiwo, ngokobuchwepheshe nangokweenkqubo zokuphathwa nokulawulwa kwenkqubo yezindlu. Olu ncediso lubandakanya uqeqesho nezikhokelo kubazuzi ukuze bazakhele izindlu zabo.
Le ndlela yokuzikhethela ifumaneka kubazuzi ngokusekelwe kwiprojekthi, ngokwenkqubo yesabhsidi yesongezelelo sokuqinisa, yamaziko kunye nenxulumene neprojekthi. Ngaphezu koko, iyafumaneka kwimimandla yasezilalini apho abantu banamalungelo emiqathango yosetyenziso kuphela kumhlaba abahleli kuwo.
Isebenza njani iNkqubo yaBantu yezeZindlu?
Le nkqubo ikuvumela ukuba usebenzise uncediso lwesabhsidi ukuze uzakhele indlu yakho. Njengoko uncediso lobuchwepheshe lungundoqo kule nkqubo, wonke umntu othabatha inxaxheba kule nkqubo kudingeka ukuba abenombutho wenkxaso. Lo mbutho unika inkxaso yobuchwepheshe ukuze uqinisekise ukuba indlu yakhiwa ngokufanelekileyo.
Abantu abazakhela izindlu zabo ngokwabo okanye abaququzelela ukwakhiwa kwezindlu zabo, bangakha izindlu ezinkulu ngemali encinane.
Inkqubo yaBantu yezeZindlu ikuvumela ukuba:
wonge iindleko zabasebenzi ngokwenza omnye umsebenzi wokwakha ngokwakho okanye ngokuncediswa yifemeli yakho, abamelwane, abahlobo kunye nabanye abantu ukuze bakuncede usinde ekubeni uhlawule inzuzo (iprofiti) kubaphuhlisi bemihlaba, kwaye uthabathe ezona zigqibo zingcono kakhulu.
Ukuze uvumeleke ungene kule nkqubo, kufuneka:
Ube utshatile okanye uhlalisana nomnye umntu, okanye kufuneka kubekho abantu abaxhomeke kuwe ngokwemali.
Ukwazi ngokwasemthethweni ukungenela isivumelwano sekhontrakthi. Oko kukuthi, kufuneka ubengaphezulu kwama 21 eminyaka yobudala okanye ube utshatile kwaye kufuneka ubesengqondweni efanelekileyo.
Ube zange ngaphambili wafumana uncediso lwesabhsidi kuRhulumente yokuthenga indlu.
Qaphela ukuba kufuneka ungene kwisivumelwano sekhontrakthi nombutho wenkxaso oliqumrhu elisemthethweni. Lo mbutho wenkxaso uyakukuncedisa ngokobuchwepheshe nangokweenkqubo zokuphatha nokulawula.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe nxulumana neSebe lezeZindlu kwiPhondo khupha iNcwadi yeSazisi yakho, eyomlingane wakho kunye nezabantwana khupha ikopi yencwadi ebonisa umvuzo wakho okanye ubungqina bemali oyamkelayo.
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Isicelo siqhubekiswa ngamasebe ezindlu kumaphondo. Ixesha elithatyathwayo ukuze kuziswe le nkonzo lixhomekeka kwimeko ngemeko.

Iindleko
Inkcazelo
IPolisa eliNgesosigxina elikuDidi A - Kwiinkqubo zemisebenzi yobupolisa:
o eli polisa lisebenza kuyo yonke imiba yeenkqubo zemisebenzi yobupolisa nokuba kukwinqanaba lasesikhululweni samapolisa, elommandla okanye kwelephondo, kodwa ingeyiyo imisebenzi yobuchule obuthile o lingayinxiba iyunifom o liyakuqeqeshwa kwimiba efanelekileyo yeenkqubo zemisebenzi yobupolisa.
IPolisa eliNgesosigxina elikuDidi B - Kwiinkonzo zenkxaso:
o eli polisa lenza imisebenzi engqalileyo yenkxaso kwi-administreyshini kwinqanaba lelizwe, elephondo, elommandla okanye elesikhululo samapolisa, kwaye alinakusebenza kwiinkqubo zemisebenzi yobupolisa.
o alinxibi yunifom o xa kuyimfuneko, liyakuqeqeshwa kwimiba efanelekileyo yasemthethweni, yomgaqo kunye nemiyalelo ebandakanyeka kwimisebenzi engqamene nalo.
IPolisa eliNgesosigxina elikuDidi C-Imisebenzi yobupolisa enobuchule obuthile:
o liyakwenza imisebenzi engqalileyo kwicandelo lalo lobuchule bobungcaphephe o ngemvume yenkumanda yalo, lingayinxiba iyunifom o kufuneka liqeqeshwe kwimiba efanelekileyo yasemthethweni, yomgaqo kunye nemiyalelo ebandakanyeka kwimisebenzi engqamene nalo.
o eli polisa lisebenza kwimiba yeenkqubo zemisebenzi eyayamene nobupolisa becandelo kwimimandla yasezilalini neyeedolophu kwicandelo elingqalileyo kwinqanaba lasesikhululweni samapolisa; liyakwenza imisebenzi kuphela kwimimandla echaziweyo kwicandelo elingqalileyo ngokubona kwenkumanda o lingayinxiba iyunifom, kuxhomekeke kwindlela elisetyenziswa ngayo
Kufuneka liqeqeshwe kwimiba efanelekileyo yobupolisa becandelo kunye nakwinkqubo yemisebenzi okanye kwinkqubo yemisebenzi yobupolisa eyayamene nemisebenzi yalo. Kuyakufuneka uqeqesho olongezelelweyo ukubangaga libandakanyeka kwiinkqubo zemisebenzi yobupolisa becandelo.
Ipolisa elingesosigxina elityunjelwe kudidi oluthile lingatshintshelwa kulo naliphina olunye udidi ukubangaba liyahambisana nazo zonke iimfuneko zelo didi lingqalileyo kwaye liqeqeshiwe okanye lizimisele ukuya kuqeqesho olufunekayo kolo didi.
ubengumhlali osisigxina waseMzantsi Afrika ubeneminyaka eli 18 nangaphezulu ubudala, kwaye ubengaphantsi kweminyaka engama 70 ubudala ugcwalise uxwebhu lwemibuzo yempilo njengoko kuqulungqwe nguMkomishina weLizwe ungabinanto ethe gqwithi engqondweni, isifo okanye ubuthathaka obungaphazamisana nokwenza imisebenzi yakho ngokufanelekileyo ubengumntu oziphethe kakuhle, kwaye ke kuyakufuneka kufunyanwe imbali yakho yokuziphatha kakuhle ugqibe ngempumelelo uvavanyo lokusebenza kwengqondo oluqulungqwe nguMkomishina waMapolisa eLizweni okungenani ubene-senior certificate okanye iikhwalifikheyshini ezilingana naso kwaye unike ubungqina ngokwemiqulu kufuneka ukwazi ukuthetha, ukufunda nokubhala nge-English okungenani, njengelinye leelwimi ezigunyazisiweyo uvume ukunyatheliswa iminwe (iifingaprinti) kwaye ube awuzange wafunyaniswa unetyala lesenzo sobugebenga okanye awukho phantsi kotshutshiso ngesenzo sobugebenga uzimisele ukuya kuqeqeshwa uzimisele ukwenza isifungo sesikhundla ungabinemivambo ebonakalayo;kwaye ngokulicebo elihle, ubenelayisensi yokuqhuba, nangona nje ingeyomfuneko ekumele iqale ifezekiswe ngamapolisa angesosigxina phambi kokuba angenele lo msebenzi.

o isithembiso sokuzinikela (Isihlomelo C)
o uxwebhu lwemibuzo yempilo, (Isihlomelo E)
Imvume esuka kubazali bakho okanye kumlondolozi wakho (SAPS 30) ukubangaba uneminyaka yobudala engaphantsi kwama 21
Phatha le miqulu ilandelayo:
o ikopi eqinisekisiweyo yencwadi yakho yesazisi o ikopi eqinisekisiweyo yelayisensi yokuqhuba, ukuba unayo o iikopi eziqinisekisiweyo zeekhwalifikheyshini zakho zemfundo.
Umntu oyekisiweyo emsebenzini kumqashi wangaphambili ngenxa yobuthathaka bempilo
Umntu owayekade elilungu leNkonzo yaMapolisa aseMzantsi Afrika, esathi saliwa isicelo sakhe sokuphinda angene kule nkonzo umntu onomsebenzi othile okanye onesikhundla kwiqela lezopolitiko unondaba osisigxina okanye ummeli weenkonzo zosasazo lweendaba umfundi wesikolo unogada/igosa eliyisetyhorithi ilungu leNkonzo yaMapolisa kaMasipala.

Ukubangaba ufunyaniswe ufanelekile, isicelo sakho siyakuvunywa nguMkomishina woMmandla kwaye uyakufungiswa. Awuyikuvunyelwa wenze imisebenzi yobupolisa phambi kokuba ugqibe ngempumelelo uqeqesho lwakho. Emva koko ke, uyakunikwa isatifiketi esigunyazisiweyo sokufakwa emsebenzini.

Yenza isicelo sepemethe okanye selayisensi
Isicelo selungelo lokukhangela ubukho besimbiwa
Isicelo selungelo lokukhangela ubukho besimbiwa
Inkcazelo
Ilungelo lokukhangela ubukho besimbiwa liphepha lemvume (yipemethe) evumela inkampani okanye umntu othile ahlole okanye aphande ummandla womhlaba othile ngeenjongo zokuchonga isimbiwa esikhoyo ngokwenene okanye ekungenzeka ukuba sikhona. Nawuphi na umntu onqwenela  ukwenza isicelo selungelo lokukhangela ubukho besimbiwa kufuneka afake isicelo kwi-ofisi yoManejala weNgingqi okwingingqi omi kuyo lo mhlaba.
Ilungelo lokukhangela ubukho besimbiwa lisebenza iminyaka emihlanu, kodwa ke emva kokuphela kwale minyaka mihlanu, umenzi-sicelo angacela ukuvuselelwa kwelungelo lokukhangela ubukho besimbiwa, ithuba elingagqithanga kwiminyaka emithathu.
Ilungelo lokukhangela ubukho besimbiwa liya kunikwa ukubangaba ezi mfuneko zilandelayo zifezekisiwe:
Umenzi-sicelo unayo imali kunye nobuchule bokuqhuba ngokugqibeleleyo, oku kukhangelwa kupoposhwayo kobukho besimbiwa.
Isicwangciso sokuxhasa ngemali siyangqinelana nale nkqubo yokukhangela ubukho besimbiwa kunye nexesha elizakuthatyathwa yile nkqubo.
Akuyi kubakho ngcoliseko okanye monakalo ongamkelekanga kwimo yokusingqongileyo ngenxa yale nkqubo yokukhangela ubukho besimbiwa.
Ukuze ufumane inkcazelo ebanzi, yiya kwiSebe leZimbiwa naMandla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Yenza isicelo kwi-ofisi yoManejala weNgingqi weSebe leZimbiwa naMandla okwingingqi omi kuyo lo mhlaba.
Ukubangaba uManejala weNgingqi uyasamkela isicelo sakho, uyakukucela ukuba uthumele isicwangciso sokulawula imo yokusingqongileyo kwaye ubonisane nomnikazi-mhlaba, umntu ohlala ngokusemthethweni kulo mhlaba okanye nawuphina omnye umbandakanyeki ochaphazelekayo.
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Ukubangaba uManejala weNgingqi akasamkeli isicelo, kufanele akuxelele ngencwadi ebhaliweyo kwisithuba seentsuku ezili 14 kwaye asibuyisele kuwe esi sicelo.
Ukubangaba uManejala weNgingqi uyasamkela isicelo, kufuneka akuxelele kwisithuba seentsuku ezili 14 ukuba uthumele isicwangciso sokulawula imo yokusingqongileyo, kwaye ubonisane nomnikazi-mhlaba okanye umntu ohlala ngokusemthethweni kulo mhlaba, ndawonye nawuphina omnye umbandakanyeki ochaphazelekayo.
Kufuneka uthumele isiphumo esibhaliweyo sokubonisana kuManejala weNgingqi kwisithuba seentsuku ezingama 30.
Zakuba zifezekisiwe ezi mfuno, uManejala weNgingqi kufuneka athumele isicelo kuMphathiswa ukuze asiqwalasele.
;[UMqulu oPhangaleleyo weShishini leMigodi yaseMzantsi Afrika wokuNika aMandla kwiNtlalo noQoqosho]

Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Inkampani yoluntu liqumrhu elinomnikazi oluluntu kwaye inabalawuli (directors) abasixhenxe ubuncinane. Ekupheleni kwegama lenkampani kubhalwa igama elithi "Limited". Ubhaliso lwenkampani yoluntu lubandakanya le miba ilandelayo:
Uluntu lunikwa izabelo.
Nangona nje kungekho siqingqo sothintelo malunga nenani ekufanele bangagqithi kulo abanikazi bezabelo, aba bantu kufuneka babesixhenxe ubuncinane.
Ekupheleni kwegama lenkampani kubhalwa igama elithi "Limited".
Le nkampani kufuneka yenze ukuba inkcazelo ethile ifumaneke kuluntu.
Olu hlobo lweshishini ludla ngokudinga ukutyalwa kweemali ezinkulu.
Abalawuli babini ubuncinane.

Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Intlanganiso yoxolelwaniso yinkqubo apho umkomishina (okanye igqiza labaxoxi, kwimeko yebhunga okanye i-arhente yeengxoxo zokwenza izigqibo ezineenzuzo) ahlangana nemihlambi eyalanayo kwimpikiswano ukuze akhangele iindlela zokusombulula le mpikiswano ngesivumelwano.
Kwintlanganiso yoxolelwaniso umqeshi angaziyela ngokwakhe okanye angamelwa ngumqondisi okanye ngomnye umqeshwa okanye ngumbutho wabaqeshi. Umqeshwa angamelwa ngumngcini-sihlalo okanye ligosa lombutho obhalisiweyo womqeshwa.
Ukubangaba umenzi-sicelo akaphumelelanga ukuya kwintlanganiso yoxolelwaniso ngexesha elibekiweyo, lo mbandela uya kuchithwa. Ukubangaba umenzi-sicelo unqwenela ukuqhubeka, kufuneka kwenziwe isicelo sokurhoxisa oko kuchithwa.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Thumela ikopi yale fom kulo uphikisana naye.
Nika ubungqina bokuba ikopi yale fom isiwe kulo uphikisana naye, ngokufaka ezi zinto zilandelayo kwisicelo sakho:
o ikopi yesiliphu serejista esiphuma ePosini o ikopi yerisiti esayiniweyo ukubangaba ikopi isiwe ngesandla o ingxelo esayiniweyo yalo mntu uhambise ikopi yefom, engqina ukusiwa kwefom o ikopi yesiliphu esingqinayo sefeksi okanye nabuphi na obunye ubungqina obanelisayo benkonzo.

Entla

Isicelo sokubuyiselwa iintlawulo zelayisensi
Isicelo sokubuyiselwa indleko zephepha-mvume
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Ungasenza isicelo sokubuyiselwa indleko zephepha-mvume lemoto, xa imoto yakho yebiwe, ingasenakuphinda ilungele ukuhamba endleleni okanye icinyiwe kubhaliso lwemoto.
Isicelo sokubuyiswa kwendleko kufuneka senziwe zingaphelanga inyanga ezintathu ukususela ngomhla wesaziso sokwebiwa kwemoto, sokuba ngeke iphinde ikulungele ukuhamba endleleni okanye ngosuku lokucinywa kobhaliso lwemoto.
Qaphela: Imali engaphantsi kwamashumi amathathu ayibuyiselwa.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
o incwadi yesaziso o ingxelo efungelweyo eqinisekisa ukwebiwa kwemoto, angeke iphinde ikulungele ukuhamba endleleni okanye isatifiketi sokucinywa kobhaliso.
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Isicelo siqulunqwa kwangolo suku, kodwa imali ibuyiswa emva kwentsuku ezimbalwa ngenxa yokuphicothwa  kwencwadi zemali zangaphakathi.
Entla
Iindleko
Le nkonzo ayihlawulelwa.
Entla
Ifomu lesicelo sokubuyiselwa indleko zephepha-mvume lemoto, RLF, liyafumaneka ezindaweni ezikhupha amaphepha-mvume.

Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Zalisa ifom ngokuprinta ungadibanisi usebenzisa oonobumba abakhulu kuphela kwakunye nenkcazelo ezinika ingcaciso ebhaliweyo apho kuyimfuneko.
Nika le ngcaciso ilandelayo:
o inombolo yokubhalisa (registration number) yenqanawa o ilizwe elinegunya lolawulo (Flag State) inqanawa ebhaliswe phantsi kwalo njengangoku (nenikwe imvume yokuloba kulo okanye abemi baseMzantsi Afrika abangabanini ngokuhlangeneyo)
Ngenisa ifom yokwenza isicelo yakho kunye nelungelo lakho lokuloba okanye imvumelwano ekugqitywe ngayo kunye nomnikazi ochaphazelekayo wenqanawa eza kusetyenziswa ukuba akunguye umntu onelungelo lokuloba.
Xela ithuba necandelo lokuloba apho inqanawa iya kusetyenziswa khona.
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Isicelo singathatha iintsuku ezi-3 kwezokusebenza okanye ngaphezulu, ngokuxhomekeka ekufakweni okufanelekileyo kwesicelo.

Inkcazelo
Nangona nje uMthetho weeNkampani (Companies Act, 1973), umisela iintlanganiso ezisisinyanzelo kwiinkampani, ngakumbi malunga neentlanganiso zoluntu, akukho mfuneko malunga noku kwii-CC. Iintlanganiso zidla ngokubanjwa phakathi kwamalungu ngeloo xesha kukho imfuneko ethile.

Fumana incwadi yemvume esuka kwiGosa eliMele iiNkonzo.

Isicelo sokubhalisa ilungelo lokukhusela umsebenzi
Isicelo sokubhalisa ilungelo lokukhusela umsebenzi owenzileyo (i-copyright)
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Ilungelo lokukhusela umsebenzi othile owenzileyo (i-copyright), lilungelo lokukhusela umsebenzi othile umntu awenzileyo, ongaba ngumsebenzi obhaliweyo kunye nomsebenzi oluqobo lwemvelaphi yawo, iinkqubo zeekhpmpiyutha, imisebenzi yobugcisa, izinto nezixhobo zosasazo, umculo, imiboniso-bhanyabhanya (iifilimu) okanye iividiyo.
Eli gama lithi "Protect" ("khusela") lithetha ukunqanda abanye bangakwazi ukukopa okanye ukuvelisa ngokutsha umsebenzi okwafana naloo msebenzi uwenzileyo okanye loo nto uyenzileyo, kunye nokuwusebenzisa (ngaphandle kwemvume yakho) ukuze bazalisekise iinjongo zokuzizuzela imali. UMthetho waMalungelo okuKhusela iMisebenzi ethile eyenziweyo (Copyright Act, 1978) unika imiyalelo ye-copyright.
Ngokubanzi, umntu obhale, oshicilele, opapashe, obonise ngokomdlalo, oqingqe, ozobe, ofote okanye ofake kwiingxelo zokugcina, umsebenzi othile, ungumnikazi welungelo lokukhusela loo msebenzi (copyright), ngokuzenzekelayo. Nangona kunjalo, ngamanye amaxesha, xa umntu eyalelwe ukuba enze umsebenzi othile, kwaye ehlawulwe ukuze enze umsebenzi othile, ilungelo lokukhusela loo msebenzi iba lelomqashi.
Kwimisebenzi emininzi,(ngaphandle kwemiboniso-bhanyabhanya), akuyomfuneko ukwenza isicelo selungelo lokukhusela umsebenzi (i-copyright).
Ilungelo lokukhusela umsebenzi othile owenzileyo malunga nemiboniso-bhanyabhanya okanye iividiyo, ezenzelwe ukusetyenziselwa urhwebo, kufuneka lenzelwe isicelo ngokugunyazisiweyo, ngokwale miqulu ilandelayo, efumaneka ngaphandle kwentlawulo kwi-Ofisi yaMalungelo okuKhusela iMisebenzi ethile eyenziweyo (Copyright Office):
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Nxulumana neSebe lezoRhwebo naMashishini.

Entla

Emva kwethuba leenyanga ezintandathu, kwenziwa izintoyinto ezigunyazisiweyo zeemviwo ezigunyazisiweyo, kwaye ilungelo lokukhusela umsebenzi othile owenzileyo (i-copyright) lidla ngokunikwa kwinyanga yesixhenxe.

Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Ngokusisiseko "uyilo" ("design") lumalunga nokwakheka nokubumbeka kunye neempawu ezinomtsalane emehlweni. Ezinye iintlobo zoyilo (design) zibaluyilo ngenxa yomsebenzi wazo kwaye ezinye zibanjalo ngenxa yobuhle nembonakalo yobuhle.
Zimbini iintlobo zoyilo ezingabhaliswa, kodwa ke xangaba zifezekisa iimfuno ezichazwe apha ngezantsi:
Uyilo oluphenjelelwa bubuhle nembonakalo yobuhle kufuneka into ibentsha kwaye ibeluqobo lwayo lwemveli;
ibenobuhle ekwakhekeni nasekubunjweni, kwingqaleko okanye ekuhonjisweni; kwaye kufuneka ikwazi ukuveliswa yinkqubo yamashishini.
Uyilo oluphenjelelwa ngumsebenzi wento kufanele into ibentsha kwaye ingabiyonto eqhelekileyo;
Nangona nje kungesosinyanzelo ukufunisa ukuze kukhangelwe uqobo lwemveli yoyilo okanye ukuze kuqinisekiswe ukuba olu yilo okanye uyilo olufana nolu aluzange lwabhaliswa na ngaphambili, kulicebo elihle ukwenza njalo phambi kokufaka isicelo sobhaliso. Kungafuniswa ngoyilo kwi-Ofisi yoBhaliso loYilo (Design Registry Office) e-Pretoria. Oku kufunisa kufuneka kwenziwe ngumntu ubuqu bakhe okanye ngumnxulumanisi (yi-eyijenti), ofana negqwetha lamalungelo okuvelisa nokuqamba.
Uyilo luyavuselelwa qho emva kweminyaka emithathu.

Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Nxulumana neSebe lezoRhwebo naMashishini.
Thumela ikopi eqinisekisiweyo yencwadi yakho yesazisi.

Isicelo sokubhalisa inkampani yelizwe langaphandle
Isicelo sokubhalisa inkampani yelizwe langaphandle
Inkcazelo
Umbutho welizwe langaphandle ongaphandle koMzantsi Afrika onqwenela ukuqhuba naliphi na ishishini eMzantsi Afrika ungenza isicelo sepemethe njengenkampani yelizwe langaphandle. Inkampani yelizwe langaphandle yinkampani ebhaliswe kwilizwe langaphandle kwaye enqwenela ukuseka inkampani eMzantsi Afrika.
Ngenxa yeenkqubo ezininzi eziqhubekayo njengenxenye yenkqubo yobhaliso iyonke, kulicebo elihle ukuba usebenzise iinkonzo zamagqwetha aseMzantsi Afrika.
Kufanele unxulumane nengcaphephe yasemthethweni eMzantsi Afrika, njengoko iimfuneko ezithile zomThetho weeNkampani (Companies Act, 1973), zingafezekiswa kuphela ngamalungu elo candelo loqeqesho lobuchule.
Nceda uqaphele ukuba yonke imiqulu kufuneka izaliswe nge-inki emnyama enzulu nesisigxina.
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Khupha iikopi eziqinisekisiweyo zeencwadi zezazisi okanye iipaspoti ezisebenzisekayo zabo bonke abantu ababandakanyeka kule nkampani izakubhaliswa.
Yonke imiqulu kufuneka ikhatshwe yiMimiselo kunye neMigaqo yokuManyana, ekufuneka ibesencwadini kwaye kufuneka iqinisekiswe ngokwegunya lasemthethweni kwiphepha ngalinye nguMntu oneGunya laseMthethweni lokuQinisekisa iMiqulu kwilizwe lemvelaphi.

Ubhaliso lungathabatha iintsuku ezintlanu.

Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Abantu okanye imibutho inelungelo lokwenza isicelo se namba pleyiti yesimntwiso xa befuna ukusebenzisa amagama abo okanye awemibutho njengamanani okubhaliswa kwemoto. Eli nani limntwisiweyo libonakaliswa ngendlela efanayo nenani lobhaliso lwemoto lesiqhelo. Inani liba yimpahla yomntu inamba pleyiti ebhaliswe ngaye.
Inamba pleyiti ebhaliswe ngegama lomntu okanye le nkampani kufuneka ilandele yonke imiqathango elandelwa xa kubhaliswa inamba pleyiti yesiqhelo (umzekelo kufuneka ibe nelogo yephondo).
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Dibana neofiso yamagosa endlela ekufutshane.
Khupha ikopi eqinisekisiwe yencwadi yesazisi nesatifiketi sobhaliso semoto.
Bhatala imali ebekiweyo.

Inkcazelo
Ukuze ubhalise, kuya kufuneka uhlawule idipozithi ebuyiswayo, kwi-akhawunti ye-CIPRO. Emva kokuba kufunyenwe ubungqina bobhaliso lwakho, i-akhawunti iyakushukunyiswa kwaye ilungele ukusetyenziswa. Iindleko zokujonga nokuprinta iSatifiketi seNkampani okanye seQumrhu elingaVulelekanga elibhalisiweyo yi- R30 isatifiketi sisinye. Le mali iya kuba kwi-akhawunti yedipozithi enxulumaniswe kuphawu lwakho lokubayi-arhente, eya kusetyenziswa ngokuzenzekelayo ukuze ikuthumele ibango lokuhlawula ekupheleni kwenyanga.

Iinkonzo zabantu
Imfundo noqeqesho
Amaziko akwinqanaba lesithathu
Isicelo sokubhalisela ukubangusosayensi wezendalo oqeqeshiweyo
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
ukuphakamisa ukusetyenziswa kwezifundo zoqeqesho lwenzululwazi (lwesayensi) yezendalo eMzantsi Afrika;
Abantu abangabhaliswanga abanako ukwenza umsebenzi ochongelwe abantu ababhalisiweyo.
Kutheni kufanele ubhalise?
Ukuze wenze umsebenzi wezifundo zoqeqesho
Ukuze uqhube umsebenzi ngokwesikhundla sokuba yikhonsalthenti
Ukuze uxhamle ubume bemfundo yoqeqesho kwaye ubandakanyeke kwiinzuzo ezinikwa ngamaziko ezemali
Ukuze kukhuselwe kwaye komelezwe ezi zifundo zoqeqesho
Ziintoni ezifunekayo ukuze ubhaliswe?
Ukuze ubhalisele ukubangusosayensi wezendalo oqeqeshiweyo - kufuneka ubenesidanga (idigri) seminyaka emine okanye idiploma yeminyaka emine, idibane namava weminyaka emithathu
Ukuze ubhalisele ukubangusosayensi wezendalo ongumlingwa - kufuneka ubenesidanga seminyaka emine okanye idiploma yeminyaka emine, ungabinamava
Ukuze ubhalisele ukubangusosayensi wezendalo oqinisekisiweyo - kufuneka ubenesidanga seminyaka emithathu okanye idiploma yeminyaka emithathu, ubenama onyaka omnye
Amacandelo obhaliso ngala alandelayo:
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Faka kwisicelo sakho intlawulo eqingqiweyo yobhaliso..
IBhunga liyakukubhalisa kwaye likhuphe isatifiketi sobhaliso ukubangaba lanelisekile ukuba unazo iimfuneko ezibandakanyekayo zemfundo namava njengoko kuqulungqwe liBhunga.
Isiphumo sovavanyo asiyikwaziswa kude kubesemva kwentlanganiso yeBhunga.
IBhunga lingala ukubhalisa isicelo phantsi kwezi meko zilandelayo:
Ukubangaba, emva kokuqalisa koMgaqo-siseko weRiphabhlikhi yaseMzantsi Afrika, 1996, umenzi-sicelo ufunyaniswe enetyala lokwaphula umthetho, ngaphakathi kwiRiphabhlikhi okanye kwenye indawo, waze wagwetyelwa ukuvalelwa entolongweni isithuba esidlula iinyanga ezintathu, okanye ifayini endaweni yokuvalelwa entolongweni.
Ukubangaba umenzi-sicelo ususwe esikhundleni sokuthembeka, ngenxa yokuziphatha okungafanelekanga..
Ukubangaba umenzi-sicelo ungumntu ongakwaziyo ukuhlawula amatyala nongabuyiselwanga kwimeko yesiqhelo, kwaye oko kungakwazi ukuhlawula amatyala kwabangelwa kukungakhathali kwakhe okanye ukungabinalwazi nezakhono zokwenza umsebenzi owela kwimiba echatshazelwa licandelo enzela lona isicelo sobhaliso.
IBhunga liyakukwazisa ngencwadi ebhaliweyo ukubangaba isicelo sakho sobhaliso saliwe
Ungafaka isibheno esiphikisa isigqibo seBhunga, kwisithuba seentsuku ezingama 30.
Kufuneka wenze isicelo sokuvuselela ubhaliso lwakho kwiBhunga, okungenani kwiinyanga ezintathu phambi kokuphelelwa kobhaliso lwakho.
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Ubhaliso lungathabatha iiveki ezintandathu ukuya kwezisibhozo, kuxhomekeke ekungenisweni kwemiqulu efunekayo.
Entla
Iindleko
Kwiinkonzo zebhanki zobuxhakaxhaka bombane kunye needipozithi nqo: Nceda usebenzise oonobumba bokuqala bamagama akho kunye nefani yakho ukuze uchaze intlawulo yakho kwisitetimenti sethu sebhanki, uze uthumele ubungqina bentlawulo ngefeksi, buhambe kunye nephepha LOKUQALA lefom yakho yesicelo, kwinombolo ethi: 841 1057.
Iinkcukacha zebhanki:

Iinkonzo zemibutho
Isicelo sokubhalisela ukubangumhlawuli werhafu yokubambisa
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Umhlawuli werhafu yokubambisa angachazwa ngolu hlobo lulandelayo:
Xa inkampani ingakhange yayifumana irhafu yabasebenzi kumqondisi, akanakuzithathela ingqalelo iintlawulo zerhafu zabo basebenzi xa equlungqa imfaneleko yoxanduva lokuhlawula irhafu yokubambisa.
Umntu ofaneleka ukuba ahlawule irhafu yokubambisa kufuneka, kwisithuba seentsuku ezingama 30 zokungena kolo xanduva lokufaneleka, enze isicelo esibhaliweyo sokubhaliswa kwi-ofisi yebhrentshi ye-SARS ekwindawo ahlala kuyo. Ukungaphumeleli ukwenza njalo kungakhokelela kwinzala nezohlwayo kwiintlawulo ezifike emva kwexesha kunye nerhafu eyongezelelweyo ngenxa yokuthumela kade iifom zokubuyisa zerhafu.
Akukho mfuneko yokuba aba bantu balandelayo bahlawule irhafu yokubambisa:
nawuphina umntu ofumana ingeniso-mali emvuzweni kuphela nawuphina umntu onengeniso-mali engadlulanga kwisiqingqo somda wokurhafa, esiyi R43 000 kubantu abaneminyaka engaphantsi kwe 65 ubudala, ne R69 000 kubantu abangaphezulu kwama 65 iminyaka yobudala nawuphina umntu, ngaphandle kwengeniso-mali evela kutyalo-mali, ofumana ingeniso-mali yotyalo-mali engagqithanga kwi R18 000 kubantu abangaphantsi kwama 65 eminyaka yobudala, okanye i R26 000 kubantu abangaphezulu kwama 65 eminyaka yobudala. Iinzala nezahlulo zakumazwe angaphandle zinikwa umnyenyevu wokungahlawuli ofika nje kwi R3 000 yomnyenyevu opheleleyo nawuphina umntu oneminyaka engama 65 okanye nangaphezulu ubudala, akukho mfuneko yokuba ahlawule irhafu yokubambisa ukubangaba:
Ingeniso-mali erhafelwayo kunyaka werhafu ayidluli kwi R80 000 kwaye ibandakanya intlawulo yomvuzo, ipenshele, inzala, izahlulo okanye ingeniso-mali yerenti, kwaye
Akaqhubi shishini lithile.

Impahla nezinto eziyimveliso yengqondo
Ukubhalisa impahla nezinto eziyimveliso yengqondo
Isicelo sokubhalisa uphawu
Isicelo sokubhalisa uphawu okanye igama lokwazisa ngempahla nezinto okanye ngeenkonzo (i-trademark)
Inkcazelo
Uphawu okanye igama lokwazisa ngempahla nezinto okanye iinkonzo (i-trademark) ligama lohlobo oluthille (i-brand), intetho emfutshane yokwazisa ngempahla nezinto okanye ngeenkonzo ezithile (i-slogan) okanye uyilo lophawu lokwazisa ngempahla nezinto okanye ngeenkonzo ezithile (i-logo). I-trade mark ichaza iinkonzo okanye impahla nezinto zomntu kwaye yenza zicace kwaye zahluke kwimpahla nezinto kunye neenkonzo zomnye umntu. Imizekelo ibandakanya le ilandelayo:
Ngoko ke, igama lohlobo (i-brand name) ligama okanye intlanganisela yamagama (umzekelo, Kentucky Fried Chicken). Intetho emfutshane yokwazisa ngempahla nezinto okanye ngeenkonzo (i-slogan), libinzana elifutshane okanye isivakalisi esifutshane kwaye uyilo lophawu lokwazisa ngempahla nezinto okanye ngeenkonzo (i-logo) ngumfanekiso okanye uphawu lokwahlula. Ezi mpawu zinika ulwaziso olwahlukileyo, kwintengiso, kwaye zingasebenziseka kwiimveliso nakwiinkonzo.
Xa uphawu okanye igama lokwazisa ngempahla nezinto okanye iinkonzo (igama lohlobo, intetho emfutshane yokwazisa ngempahla nezinto okanye ngeenkonzo okanye uyilo lophawu lokwazisa ngempahla nezinto okanye ngeenkonzo), sele libhalisiwe, akukho mntu ongomnye ongasebenzisa olu phawu okanye eli gama okanye asebenzise elifana nalo. Ukuba oku kuyenzeka, kungalandela amanyathelo asemthethweni. Kuke kwakho amatyala akwizinga eliphakamileyo eMzantsi Afrika afana naxa i-MacDonalds (USA) yathi yamangalela umthengisi wokutya okuphekwa ngokukhawuleza (fast food) eMzantsi Afrika owayesebenzisa uphawu olufana nele-MacDonalds elino "M".
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Fumana ifom ekuthiwa yi-TM1 kwaye uyigcwalise ngokuphindwe kathathu. Iikopi ezimbini zisetyenziswa yi-ofisi kwaye eyesithathu igcinwa nguwe njengobungqina besicelo sakho.
Qala uhlawule imali yobhaliso okanye uyihlawule xa usisa isicelo.
Uqaphele kwaye ulumke kakhulu ungafaki impahla nezinto okanye iinkonzo ezikwiindidi ezahlukeneyo kwisicelo esinye sophawu okanye segama lokwazisa ngempahla nezinto okanye ngeenkonzo. Ukuba wenza njalo, uyakucetyiswa ukuba ulungise inkcazelo ibandakanye impahla nezinto okanye iinkonzo zolo didi luxeliweyo. Kwezinye, kuyakufuneka ufake isicelo esahlukileyo ngokutsha.
Emva koko ke uluntu lunikwa ithuba leenyanga ezintathu ukuze lufake iinkcaso.
Hlawula ebhankini usebenzise uvimba wophawu lweekhastoma.
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Kungathabatha iminyaka emibini ukuze kugqityezelwe ubhaliso lophawu okanye lwegama lokwazisa ngempahla nezinto okanye ngeenkonzo.
Iindleko
R85, yokufunisa nokukhangela iimpawu ezikhoyo okanye amagama akhoyo okwazisa ngempahla nezinto okanye ngeenkonzo
R266, yodidi ngalunye lophawu okanye lwegama lokwazisa ngempahla nezinto okanye ngeenkonzo

Isicelo sobhaliso lwesikhululo sovavanyo lwemoto
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Isikhululo sovavanyo lwemoto liziko elivavanya iimoto likhuphe isatifiketi sokulungela ukuhamba endleleni.Kukhona izikhululo zovavanyo lwemoto ezizimeleyo nezikarhulumente. Zonke izikhululo zovavanyo lwemoto kufuneka zibhaliswe, zinikwe izinga lokusebenza ngaphambi kokuba zikhuphe isatifiketi sokulungela ukuhamba endlelen. Lisakufumana isicelo iCandelo lezoThutho lizakuthumela umhloli ayokujongisisa ukuba isikhululo sovavanyo abone ukuba siyilandele imithetho yobugcisa obubeka isikhululo emgangathweni wobhaliso obekwe yingqokelela yemithetho Yolawulo loMgangatho yase Mzantsi Afrika (SABS).
Ukuphumelelangobugcisa kubhekiselele ezintweni zokusebenza zesikhululo sovavanyo noqeqesho abalugqibileyo abavavanyi bemoto.
Izikhululo zovavanyo ezibhalisiweyo zingavavanya kuphela iimoto ngokomgangatho wesikhululo eso.
Ukubhalisa isikhululo esizimeleyo sovavanyo lwemoto, dibana ne ofisi lamagosa endlela ekufutshane ufumane ulwazi oluphangalele.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Thumela incwadi yakho yesaziso neyomntu omele abalawuli xa isicelo usenzela isikhululo sovavanyo.
Kungafuneka uthumele amanye amaxwebhu afunwa yiNkulu Mbuso (MEC).
Bhatala imali ebekiweyo.

Inkqubo emayilandelwe

Uthutho
Bhalisa imisebenzi okanye iinkonzo zothutho
Ubhaliso lweziko lokuthesta iilayisensi zokuqhuba
Isicelo sokubhalisa iziko lovavanyela amaphepha-mvume okuqhuba imoto.
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Isicelo sokubhalisa iziko lokuvavanyela amaphepha-mvume okuqhuba masenziwe kumafomu esicelo amisiweyo.Njengenxalenye yokuphononongwa kwesicelo kulindeleke ukuba uchaze abameli babalawuli nabavavanyi bamaphepha-mvume okuqhuba.
Xa inkulu mbuso yanelisekile lucwaningo uza kulinika umgangatho iziko lovavanyo, agcine ikcukacha kwincwadi yokubhalisa yamaziko okuvavanyela phepha-mvume lokuqhuba akhuphele umceli isatifiketi sobhaliso.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Qhakamshelana neCandelo lezoThutho lephondo.
o iincwadi zezazisi zabalawuli beziko lovavanyo lokuqhuba (kuquka abavavanyi bamaphepha-mvume)
o isatifiketi sokubhaliswa kweshishini.

Kungathabatha iinyanga ezintandathu ukubhalisa iziko lovavanyo.

Inkcazelo
Kufuneka i-arhente yokungenisa elizweni ithobele izinto ezilandelayo:
isakhelo kufuneka sibenazo zonke izixhobo ezimiselweyo malunga nokusebenza ngezixhobo zofuzo lwezilwanyana ilebhu kunye nesakhelo sokuqinisekisa serhafu yokungenisa elizweni kufuneka silandele imiqathango esezantsi emiselweyo abaqeshi kufuneka bafaneleke ukusebenza ngencindi yobudoda.

Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Nabanina onqwenela ukufuya iinyathi kufuneka aqale abhalise umhlaba lowo kwiSebe leZolimo.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Cela ugqirha wezilwanyana wombuso okwindawo ohlala kuyo ahlole umhlaba nocingo kwaye angqine ngobume beenyathi ngokwezifo.
Intloko yeenkonzo zezilwanyana kwiphondo kufuneka inike ubungqina bokuba, zikho izinto eziyimfuneko zokubeka iliso rhoqo kwiimeko zefama, zonke iintshukumo nokuhambahamba kweenyathi xa zingena kwifama naxa ziphuma kuyo kungajongwana nazo ngokufanelekileyo kwaye izinto ezingahambi njengesiqhelo ziyakuqwalaseleka ngaphandle kokulibazisa.
Isicelo kufuneka sikhatshwe zezi ncwadi zilandelayo: 
o isatifiketi esigunyazisiweyo sokurhangqeleka okufanelekileyo esikhutshwe ngoogunyaziwe bolondolozo lwendalo o ikopi yemephu ebonisa nqo ukunaba nobungakanani bomhlaba ocelwayo.
Hambisa isicelo kuManejala oMkhulu weMpilo yeZilwanyana, iFeksi: 329-0499.
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Ixesha elithatyathwayo ukuze kuvunywe isicelo lahluka ngokwephondo. Sakuba sivunyiwe isicelo, sithunyelwa kwiSebe leLizwe leZolimo.
Amagosa kwisebe lelizwe akhupha inombolo yobhaliso egunyazisiweyo, afake inkcazelo kwincwadi yelizwe ebhalise iinyathi aze aprintele umnini-mhlaba isatifiketi sobhaliso. Le nkqubo ingathabatha iintsuku zokusebenza ezilishumi.

Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Ukuze ufaneleke okanye ulungele ukuba uvote kunyulo lukazwelonke, olwephondo okanye unyulo lukamasipala, kufuneka ubhalisele ukuvota kweso sithili uhlala kuso. Oku kubalulekile ingakumbi kunyulo loomasipala ngenxa yokuba unokuvota kuphela kwisithili owawubhalise kuso. Wakuba ubhalisile zaze iinkcukacha zakho zangqinisiswa kwiRejista yabemi belizwe, igama lakho liya kufakwa kuMqulu woluhlu lwabaVoti oyi-National Common Voter's Roll.
Ukuze ufaneleke ekubeni ubhalise kufuneka:
Ube ngummi waseMzantsi Afrika
Ubeneminyaka eli-16 ubudala okanye ngaphezulu
UMqulu woluhlu lwabaVoti uyavalwa ukulungiselela unyulo kanye ngalo mhla wonyulo kolo nyulo luthe ngqo luthe lwabhengezwa kwiGazethi kaRhulumente.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Bhalisa ngokwakho buqu kwisikhululo sokuvota kwisithili sokuvota apho uhlala khona ngexesha lokubhalisela ukuvota.
Bhalisa nangaliphi na ixesha ngethuba leeyure zokusebenza kwiKhomishoni yoNyulo eZimeleyo 
Zalisa ifom yokwenza isicelo efanelekileyo.
Igosa lobhaliso liya kufaka istikha kwincwadi yesazisi (ID) yakho enenombolo yesithili sokuvota kuyo.

Iimanyano zabasebenzi kunye nemibutho yabaqashi
Inkcazelo
Iyuniyoni ngumbutho wabasebenzi ophakamisa kwaye okhusela iminqweno yamalungu ayo kwimibandela efana nemivuzo kunye neemeko zokusebenza, ngakumbi ngokothetha-thethwano nabaqeshi.
Iikopi ezintathu ezishicilelweyo zomgaqo-siseko weyuniyoni
Uluhlu oluneenkcukacha zamagosa eyuniyoni, oluchaza izikhundla zabo okanye imisebenzi abayenzayo.
Ikopi nganye yomgaqo-siseko mayisayinwe nguNobhala nanguMhlali-Ngaphambili, bezivuma ukuba ziikopi zokwenyani.
Ukuze ufumane inkcazelo ebanzi, yiya kwiSebe leZabasebenzi.
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Zalisa iikopi ezimbini zefom yesicelo.
Faka iikopi ezintathu zomgaqo-siseko weyuniyoni (iincwadi ezintlanu zizonke) kwifom yesicelo eya kuthunyelwa kuMphathi woBhaliso (Registrar).
Ikopi nganye yomgaqo-siseko mayisayinwe nguNobhala nanguMhlali-Ngaphambili, bezivuma ukuba ziikopi zokwenyani.

Isicelo sokubhalisela ukusebenzisa amanzi  
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Bonke abasebenzisi bamanzi, abangafumani unkinkisho lwabo lwamanzi kumniki-nkonzo, kugunyaziwe wendawo yabahlali, kwibhodi yamanzi, kwibhodi yonkcenkceshelo, kuyilo lwenkqubo karhulumente okanye komnye umnkinkishi wesixa samanzi, kufuneka babhalise ukusebenzisa kwabo amanzi kwiSebe lezaManzi naMahlathi ekuthiwa yi-Department of Water Affairs and Forestry (DWAF). Aba basebenzisi kufuneka babe basebenzisa amanzi ngezi njongo zilandelayo:
Olunye usetyenziso lwamanzi ekufuneka lubhaliswe lubandakanya:
o ukuchithwa kwenkunkuma okanye amanzi anenkunkuma o ukutshintshwa kweendlela ekuhamba ngazo imilambo nemisinga okanye uguqulelo kwizandlalelo zemilambo okanye iindonga zemilambo okanye iimpawu zecala amanzi aya ngakulo.
Ukugcinwa kwamanzi - Nawuphi na umntu okanye iqumrhu eligcina amanzi ngazo naziphi na iinjongo (kubandakanywa unkcenkceshelo, unkinkishelo lwasekhaya, usetyenziso lwezamashishini, ukwembiwa kwemigodi, ukufuya izilwanyana ezihlala emanzini nokutyala izityalo ezihlala emanzini, ukuloba, imidlalo yamanzi, ukuxatyiswa kobuhle, ukusetyenzwa kwesitiya, ukuyilwa komhlaba wesitiya, ukudlalwa kwegalufa, njalo-njalo) ekubalekeni phantsi emhlabeni, amanzi aphantsi emhlabeni, okanye ukuqukuqela kwemithombo egqitha ngaphaya kwe 10 000 cubic meters okanye apho ummandla wamanzi kwinqanaba lonkinkisho olupheleleyo udlula i-akire e 1 iphelele, kumhlaba onobunikazi baloo mntu okanye ohlalwa nguloo mntu okanye liqumrhu elingenapemethe okanye imvume.
Imisebenzi yokunciphisa ukuqukuqela kwemisinga (Ukwakhiwa kwamahlathi) - Yonke imisebenzi yolwakhiwo lwamahlathi (ukutyalwa kwemithi) ngeenjongo zorhwebo, kubandakanywa iinkonzo zamahlathi adityanelweyo ngeenjongo zenzuzo yorhwebo, ezaqhubeka phambi kuka 1972, kufuneka zibhaliswe. Abanikazi bamahlathi abaneepemethe ezakhutshwa phantsi komThetho waMahlathi ekuthiwa yi-Forestry Act, 1998 (Act 84 of 1998), akukho mfuneko yokuba babhalise, njengoko siya kubathumela imiqulu yokubhalisa egcwalisiweyo, ukuze bayilungise ukuba kuyimfuneko, bayisayine baze bayibuyisele kwisebe.
Usetyenziso ngoogunyaziwe beendawo zabahlali kunye nabanye abankinkishi besixa abanemithombo yabo yamanzi kunye nemisebenzi yokungcwenga nokucoca.
IMisebenzi eLawulwayo, efana nokunkcenkceshela ngenkunkuma, ukuvelisa amandla ombane ngamanzi, ukulungelelaniswa komoya ojikeleze umhlaba okanye ukumpompa amandla kumatye afunxa nakhupha amanzi.  
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Khangela usetyenziso lwamanzi oluchanekileyo.
Zalisa iifom ezibandakanyekayo ngokuncediswa ligosa lengingqi.
o iinkcukacha zomenzi-sicelo o ipropati apho kuqhubeka khona usetyenziso lwamanzi o iinkcukacha zomnikazi wepropati o isibhengezo somenzi-sicelo o isibhengezo somnikazi wepropati o inkcazelo yesaziso sokuhlawula o ikopi eqinisekisiweyo yencwadi yesazisi o ikopi eqinisekisiweyo yomqulu wesigqibo sasemthethweni sepropati o ikopi eqinisekisiweyo yesivumelwano sengqeshiso o ukuhambisana nazo zonke iimfuneko zeenkonzo ezahlukeneyo ekwenziwa isicelo sazo.

Imfundo noqeqesho
Isicelo sokubhalisela ukubangusosayensi wezendalo oqeqeshiweyo, kwicandelo leNzululwazi esetyenziswa kuPhando loBugebenga
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
ukuphakamisa ukusetyenziswa kwezifundo zoqeqesho lwenzululwazi (lwesayensi) yezendalo eMzantsi Afrika;
ukubeka iliso kumgangatho wemfundo noqeqesho loososayensi bezendalo, kunye 
Abantu abangabhaliswanga abanako ukwenza umsebenzi ochongelwe abantu ababhalisiweyo..
Kutheni kufanele ubhalise?
Ukuze wenze umsebenzi wezifundo zoqeqesho
Ukuze uqhube umsebenzi ngokwesikhundla sokuba yikhonsalthenti
Ukuze uxhamle ubume bemfundo yoqeqesho kwaye ubandakanyeke kwiinzuzo ezinikwa ngamaziko ezemali
Ukuze kukhuselwe kwaye komelezwe ezi zifundo zoqeqesho
Ukuze uvumeleke ubhaliselwe ukusebenza kwicandelo leNzululwazi (leSayensi) esetyenziswa kuPhando loBugebenga, kufuneka ufezekise ezi mfuneko zilandelayo:
kufuneka ifundwe ngokunzulu nangokubanzi ngendlela eyandayo kwiminyaka emine;
Uqeqesho olongezelelweyo:
Kufanele ukwazi ukunika ubungqina boqeqesho kwiNzululwazi esetyenziswa kuPhando loBugebenga okanye kuPhando olusebenzisa iNzululwazi yoBugebenga, umzekelo, ukuphonononga imiqulu, uphando lomlilo, uphando lokuqaphela ukuphawulwa kwezinto, uphando lokutshutshisa, imigaqo yomthetho neyenkundla, ingqina lobungcaphephe, okanye ezinye iikhosi ezimfutshane ezinikwe uqinisekiso lokuvunywa. 
Kufuneka ubenengxelo ecacileyo nesulungekileyo yomsebenzi nophando olwayamene nenzululwazi esetyenziswa kuphando lobugebenga.
Imiba yolwazi eyimfuneko kwingcali yenzululwazi esetyenziswa kuphando lobugebenga ibandakanya iinkqubo zemisebenzi yeekhosi ezisetyenziswa kuphando lobugebenga: Kubalulekile ukuba usosayensi oqeqeshwayo wenzululwazi esetyenziswa kuphando lobugebenga aqonde ngemiba yolwazi eyimfuneko kwiNzululwazi esetyenziswa kuPhando loBugebenga, kwaye afumane izakhono namava ekusetyenzisweni kwezi zibakala zilandelayo zisisiseko kuphando lobugebenga:
Intshayelelo kwezomthetho
Ukuqinisekiswa komgangatho 
Imimiselo elawula okanye ephembelela indlela yokuziphatha
Ukusebenza ngendlela enemfundo noqeqesho
Ukuchonga ubungqina, ukubuqokelela, kunye nokubuqhubekisa
Izakhono zokusombulula iingxaki, zobunzululwazi nezaselabhorathri
Ukusebenzisa inzululwazi (isayensi) kwiinkqubo zomthetho
Iindlela zobuchule zophando lobugebenga
Uphando kwindawo ekwenzekele kuyo ubugebenga
Ulwazi lokucubungula amachiza kunye neendlela zokusebenzisa izixhobo zokucubungula
Ukucubungula iziyobisi, ukucubungula ubuhlungu nobutyhefu bamachiza, ukusebenzisa isixhobo sokubonisa izinto ezincinane ekuthiwa yimayikhroskopu, kunye nokucubungula izinto ezithile
Ukusebenzisa inzululwazi yezidalwa eziphilayo kuphando lobugebenga
Amava omsebenzi
Ukuphonononga nokuhlela izixhobo okanye iimbumbulu namakhoba azo
Ukunxulumanisa isixhobo nobugebenga, ukuya kwenza umsebenzi kwiindawo ekwenzekele kuzo ubugebenga kunye nokuvavanya amandla obungqina bophando lobugebenga
Inkxaso yobuchule kuphando lweengozi zezithuthi zendlela, ukwakha umfanekiso wezinto ezenzekileyo ezikhokelele kungquzulwano lwezithuthi, ukuphonononga nzulu nangokubanzi izakhi zezithuthi, ulwazi oluthile lobuchwepheshe bezinto ezizenzekela ngomatshini. (Ziyakufaneleka iikhwalifikheyshini kwi-physics okanye kwiinzululwazi zezinto ezibambekayo.)
Ukuphanda ngomlilo
Izifundo ngemiqulu yemibuzo - ukuchaza imvelaphi yemibhalo yesandla
Ukwenza kufezekiseke kwaye kubelula ukubona nokuhlangula ubungqina
Ukuphakamisa izinga lokuxabiseka kobungqina
Ukuya kusebenza kwiindawo ekwenzekele kuzo iingozi ngokwesikhundla sokucebisa
Uxanduva lokuphatha kwizinto ezinxulumana nokuphononongwa kwaselabhorathri okwayamene nezenzo zobugebenga
Ukucubungula - inzululwazi yezidalwa eziphilayo, ucubungulo lwamachiza, iziyobisi kunye nobuhlungu nobutyhefu bamachiza
Ubungqina bezobunzululwazi obungakheth'icala elithile kwiinkundla zamatyala ukuze kuxhaswe utshutshiso okanye iqela elikhusela umtyholwa kuphando lobugebenga
Amacandelo obhaliso ngala alandelayo:
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Faka kwisicelo sakho intlawulo eqingqiweyo yobhaliso.
IBhunga liyakukubhalisa kwaye likhuphe isatifiketi sobhaliso ukubangaba lanelisekile ukuba unazo iimfuneko ezibandakanyekayo zemfundo namava njengoko kuqulungqwe liBhunga.
Isiphumo sovavanyo asiyikwaziswa kude kubesemva kwentlanganiso yeBhunga.
IBhunga lingala ukubhalisa isicelo phantsi kwezi meko zilandelayo:
Ukubangaba, emva kokuqalisa koMgaqo-siseko weRiphabhlikhi yaseMzantsi Afrika, 1996, umenzi-sicelo ufunyaniswe enetyala lokwaphula umthetho, ngaphakathi kwiRiphabhlikhi okanye kwenye indawo, waze wagwetyelwa ukuvalelwa entolongweni isithuba esidlula iinyanga ezintathu, okanye ifayini endaweni yokuvalelwa entolongweni.
Ukubangaba umenzi-sicelo ususwe esikhundleni sokuthembeka, ngenxa yokuziphatha okungafanelekanga.
Ukubangaba umenzi-sicelo ungumntu ongakwaziyo ukuhlawula amatyala nongabuyiselwanga kwimeko yesiqhelo, kwaye oko kungakwazi ukuhlawula amatyala kwabangelwa kukungakhathali kwakhe okanye ukungabinalwazi nezakhono zokwenza umsebenzi owela kwimiba echatshazelwa licandelo enzela lona isicelo sobhaliso.
IBhunga liyakukwazisa ngencwadi ebhaliweyo ukubangaba isicelo sakho sobhaliso saliwe
Ungafaka isibheno esiphikisa isigqibo seBhunga, kwisithuba seentsuku ezingama 30.
Kufuneka wenze isicelo sokuvuselela ubhaliso lwakho kwiBhunga, okungenani kwiinyanga ezintathu phambi kokuphelelwa kobhaliso lwakho.
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Ubhaliso lungathabatha iiveki ezintandathu ukuya kwezisibhozo, kuxhomekeke ekungenisweni kwemiqulu efunekayo.
Entla
Iindleko
Kwiinkonzo zebhanki zobuxhakaxhaka bombane kunye needipozithi nqo: Nceda usebenzise oonobumba bokuqala bamagama akho kunye nefani yakho ukuze uchaze intlawulo yakho kwisitetimenti sethu sebhanki, uze uthumele ubungqina bentlawulo ngefeksi, buhambe kunye nephepha LOKUQALA lefom yakho yesicelo, kwinombolo ethi: 841 1057.

Inkcazelo
Inkcazelo ephathelelene nobhaliso lwepropati engashukumiyo, efana nale ilandelayo:
o amagama, iinkcukacha zokuzazisa kunye nobume bomtshato babanikazi ababhalisileyo o amanani emiyalelo yenkundla yokuthintela izenzo ezithile efakelwe abantu kunye nepropati o iinkcukacha zokutshintshelwa kwepropati, kubandakanywa imihla yobhaliso kunye namaxabiso okuthenga o iinkcukacha zobambiso ngepropati njengesetyhorithi yemali-mboleko,  kubandakanywa amagama wabantu ababambise ngeepropati njengesetyhorithi yemali-mboleko kunye neemali eziyinkunzi
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Uyakunikwa igama lomsebenzisi. Eli gama iyakuba yinombolo yakho ye-akhawunti yazo zonke iinjongo zezemali. Kwakhona, uyakunikwa igama eliyimfihlo lokungena (oko kukuthi igama elithi "password") ekufuneka emva koko ulitshintshe kwamsinyane kangangoko unako.
Hlawula imali yokubhalisa. Imiyalelo yebhanki kunye neenkcukacha ziyabonakala kwi-website.

Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Iintlobo-ntlobo ezininzi zeekhwalifikheyshini ezahlukeneyo kwicandelo lenzululwazi yezokusingqongileyo ezinikwa ziiyunivesiti ngokungakumbi, zenza ukuba ngamanye amaxesha phantse kungakwazeki ukuvavanya ikhwalifikheyshini eyodwa kule nzululwazi (sayensi) ineendidi ezininzi zamacandelo ezifundo. Ngoko ke, kuyimfuneko ukuqala uqonde ukuba ingaba umntu angavumeleka na abengusosayensi kwelinye lamacandelo okusebenza aludidi oluphangaleleyo. Oku kuthetha ukuba kuyakufuneka ukuba umntu aqeqeshelwe ukuba ngusomachiza (ngusokhemesti), abengusosayensi wezobume nokwakhiwa komhlaba (i-geologist), abengusosayensi wezityalo okanye naliphina kumanye amacandelo ezendalo kwaye afezekise zonke iimfuneko zeekhwalifikheyshini phambi kokuba afaneleke abhaliswe kwicandelo leNzululwazi yezokuSingqongileyo (Environmental Science). Oku akuthethi ukubhalisa kabini.
Okungenani i 50 % yezi zifundo kule nkqubo kufuneka ihlelwe njengezifundo zenzululwazi yendalo.
Ukwengeza kwezi mfuneko zingentla, umntu onqwenela ukubhaliswa kwicandelo leNzululwazi yezokuSingqongileyo kufanele abenako ukunika ubungqina boqeqesho kuLawulo lwezokuSingqongileyo (umzekelo, uvavanyo lochaphazeleko kwezokusingqongileyo, umthetho wezokusingqongileyo). Ezi zifundo zingabayinxenye yenkqubo yesidanga seminyaka emine okanye zingenziwa ngokweekhosi ezimfutshane ezinikwe uqinisekiso lokuvunywa. Kufanele ubenengxelo ecacileyo nesulungekileyo yomsebenzi nophando olwayamene nenzululwazi yezokusingqongileyo. Kwakhona, usengenza imiba ebanzi echatshazelwa zizinto ezenziwa ziingcali zezokusingqongileyo.
IBhunga lingala ukubhalisa isicelo phantsi kwezi meko zilandelayo:
Ukubangaba, emva kokuqalisa koMgaqo-siseko weRiphabhlikhi yaseMzantsi Afrika, 1996 (Act 108 of 1996), umenzi-sicelo ufunyaniswe enetyala lokwaphula umthetho, ngaphakathi kwiRiphabhlikhi okanye kwenye indawo, waze wagwetyelwa ukuvalelwa entolongweni isithuba esidlula iinyanga ezintathu, okanye ifayini endaweni yokuvalelwa entolongweni.
Ukubangaba umenzi-sicelo ususwe esikhundleni sokuthembeka, ngenxa yokuziphatha okungafanelekanga.
Ukubangaba umenzi-sicelo ungumntu ongakwaziyo ukuhlawula amatyala nongabuyiselwanga kwimeko yesiqhelo, kwaye oko kungakwazi ukuhlawula amatyala kwabangelwa kukungakhathali kwakhe okanye ukungabinalwazi nezakhono zokwenza umsebenzi owela kwimiba echatshazelwa licandelo enzela lona isicelo sobhaliso.
IBhunga liyakukwazisa ngencwadi ebhaliweyo ukubangaba isicelo sakho sobhaliso saliwe.
Ungafaka isibheno esiphikisa isigqibo seBhunga, kwisithuba seentsuku ezingama 30.
Kufuneka wenze isicelo sokuvuselela ubhaliso lwakho kwiBhunga, okungenani kwiinyanga ezintathu phambi kokuphelelwa kobhaliso lwakho.

Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Xa idilesi yomntu itshintshile emva kokubhaliswa kwi-SARS njengomrhafi, makanike i-SARS iinkcukacha zedilesi entsha kwisithuba seentsuku ezingama- 60 ukusukela kumhla wokutshintsha.
Nayo iNcwadi yokuBuyisa yeRhafu yeNgeniso (Income Tax Return) esiwa kwi-SARS qho ngonyaka iya kulungiselela ukuxelwa koguquko lwedilesi, iinkcukacha zebhanki kunye nezinye iinkcukacha zobuqu. Isininzi sezaziso neencwadi zokubuyisa ze-SARS ziyawenza amalungiselelo okuxelwa kotshintsho lweenkcukacha zedilesi. Ezo nguqu ziya kulungiswa kwinkqubo ebandakanyekayo ye-SARS xa isaziso okanye incwadi yokubuyisa zizokufakwa.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Qinisekisa ukuba inkcazelo ngobuqu bakho njengoko ibonisiwe kwizaziso okanye kwiincwadi zokubuyisa ezamkelwa yi-SARS, ichanekile. Ukubangaba inkcazelo iboniswe ngokungachanekanga, phawula inkcazelo echanekileyo kwisaziso okanye kwincwadi yokubuyisa ebandakanyekayo phambi kokuba uyithumele kwi-SARS.
Faka iinguqu kwiinkcukacha zobuqu okanye kwiidilesi ngezi ndlela zilandelayo:
o thumela isicelo sokwenza iinguqu kwi-ofisi yesebe le-SARS ekufuphi kuwe o yenza izicelo ngokutsalela umnxeba kwiZiko lokuTsalela uMnxeba le-SARS ebandakanyekayo o thumela ifeksi kumaZiko okuTsalela uMnxeba eSARS ebandakanyekayo okanye kwi-ofisi yesebe le-SARS ekufuphi kuwe.

Ukurhafisa
Isicelo sokubhalisela ukubangumrhafi okanye ukuguqula iinkcukacha ezibhaliselwe irhafu yengeniso-mali

Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Xa idilesi yomntu itshintshile emva kokubhaliswa kwi-SARS njengomrhafi, makanike i-SARS iinkcukacha zedilesi entsha kwisithuba seentsuku ezingama- 60 ukusukela kumhla wokutshintsha.
Nayo iNcwadi yokuBuyisa yeRhafu yeNgeniso (Income Tax Return) esiwa kwi-SARS qho ngonyaka iya kulungiselela ukuxelwa koguquko lwedilesi, iinkcukacha zebhanki kunye nezinye iinkcukacha zobuqu. Isininzi sezaziso neencwadi zokubuyisa ze-SARS ziyawenza amalungiselelo okuxelwa kotshintsho lweenkcukacha zedilesi. Ezo nguqu ziya kulungiswa kwinkqubo ebandakanyekayo ye-SARS xa isaziso okanye incwadi yokubuyisa zizokufakwa.

Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Inkampani ya phesheya ayifanelanga ukwenza isicelo sokungenisa elizweni apha eMzantsi Afrika. Isicelo sokubhalisa amayeza ezolimo singenziwa kuphela yinkampani yasekhaya ebhalisiweyo, ummi waseMzantsi Afrika okanye umbutho osemthethweni obhalisiweyo apha eMzantsi Afrika.
Umbhalisi: Act 36 of 1947 (UmThetho 36 wowe- 1947) kufuneka aziswe ngokubhaliweyo malunga neenjongo zokuqhuba iimvavanyo ezifunwayo malunga nobhaliso lwamayeza ezolimo ukwenzela akwazi ukuhlola ukusebenza kwawo ngempumelelo.
Umbhalisi angafuna ulwazi olongezelelweyo ukuze amisele ukuba ingaba iyeza liyamkeleka malunga nokuba luncedo eluntwini, ukufaneleka nokusebenza ngempumelelo ngokwebhayoloji.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Khupha ifomu yesicelo kwi-inthanethi uze uyizalise ngokupheleleyo. Apho kukho imfuneko, ulwazi olufunwayo lungathunyelwa njengeziqhoboshelo ezahlukeneyo ezinikwe iinombolo.
Thumela kumbhalisi:
Iinkqubo I ne-II zisetyenziswa njengeenkqubo zokuhlola nesalathiso sokuqinisekisa ukuba umenzi wesicelo unikele ngedata yonke efanelekileyo.
Xa iyeza kufuneka lamkelwe njengelingeniswa elizweni, thumela ezilandelayo:
o izibuko lokungena o umlinganiso weyeza o iprothokholi yovavanyo o iziko lovavanyo o imixube esebenzayo o naluphi na olunye ulwazi olunokufunwa nguMbhalisi o ubungakanani obuya kuba kokungeniswa elizweni.
Izicelo ezingazaliswanga ngokupheleleyo ziya kuphindiswa kumenzi wesicelo yaye akukho xanduva luya kwamkelwa malunga nakuphi na ukuphazamiseka okunokwenzeka.
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Uphengululo lomxube omtsha osebenzayo lungathatha ukuya kutsho kunyaka omnye. Izicelo zeentsebenziso ezintsha okanye ukwakheka zikholisa ukuhlelwa kwithuba leenyanga ezintandathu.
Entla
Iindleko
Entla
Minyaka le iofisi yoMbhalisi ithumela iileta malunga nohlaziyo neefomu zesicelo kubo bonke abanobhaliso.

Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Ilungelo lokuvelisa nokuqamba ekuthiwa yi-patent lilungelo elikhethekileyo elinikwayo ngenxa yokuvelisa nokuqamba into ethile. Olo veliso noqambo kufuneka lubeyimveliso okanye inkqubo ezisa indlela entsha yokwenza izinto, okanye enika isisombululo esitsha sobuchule kwingxaki ethile.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Nxulumana noMphathi woBhaliso lwaMalungelo okuVelisa nokuQamba (Patents Registrar) kwiSebe lezoRhwebo naMashishini kwaye ukhangele ukuba akukho lungelo lokuvelisa nokuqamba esele likhona na.
Fumana iifom eziyimfuneko zesicelo (ngaphandle kwentlawulo) kwi-ofisi yoMphathi woBhaliso lwaMalungelo okuVelisa nokuQamba.
Hambisa ikopi eqinisekisiweyo yencwadi yakho yesazisi.
Faka isicelo sokubambisa kwifom efanelekileyo- oku kungenziwa ngumenzi-sicelo encediswa ligqwetha okanye engancediswa ligqwetha.
Faka isicelo esipheleleyo - oku kufuneka kwenziwe ngokuncediswa ligqwetha lamalungelo okuvelisa nokuqamba.
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Ilungelo lokubambisa lokuvelisa nokuqamba lithabatha iinyanga ezimbini ukuze libhaliswe.
Isicelo esipheleleyo sithabatha malunga neenyanga ezintandathu ukuze sigqitywe .

Inkcazelo
Unoxanduva nemfaneleko yokuba ubhalisele iRhafu yokuThengisa nokunika iiNkonzo, ebizwa ngokuba yi-VAT, ukubangaba imali ekungenelayo ngenxa yentengiso yezinto okanye iintlawulo ozifumene kwiinkonzo ozinikileyo, ingaphezulu kwe R300 000 ngonyaka, okanye ngokwengqiqo, ilindeleke ukuba ibengaphezulu kule mali.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Imiqulu neencwadi ekufuneka zikhaphe isicelo zezi zilandelayo:
Imiqulu engqina ngolwaziso lobuqu bakho:
Kwimeko yeshishini lelizwe langaphandle, iinkcukacha zommeli otyunjiweyo eMzantsi Afrika.
Eminye imiqulu ngokubanzi (zonke izicelo):
Isicwangciso seshishini, uphando lokukhangela ukuba ishishini linganako na ukuqhubeka, izivumelwano ezisayiniweyo zeekhontrakthi, isivumelwano sokugunyazisa ishishini okanye uthelekelelo lwendlela eliyakuqhuba ngayo ishishini, okanye obunye ubungqina obubonisa ukuba ixabiso lezinto ezirhafelwayo lingahle lidlule iR300 000. Oku akuyomfuneko ukubangaba sowuyidlulile iR300 000. Kwimeko yobhaliso lokuzithandela kufuneka kukhutshwe ubungqina bokuba iintengiso ezenziweyo nqo ziyidlulile iR20 000.
Ilayisensi yokuRhweba, ukubangaba iyabandakanyeka kwelo shishini, umzekelo, ilayisensi yokushishina ngotywala okanye ilayisensi yokuloba.
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Linda nje okungenani iintsuku zokusebenza ezili 10 ukuze i-ofisi yebhrentshi ekwindawo ohlala kuyo iqhubekise iincwadi zakho. Isatifiketi siyakuposelwa kwi-adresi yokuposa enikwe kwisicelo sakho sokubhalisa kwaye kufanele sifunyanwe kwisithuba seeveki ezi 2 emva kokuba siqhubekisiwe isicelo sakho.

Inkcazelo
Izilwanyana okanye iimveliso zezilwanyana zingathunyelwa kumazwe angaphandle kuphela xa ziphuma kwiindawo ezihambisana nemigangatho yehlabathi okanye nemithetho yelizwe eziyakungena kulo. Ezi ndawo ingaba ziindawo ezivunyiweyo zokuxhelela, iziko lokumithisa izilwanyana ngomatshini, iziko lokuqokelela, ifektri yokwenza iimveliso zokutya, iindawo zokugcina ukutya, njalo-njalo.

Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Nxulumana noGqirha weZilwanyana woMbuso kwiPhondo ukuze wenze isicelo sokuhlolelwa ubhaliso lokuthumela kumazwe angaphandle.
UGqirha weZilwanyana woMbuso kwiphondo uyalihlola iziko.
Ingxelo yokuhlolwa kweziko ithunyelwa kwiSebe leZolimo ukuze ivunywe ngemiba yophakamiso lwe-PSV kunye neziphakamiso zokugqibela.
Ukubangaba iziko livunyiwe, liyabhaliswa kuze ke kukhutshwe isatifiketi sokubhalisa ukuthumela kumazwe angaphandle.

Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Ipemethe yesizalwane ikhutshelwa umntu welizwe langaphandle oyifemeli esondele nqo yommi okanye yomhlali waseMzantsi Afrika. Loo mmi okanye loo mhlali kufuneka anike uqinisekiso lwemali ebekiweyo. Ipemethe yesizalwane isebenziseka ixesha elingagqithiyo kwiminyaka emibini.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Veza ubungqina bokuba yifemeli esondele nqo yalo mmi okanye lo mhlali uza kuye.
Veza isiqinisekiso esiphuma kumgcini nomhloli wee-akhawunti zemali olilungu lequmrhu labagcini nabahloli bee-akhawunti zemali, okanye ubungqina bemiqulu ehambelanayo engqina iindlela zenkxaso yalo mntu kuyiwa kuye okanye iindlela zokubanako zalo mntu kuyiwa kuye zidibene nezakho. Le nkxaso akufanelanga ibengaphantsi kwe R5 000 ngenyanga kumntu ngamnye ngalo lonke eli xesha lotyelelo (oku akubandakanyeki kwimeko yomlingane okanye kubantwana abaxhomekekileyo abangekakwazi ukuzithabathela izigqibo ngokwasemthethweni).
Ungacelwa ukuba uveze omnye umqulu okanye eminye yale miqulu ilandelayo:
o isatifiketi sokuzalwa esingafinyezwanga sokungqina ubuzali, apho kubandakanyeka khona o isatifiketi somtshato o ubungqina bobudlelwane bobulingane ukubangaba utshatile, nahlukene, niqhawule umtshato okanye ubhujelwe.
Isatifiketi esiphuma emapoliseni esiqinisekisa ubume obumsulwa, ukubangaba uneminyaka yobudala engama 21 okanye nangaphezulu, ngokuphathelelene nawo onke amazwe oke wahlala kuwo unyaka omnye okanye nangaphezulu, ekufuneka sikhutshwe kwisithuba seenyanga ezili 12 ukubangaba asifumaneki kwangoko.
Iingxelo zonyango neze-eksreyi ngokuphathelelene nomenzi-sicelo ngamnye. Yona ingxelo ye-eksreyi ayiyikufunwa kubantwana abangaphantsi kweminyaka eli 12 ubudala, nakwabasetyhini abakhulelweyo.

Entla

Le nkonzo ithabatha ixesha elingagqithiyo kwiintsuku ezingama 30.
