Ukuvuselela ilayisensi yomqhubi
Uhlaziyo lwephepha-mvume lokuqhuba
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Ikhadi lakho lephepha-mvume lokuqhuba lisemthethweni kanga ngeminyaka emihlanu ukusesela ngosuku eyakhutshwa ngalo, kufuneka ihlaziywe emva kweli xesha. Nangona usuku lokuphelelwa lephepha-mvume libhaliwe kwalapha kulo iasziso sokuphelelwa kwalo siza kuthunyelwa ngeposi.
Ungalihlaziya iphepha-mvume lakho nokuba kunini ngaphambi kokuba liphelelwe lixesha. Iphepha-mvume elitsha lizakuba semthethweni iminyaka emihlanu ukususela ngosuku lohlaziyo.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ungahlaziya iphepha-mvume lokuqhuba nakuyiphi na indawo yovavanyo apha eMzantsi Afrika, kodwa kuyakufuneka ulilande ikhadi kwakulondawo yovavanyo olihlaziye kuyo.
o incwadi yesazisi (ID), Incwadi yethutyana yesazisi, ikhadi elidala lephepha-mvume lokuqhuba okanye incwadi yoku ndwendwela esemthethweni yase Mzantsi Afrika o ifoto zesazisi ezimbini ezimnyama namhlophe o indleko zesicelo.
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iphepha-mvume elitsha lizakuba selilungile emva kweveki ezine ukuya kwezintandathu.
Entla
Iindleko iPhondo
Mpumalanga
Entla
Ifomu lesicelo sohlaziyo lephepha-mvume lokuqhuba, DL1
Ifomu liyafumaneka endaweni yokuvavanyelwa ukuqhuba.

Inkcazelo
Zonke izityalo ezibulala iintsholongwane ezisebenzayo apha eMzantsi Afrika kufuneka zibhaliswe kuMbhalisi: Act 36 of 1947 (UmThetho 36 wowe- 1947). Isityalo esibulala iintsholongwane sisetyenziswa ukubulala iintsholongwane kumathambo okanye ezinye izinto ezivela kwizilwanyana.
Minyaka le iofisi yoMbhalisi ithumela iileta malunga nohlaziyo neefomu zesicelo kubo bonke abanobhaliso.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Zalisa ifomu yesicelo ngeekopi ezintathu. Intsayino yokwenene iyafuneka kwifomu nganye ehlukileyo.

Entla

Ubhaliso lungathatha iinyanga ezi-3.

Ukuvuselelwa kwamaphepha-mvume emoto
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Zonke iimoto ezihamba indleleni kawonke-wonke kufuneka amaphepha-mvume azo rhoqo xa kuphela unyaka. Luxanduva lomnini moto ukuqinisekisa ukuba amaphepha-mvume emoto ayavuselelwa.Ukungaphumeleli ukuvuselela amaphepha-mvume emoto kungakhokhelela kwisohlwayo.
Kukhona ixesha lofefe elinga ngentsuku ezingamashumi ambini ananye elinikwa baninimoto ababngekawavuseleli amaphepha-mvume  aphelelwe lixesha emoto zabo.Ixesha lofefe libalwa ukusukela ngosuku lokuphelelwa kwamaphepha-mvume.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Yiza nencwadi yesazisi kunye nesaziso eso.
Bhatala imali ebekiweyo kwisaziso yokuqulunqwa kwesicelo.

Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Kufuneka ugqirha wezilwanyana angqine ukuba isilwanyana samkelekile malunga:
o nemo yempilo ngokubanzi o nokungabinazo izifo o nodidi lwencindi yobudoda.
Kufuneka izicelo zifike kuMbhalisi kungagqithanga iintsuku ezingama-30 phambi kokuba imvume iphelelwe. Xa isicelo sifika kwiintsuku ezingama-90 emva kokuphelelwa kwemvume, kufuneka kuhlawulwe intlawuliso eyongezelelweyo emiselweyo.
Iinkcukacha zebhanki zezi:
Inombolo yeAkhawunti: 011219556
Ikhowudi yesebe: 000845/010845

Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Ukuvuselelwa kobhaliso kuyakwenziwa xa ngaba ngexesha lokubhaliswa kwenzeka ezi zinto zilandelayo:
izinto eziqulathwe sisichumisi esibandakanyekayo azohlukanga kweziya sele zibhalisiwe iinkcukacha kunye namagama asetyenzisiweyo avunyiweyo wemibhalo yokuphawula okuqulathiweyo okanye inkonkxa akayi kutshintshwa ngaphandle kokuba kuqale kufunyanwe imvume ebhaliweyo esuka kuMphathi woBhaliso (Registrar)
imiqathango ebekwe ngexesha lobhaliso iyalandelwa ubhaliso aluyi kugqithiselwa ubungakanani beebhegi neenkonkxa abunakuguqulwa ngaphandle kokuba kuqale kufunyanwe imvume ebhaliweyo esuka kuMphathi woBhaliso.
Qho ngonyaka, i-ofisi yoMphathi woBhaliso ikhupha iincwadi zokuvuselela ezihamba neefom ezibandakanyekayo eziya kubantu ababhalisiweyo.

Minyaka le iofisi yoMbhalisi ithumela iileta malunga nohlaziyo neefomu zesicelo kubo bonke abanobhaliso.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Uhlaziyo:
o zalisa ifomu yesicelo (form A) ngeekopi ezintathu uze ubhale ngokwahlukanisa oonobumba ubhale ngoonobumba abakhulu kuphela o thumela kuMbhalisi: Act 36 of 1947 (UmThetho 36 wowe- 1947)
Ukucima:
o zalisa iFomu B ngeekopi ezintathu uze ubhale ngokwahlukanisa oonobumba usebenzisa oonobumba abakhulu o thumela isiqinisekiso setsusa sokubhalisa
Iinkcukacha zomenzi wesicelo:
o zalisa iFomu C ukuhlaziya irekhodi yombhalisi yeenkcukacha zonxibelelwano, umzkl, idilesi, inombolo yefowuni, nomntu woqhagamshelwano.

Entla

Uhlaziyo lwenziwa xa kufunyenwe intlawulo.

Ukuvuselelwa kobhaliso kuyakwenziwa xa ngaba ngexesha lokubhaliswa okanye lokuvuselelwa kobhaliso kwenzeka ezi zinto zilandelayo:
izinto eziqulathwe koku kutya kwemfuyo yasefama kubandakanyekayo azohlukanga kweziya sele zibhalisiwe iinkcukacha kunye namagama asetyenzisiweyo avunyiweyo wemibhalo yokuphawula okuqulathiweyo okanye inkonkxa akayi kutshintshwa ngaphandle kokuba kuqale kufunyanwe imvume ebhaliweyo esuka kuMphathi woBhaliso (Registrar)
imiqathango ebekwe ngexesha lobhaliso iyalandelwa ubhaliso olubandakanyekayo aluyi kugqithiselwa ubungakanani beebhegi neenkonkxa abunakuguqulwa ngaphandle kokuba kuqale kufunyanwe imvume ebhaliweyo esuka kuMphathi woBhaliso.

Abantu abafumana iigranti abangafanelekanga bazifumane
Ukwamkelwa kwiziko lombuso
Ukubangaba umntu akekho eMzantsi Afrika ixesha elingophukanga elidlula iinyanga ezintandathu.

Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
UMqondisi-Jikelele (Director-General) weSebe, ngokubona kwakhe, angayitsala le mali ngokufaka loo mntu emthethweni.
UMqondisi-Jikelele weSebe anganika imvume yokuba intlawulo iqhubeke ixesha elithile phantsi kwemiqathango ngokubonisa kwalo mntu malunga nokufuna ukubuyisela igranti. Isicelo kufuneka senziwe kwisithuba seentsuku ezingama 90 emva kokunqunyanyiswa kwegranti yentlalo.
Ukubangaba umntu ufuna ukuqwalasela ngokutsha igranti ephelelweyo, kufuneka ayichaze nayiphina ingeniso-mali ayifumanayo ngexesha lokwenza isicelo ngokutsha. Isebe liyakwenza isigqibo ngokusekelwe kule nkcazelo malunga nokuba liyiqwalasele ngokutsha na igranti okanye hayi. Umenzi-sicelo uyakwaziswa ngesiphumo sesicelo kwiinyanga ezi 3 ezingaphambili kumhla wokuqwalaselwa ngokutsha okanye kumhla wokwenziwa kwesatifiketi.

Inkcazelo
Olu ncedo lolwabaqhubi abanelungelo lokuqhuba, abalahlekelwe ngamaphepha-mvume abo okuqhuba. Ukubuyisela iphepha-mvume elilahlekileyo okanye elonakeleyo yiya kwi ofisi yamagosa endlela ekufuphi nawe.

Bhatala imali ebekiweyo

Ungasenza nesicelo sephepha-mvume lethutyana.ezelelweyo uzise nenye ifoto emnyama namhlophe.

Xela impatho-mbi yabantu abadala
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Le nkozo ichaza ngenyathelo ongalithabatha ukuthontela okanye ukuphelisa impatho-mbi kubantu abadala.Kunendlela ezininzi abantu abadala abaphathwa kakubi ngazo. Nazi ezinye zazo:
Impatho-mbi emzimbeni:Sonke isenzo esilimazayo emzimbeni okanye sibulale umntu omdala, umzekelo, ukubetha ngempama, ukutshova, ukuphatha ngqwabalala, ukusika, ukusetyenziswa ngokungemthetho kwamachiza okanye ukuthintela ukuhamba ngokukhululekile,ukunika amayeza ngokungafanelekanga naso nasiphi na isenzo esingonwabisiyo nesidala ukuphatheka kakubi noba esoyikisayo okanye ukufa.
Impatho-mbi ngesondo:Isenzo esibangela impatho-mbi kumntu omdala esenzelwa ukuzanelisa ngesondo, bengenalwazi okanye bengaqondi noba bengavumelananga nesenzo eso.
Impatho-mbi ngokwase ngqondweni,ngokwasemphefumlweni nangamazwi:Uhlobo lwesenzo esithula isidima okanye esingonwabisiyo kubantu abadala, esiphazamisayo ngokwasengqondweni noba emoyeni. Imizekelo:ukunganakwa, ukhlaliswa wedwa okanye ingcinezelo. Ukunganikwa thuba lokuthanda noba ukuthandwa, ukuthukwa nokutyholwa.
Ukunganakwa: Ukuvinjwa okanye ukungafumani inkathalo eyimfuneko ekuncedeni ukusebenza kakuhle komzimba nengqondo.Izinto ezifana nokutya, ulwamkeleko, indawo yokuhlala impahla, amayeza inkuthazo emoyeni, ukungazihoyi, nokuzidelela.
Ukophulwa kwamalungelo oluntu:ukunganikwa amalungelo angundoqo afana nentlonipho, isidima, imfihlo yomntu, inkululeko yokucinga, inkolo, uluvo, intetho, ukuzityandigilanokuhambangokukhululekileyo kwabantu abadala. Umzekelo izinto abazenzayo ngenxa yobudala zenza kuthiwe bayathakatha. Ezizinto zenza ukuba bazondwe bahlutshwe okanye babulawe.
Ngubani onga xela impatho-mbi?
Noba ngubani obone ukunganakekelwa kwabantu abadala, ukusetyenziswa nokungemthetho, ukuphathwa kabuhlungu. Okanye unezizathu zokusola impatho mbi iyenzeka okanye yakha yenzeka.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Zingekapheli iiyure ezingamashumi amane anesibhozo ixeliwe impatho-mbi, unontlalontle uzakwenza uphando abhale ingxelo.
Ukuba impatho-mbi ibandakanya ikhaya labadala, imibutho engekho phantsi korhulumente okanye umbutho osekwe ekuhlaleni, unontlalontle kumele abhekane nale meko.

Inkcazelo
Qho ngenyanga, oogqirha bombuso kulo lonke eli laseMzantsi Afrika bathumela iingxelo zezifo zezilwanyana kuBaqondisi babo baMaphondo beeNkonzo zeZilwanyana. Ezi ngxelo ziyaphononongwa, zize ke zithunyelwe kwiCandelo lelizwe loBuqondisi beMpilo yeZilwanyana (Directorate Animal Health) e-Pretoria, zithi ke apho zifakwe kuvimba ogcina inkcazelo. Iingxelo zenyanga zezifo zezilwanyana ziqulungqwa ngokusebenzisa le nkcazelo. Ezi ngxelo zithunyelwa elizweni nakumazwe ehlabathi kubabandakanyeki nemibutho enomnqweno.

Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Le nkonzo inikwa nabanina olixhoba lobugebenga.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Xa umntu ethe walixhoba lobugebenga, anganxulumana namapolisa ngokutsalela umnxeba kwinombolo ethi 10111 okanye angaya kwisikhululo samapolisa esikufuphi kuye (jonga icandelo elithi: iinkcukacha zonxulumano) ukuze axele ngobu bugebenga.
Ummangali kufuneka aqinisekise ukuba uyayigcina le nombolo ye-CAS ukuze abhekise kuyo xa kwixesha elizayo ebuzisa malunga neli tyala lobugebenga.
Idokethi eligqityiweyo linikwa umcuphi wamapolisa oyakuqhuba uphando.Yonke imibuzo ingabhekiswa kulo mcuphi.
Umcuphi uyakwazisa ummangali ukuba aye ninina enkundleni.

Ukujongana nomthetho
Ilifa lomntu obhubhileyo
Ukunika ingxelo ngempahla izinto kunye neemali zom
Ukunika ingxelo ngempahla izinto kunye neemali zomntu ongasekhoyo
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Impahla, izinto kunye neemali (ilifa) zomntu ongasekhoyo zivela ekubhubheni komntu kwaye eshiya impahla, izinto kunye neemali (ipropati) kunye nomqulu okanye umqulu wasemthethweni ongumyolelo oyalela indlela emakwabiwe ngayo eli lifa (i-will) okanye oneenjongo zokuba ngumqulu wasemthethweni ongumyolelo oyalela indlela emakwabiwe ngayo ilifa. Eli lifa ke kufuneka lilawulwe kwaye labiwe ngokuhambisana nomqulu wasemthethweni ongumyolelo oyalelayo womfi, okanye, ukubangaba umfi akashiyanga myolelo oyalelayo, kufuneka labiwe kwaye lilawulwe ngokuhambisana nemimiselo yomthetho. Umthetho wokuLawulwa kwaMafa, ekuthiwa yi-Administration of Estates Act, 1965, uqingqa umgaqo omawulandelwe xa kulawulwa ilifa longasekhoyo.
Ilifa lomntu ongasekhoyo kufuneka lixelwe kwi-ofisi yoMphathi oyiNqununu (Master) kwisithuba seentsuku ezili 14 zomhla wokubhubha. Ukubhubha kungaxelwa nguye nawuphina umntu onolawulo okanye ophethe nayiphina impahla eyinxenye yelifa longasekhoyo, okanye onolawulo okanye ophethe umqulu obhalwe ngumfi, ongumqulu wasemthethweni ongumyolelo oyalela indlela emakwabiwe ngayo ilifa (i-will) okanye obonakala ngathi ungumqulu wasemthethweni ongumyolelo oyalela indlela emakwabiwe ngayo ilifa.
Kufuneka kuxelwe nini ukubhubha, kuMphathi oyiNqununu (Master)?
Ukubangaba umfi ubhubhele eMzantsi Afrika, kwaye ushiye impahla, izinto kunye neemali (ipropati) kunye nawuphina umqulu okanye nawuphina umqulu wasemthethweni ongumyolelo oyalela indlela emakwabiwe ngayo ilifa okanye oneenjongo zokuba ngumqulu wasemthethweni ongumyolelo oyalela indlela emakwabiwe ngayo ilifa.
Ukubangaba umfi ubhubhele ngaphandle koMzantsi Afrika, kodwa abe ushiye ipropati apha eMzantsi Afrika kunye nawuphina umqulu okanye nawuphina umqulu wasemthethweni ongumyolelo oyalela indlela emakwabiwe ngayo ilifa okanye oneenjongo zokuba ngumqulu wasemthethweni ongumyolelo oyalela indlela emakwabiwe ngayo ilifa.
Kufuneka lixelwe phi ilifa lomntu ongasekhoyo?
Nangona nje zonke ii-ofisi zoomantyi zingamaziko eenkonzo zoMphathi oyiNqununu kwaye amafa wabangasekhoyo engaxelwa apho, zona zinegunya namandla aqingqiweyo, kwaye ziyakutshintshela kwi-ofisi yephondo yoMphathi oyiNqununu (Master), wonke amafa kunye nemiqulu yasemthethweni eyimiyolelo eyalela.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
o ukubangaba umfi ubehlala eMzantsi Afrika ngexesha lokubhubha kwakhe, xela ilifa kuMphathi oyiNqununu onegunya namandla kummandla apho bekuhlala khona umfi ngexesha lokubhubha kwakhe o ukubangaba umfi wayengahlali eMzantsi Afrika ngexesha lokubhubha kwakhe, ungalixela ilifa lakhe kuye nawuphina uMphathi oyiNqununu (kodwa uxelele abemnye kuphela)
o xela ilifa ngokugcwalisa iFom J294, ethi: Isaziso sokubhubha (Form J294: Death notice) kunye neminye imiqulu ebandakanyekayo yokunika ingxelo, edweliswe apha ngezantsi o ungasifumana isaziso sokubhubha (Death notice) kunye neminye imiqulu yokunika ingxelo kuyo nayiphina i-ofisi yoMphathi oyiNqununu wenkundla ephakamileyo okanye kuyo nayiphina i-ofisi kamantyi.
o isatifiketi sokubhubha esiluqobo lwaso okanye ikopi yaso eqinisekisiweyo o isatifiketi somtshato esiluqobo lwaso okanye ikopi yaso eqinisekisiweyo - ukubangaba oku kuyabandakanyeka o uqobo lwazo zonke ii-will kunye nemifakelo eyongezelelayo (oko kukuthi, inxenye eyongezayo ye-will elungisa uqobo lwe-will okanye esusa inxenye yayo) okanye imiqulu eneenjongo ezinjalo - ukuba ikhona o uluhlu lwababolekisi kumfi - ukuba bakhona o isibhengezo sokuba eli lifa alixelwanga kwenye i-ofisi yoMphathi oyiNqununu okanye kwelinye iziko leenkonzo zoMphathi oyiNqununu.
Hambisa iifom ezigcwalisiweyo ezidweliswe apha ngasentla zikunye nale miqulu ilandelayo:
o isatifiketi sokubhubha esiluqobo lwaso okanye ikopi yaso eqinisekisiweyo o isatifiketi somtshato esiluqobo lwaso okanye ikopi yaso eqinisekisiweyo - ukubangaba oku kuyabandakanyeka.
Amaziko eenkonzo zoMphathi oyiNqununu (ii-ofisi zoomantyi) anegunya namandla kuphela xangaba umfi akashiyanga mqulu wasemthethweni osebenzisekayo ongumyolelo oyalela indlela emakwabiwe ngayo ilifa (i-will), kwaye ixabiso lilonke lelifa longasekhoyo lingaphantsi kwe R50 000. Iincwadi zegunya zivumela ummeli otyunjiweyo ukuba alawule ilifa ngaphandle kokulandela umgaqo opheleleyo oqingqwe kuMthetho wokuLawulwa kwaMafa (Administration of Estates Act, 1965).

Ixesha elithatyathwayo kule nkonzo lixhomekeka kubunzima benyewe.
Entla
Iindleko
Nxulumana ne-ofisi yoMphathi oyiNqununu ukuze ufumane iinkcukacha.

Iinkonzo zemibutho
Isicelo sokuseka i-learnership (inkqubo yokufundisa nokuqeqeshela umsebenzi), njengomniki-nkonzo zoqeqesho
Inkcazelo
Ukuze ufumaneinkcazelo ebanzi, yiya kwiSebe leZabasebenzi.
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Abaniki-nkonzo zoqeqesho mabenze isigqibo sokuba zeziphi ii-learnerships abanganika uqeqesho kuzo.
Ukuze anikwe uqinisekiso lokuvunywa nokwamkelwa, umniki-nkonzo zoqeqesho kufuneka:
Alandele iinkqubo ezifanelekileyo zemfundo, uqeqesho kunye nophuhliso; kwaye
Xa abaniki-nkonzo zoqeqesho sele beyikhethile i-learnership, kuyakufuneka bafune abaqashi ukuze banike abafundi amava omsebenzi.
Abaniki-nkonzo zoqeqesho kunye nabaqashi abayakunika amava omsebenzi kufuneka bavumelane malunga nezi zinto zilandelayo:
Indlela ekuyakukhethwa ngayo abafundi; kunye
Nendlela abaya kufumana ngayo abafundi.
Abafundi bangaba ngabasebenzi asele beqashiwe ngumqashi okanye ingaba ngabantu abangasebenziyo. Nxulumana neziko lezabasebenzi elikufuphi kuwe ukuze uqonde ukuba iSebe leZabasebenzi lingakunceda njani ukuze ufumane abafundi abangasebenziyo.
Abaqashi, abaniki-nkonzo zoqeqesho kunye nabafundi kufuneka batyikitye (basayine) isivumelwano se-learnership.
Abaniki-nkonzo zoqeqesho kufuneka baqalise uqeqesho ngomhla ekuvunyelwene ngawo kwisivumelwano se-learnership.
Ixesha elithatyyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo

Inkcazelo
Ukuhlelwa ngokukhethekileyo kwemoto kuvumeleka kuhlobo oluthile lwemoto elenzan umsebenzi othile elingavamisanga ukuhamba endleleni kawonke-wonke.
Inqwelo erhuqwayo okanye itrekta ikhululiwe ekubhataleni indleko zephepha-mvume ukuba umnini wazo ungumlimi ngokunyanisekileyouzisebenzisela ulimo kuphela.Kuyafana naxa imoto yakhiwe ngokutsha okanye itshintshiwe ukuze isetyenzselwe ukhuphiswano okanye imiboniso.

Inkqubo emayilandelwe
o incwadi yesazisi o isatifiketi sobhaliso lwemoto o incwadi yesigunyaziso ephuma kuLawulo Lomgangatho worhwebo eMzantsi Afrika o isatifiketi sokulungela ukuba sendleleni kwemoto.

Amaziko akwinqanaba lesithathu
Isicelo sobhaliso olunikwe umnyenyevu owodwa ukuze
Ubhaliso olulodwa njengenzululwazi eqeqeshiweyo - Ukwamkelwa kwemfundo namava angaphambili
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
IBhunga liye lagqiba ekubeni linike abantu abanjalo ithuba lokufaka izicelo zokubhalisela ukuba ziiNzululwazi eziQeqeshiweyo phantsi kwemiqathango ethile.
Nabanina ongenasiqinisekiso sivunyiweyo liBhunga angafaka isicelo.
Abafaka izicelo kufanele ukuba:
babe negalelo kuluntu lwezenzululwazi babe neminyaka eli-10 ubuncinane yamava angaqhawulwanga afanelekileyo oqeqesho kanye phambi kokufaka isicelo kwelo cadelo lomsebenzi abawunqwenelayo.
Qaphela: Ukuba ushiye umsebenzi wakho ngeli thuba leminyaka eli-10, awusayi kuvunyelwa ukuba ubhalise phantsi kolu lawulo lolwazelelelo.
Uvavanyo lwezicelo luya kwenziwa yiKomiti eCebisayo yemiSebenzi efanelekileyo, ukuvunywa kuya kwenziwa yiKomiti yoBhalis yeSACNASP ukuze ugunyaziso lwenziwe liBhunga liphelele.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Zalisa ifomu yesicelo eqingqiweyo ukuze ubhalise.
o ubungqina obufanelekileyo boqeqesho oluqingqiweyo nolungaqingqwanga - iikopi eziqinisekisiweyo zeziqinisekiso zezidanga okanye zeediploma, kuquka neengxelo zezifundo zala manqanaba o ingxelo ebanzi yamava omsebenzi oqeqehelwe wona kweli candelo lomsebenzi ofake isicelo kulo o uluhlu lwezinto ezipapashiweyo o ubungqina bobulungu kwimibutho yezifundiswa, umz. Umbutho waseMzantsi Afrika weNzululwazi nobuGcisa bezokuTya (SAAFoST); iQumrhu laseMzantsi Afrika leeKemikhali (SACI); Umbutho waseMzantsi Afrika wezoLwakhiwo lomhlaba (GSSA).
Ubuncinane, iingxelo ezipheleleyo ezintathu (ezibhalwe zagcinwa kubuchwepheshe bekhompyutha) othe waziqulunqa okanye obe negalelo elikhulu kuzo. Ukuba akukwazi ukuzingenisa ezo ngxelo ngenxa yemfihlelo ethile, elo galelo kufuneka libe nokuqinisekiswa.
Ubungqina obufungelweyo obucacisa ukuba lo ngumsebenzi wakho kwaye ucacise indima yakho oyidlalileyo kwezo ngxelo uzifakileyo.
Ubungqina obufungelweyo babantu ababini obakhethileyo abanokungqinisisa ngezakhono zakho kweli candelo lakho lomsebenzi.
Entla
Entla
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Ubhaliso lungathatha iiveki ezi-6 ukuya kwezi-8, kuxhomekeke ekungenisweni kwamaxwebhu afunwayo.
Iqela labantu ababini ubuncinane abonyulwe yiKomiti eCebisayo yezemiSebenzi (iPAC ngamafutshane) yeSACNASP liya kudlana indlebe nawe.
Isiphumo sovavanyo siya kwaziwa kuphela emva kwentlanganiso yeBhunga.

Ukuhlala eMzantsi Afrika
Imfundo
Isicelo sephepha lemvume (ipemethe) yokufunda
Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Iphepha lemvume (ipemethe) yokufunda yincwadi enika abantu abaphuma kumazwe angaphandle ilungelo lokufunda kulo naliphina iziko lemfundo ephakamileyo eMzantsi Afrika. Afake isicelo ngokwakhe kwiNdlu yoZakuzo yaseMzantsi Afrika okanye kwiZiko eliMele uMzantsi Afrika.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Aveze:
o incwadi egunyazisiweyo okanye ubungqina bokubhaliswa obusuka kwiziko lemfundo elibhalisiweyo laseMzantsi Afrika o iinkcukacha malunga nendawo yokuhlala elungisiweyo o ubungqina beemali ezaneleyo zokuhlawula iimali zokufunda, ukulungiswa kunye nezinye iindleko o isatifiketi sokubamsulwa esiphuma emapoliseni ngokuphathelelene namazwe abekade ehlala kuwo kumathuba angaphezulu konyaka. Esi satifiketi kufuneka sithiwe thaca kwisithuba seenyanga ezilishumi elinesibini kwenziwe isicelo ukubangaba asifumaneki kwamsinyane o ikopi yetikiti lomoya eliyiritheni okanye isiqinisekiso sokubuyiselwa ekhaya esiluhlobo lwedipozithi elingana nendleko yetikiti lomoya eliya kwilizwe avela kulo okanye ahlala kulo, ukuba kuyimfuneko o incwadi kagqirha engqina ukuba umenzi-sicelo usempilweni entle.
Abenzi-zicelo abanakungena eMzantsi Afrika phambi kokuba izicelo zabo zivunywe.
Abenzi-zicelo abanezicelo ezivunyiweyo banikwa i-visa evumela ukuba bangena-ngene kaninzi.
Abantu abasephantsi kwabazali mabathi thaca iinkcukacha zomntu waseMzantsi Afrika oyakubangumntu obamelayo. Ezi nkcukacha mazithiwe thaca nencwadi evumayo, ubungqina obuvela kubazali bobabini bemvume yeli xesha kujongwe ukuba lihlalwe, okanye obuvela kumzali onguye yedwa ogcina umntwana ndawonye nobungqina bokugcinwa ngumzali omnye.

Inkcazelo
Imali eyingeniso yeNgxowa-mali yeMbuyekezo iqulethe ubukhulu becala iimali ezihlawulwe ngabaqeshi ababhaliswe ngokusemthethweni ngokweqondo lepesentenji okanye eqingqiweyo kwiimali eziyingeniso zonyaka zabaqeshwa babo.
UMthetho ubonelela isixa esincinane semali ezihlawulwe ngabaqeshi ukuqinisekisa ukuba intlawulo ayikho ngaphantsi kweendleko zolawulo.

Inkcazelo
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Ukulobela ukuphila kunxulumene noluntu olusemanxwemeni olusebenzisa izinto eziphilayo zaselwandle njengento oluyityayo, nangona besenokuthi bazithengise okanye bananiselane ngazo apho kulo ngqingi bakuyo. Njengangoku, abalobi abalobela ukuphila balawulwa ngeminyinyiva yokuxolelwa de kube lelo thuba lokuba kumiselwe umgaqo-nkqubo onokusetyenziswa malunga noku. Ukuze umntu abenako ukufikelela kwizinto eziphilayo zaselwandle njengomlobi olobela ukuphila, makenze isicelo somnyinyiva wokuxolelwa kuqala ukuze avunyelwe ukuba enze umsebenzi wokuvuna iintlanzi okanye enze imisebenzi enxulumene nokuloba, elobela ukuphila nokwenzela iinjongo zokushishina ngokungephi.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Yenza isicelo somnyinyiva wokuxolelwa ngokusebenzisa iikomiti zolawulo ezisebenzisanayo zengingqi zakuba izicelo zomnyinyiva wokuxolelwa ziphelelwe ekupheleni konyaka ngamnye.
Abalobi abasanda kungena/kujoyina kufuneka bafaneleke kwiimfuneko zokulobela ukuphila nokulobela iinjongo zokushishina okungephi phambi kokuba kukhutshwe imvume yomnyinyiva wokuxolelwa.
Umenzi-sicelo makabonise ukuba leliphi na icandelo okanye icandelo lokuloba aza kusebenza kulo.
Amagosa esebe abiza intlanganiso yabahlali ukuze akhuphe iimvume zomnyinyiva wokuxolelwa kubo bonke abalobi ababhalisiweyo.
Phambi kokukhupha imvume zomnyinyiva wokuxolelwa abasebenzi besebe bacacisa imiqathango yemvume yomnyinyiva wokuxolelwa nomthamo oqingqiweyo womthwalo.
Bonke abanemvume zomnyinyiva wokuxolelwa balindeleke ukuba basayine kuluhlu lokuvuma ukuba bazifumene iimvume zabo zomnyinyiva wokuxolelwa.
Entla
Entla

Khupha iFom B kwi-website uyigcwalise ngokupheleleyo, uze ke uyihambise phambi kokuba uhlawule isixa sesambuku kwilungu lengxowa-mali.
Nika i-adresi yelungu yokuhlala neyokuposa.
Eyona ndlela ilula kakhulu yokwenza isicelo sesikhokelo serhafu kukusifaka nge- eFiling. Isicelo sakho sesikhokelo serhafu esenziwe ngale nkonzo sidla ngokuvunywa kwisithuba seeyure ezingama 48.

Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Iindleko
Inkcazelo
abalindele izigqebhezana zabo zamaphepha-mvume okuqhuba abenze isicelo sokuvuselela amaphepha-mvume abo okuqhuba abalahlekelwe ngamaphepha-mvume abo okuqhuba.
Eli phepha-mvume liphelelwa lixesha emva kwee nyanga ezintandathu futhi ikhutshwa yiyo nayiphi na indawo yokuvavanyelwa iphepha-mvume lokuqhuba.
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Uphathe ezi zinto zilandelayo:
o incwadi yesazisi okanye incwadi yokundwendwela o imifanekiso emibini elingana neyesazisi, ibe mhlophe namyama.
Uvavanyo lwamehlo luzokwenziwa ngaphambi kokuba likhutshwe iphepha-mvume lokuqhuba lethutyana.
Bhatala imali ebekiweyo.

Entla

Iphepha-mvume lokuqhuba lethutyana likhutshwa kwangolosuku lesicelo.

Iindleko
Inkcazelo
Inani lobhaliso endleleni likhutshelwa abemi bamazwe angaphandle abangenayo incwadi yesazisi yaseMzantsi Afrika, ithathwa njengendlela eyamkelekileyo yenani lokwazisa elisetyenziswa kulo naluphina urhwebo endleleni.Inani lobhaliso edleleni liyafuneka xa ummi welizwe langaphandle efuna ukubhalisa imoto eMzantsi Afrika. 
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Yiya kwi ofisi yamagosa endlela ekufutshane.
o ikopi yencwadi yokundwendwela eqinisekisiweyo okanye imvume yokuhlala yethutyana o incwadi yesazisi ekhutshwe ngokusemthethweni.

Yenza isicelo sepemethe okanye selayisensi

Inkcazelo
Ubhaliso lusebenziseka ithuba lonyaka omnye ukusukela kumhla wokukhutshwa kwesatifiketi sobhaliso.
Ukuhambisa impahla nezinto ezinobunzima obuyikhilogrem enye okanye nangaphantsi
Ukukhutshwa kwezitampu zokuposa
Ukunikwa kwenkonzo yokuqokelela ecaleni kwendlela kunye neebhokisi zee-adresi.
Ezi aziwabandakanyi amashishini anika iimveliso zawo, afana nommntu othengisa nocwangcisa iintyatyambo, usosilarha okanye ivenkile yegrosari.
Abantu abazimele bucala okanye amashishini azimele bucala, akhululekile enze isicelo selayisensi yokuqhuba inkonzo yeposi engabekelwanga iziko elithile (kuyo nayiphina inkonzo engabandakanywanga kolu luhlu lungentla).
Isicelo sokubhalisa kuMgqaliseli weeNkonzo zePosi ukuze uqhube inkonzo yeposi engabekelwanga iziko elithile, kufuneka siqingqwe ngendlela, kwaye sihambisane nomgaqo, ochazwe nguMphathiswa ngokweziphakamiso ezenziwe nguMgqaliseli (Regulator).
Ubhaliso lusebenziseka ithuba lonyaka omnye ukusukela kumhla wokukhutshwa kwesatifiketi sobhaliso.
Ukuze ufumane inkcazelo ebanzi, yiya kwiSebe lezoNxibelelwano
Entla
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Zalisa ifom yesicelo ngokuphindwe kathathu.
Hlawula imali efunekayo ngekhetshi okanye ngetshekhi eqinisekiswe yibhanki:
Hambisa ifom yesicelo kwiSebe lezoNxibelelwano, uyihambise nobungqina bentlawulo.
Thumela ubungqina bentlawulo ngefeksi kwinombolo ethi: 12 427 8536.
Faka ezi zinto zilandelayo:
Isatifiketi sobhaliso lweshishini
Iikopi eziqinisekisiweyo zayo yonke imiqulu ebandakanyekayo yokuseka ishishini
Iinkcukacha zabantu abanezabelo kunye nepesenti yesabelo somntu ngamnye onesabelo
Iinkcukacha zeziko eliphetheyo
Ukungaphumeleli ukuhambisana nayo nayiphi na kwezi mfuneko kungakhokelela ekubeni isicelo sakho singavumeleki ukuba siqwalaselwe.

Iinkonzo zemibutho
Iimanyano zabasebenzi kunye nemibutho yabaqashi
Isicelo sokuseka iqonga lasemsebenzini
Isicelo sokuseka iqonga lasemsebenzini
Inkcazelo
Amaqonga asemsebenzini asekelwa
Ukufezekisa iminqweno yabo bonke abaqeshwa emsebenzini, hayi nje kuphela eyamalungu ombutho wabasebenzi (eyuniyoni);
Ukuphakamisa iinkqubo zobunono emsebenzini;
Ukubonisana nabaqeshwa kwimibandela ethile; kunye
Nokubandakanya abaqeshwa ekuthabatheni izigqibo ngokuhlanganelweyo kweminye imibandela ethile.
Iqonga lasemsebenzini lingasekwa kuyo nayiphi na indawo yokusebenza enabaqeshwa abangaphezulu kwe- 100. Eli nani alibabandakanyi abaqeshwa abakwizikhundla eziphezulu zobuphathi. Isicelo singenziwa kuphela xangaba akukho qonga lasemsebenzini esele likhona ngokomThetho woBudlelwane beZabasebenzi, wowe- 1995 (Labour Relations Act, 1995).
Ukuze ufumane inkcazelo ebanzi, yiya kwiSebe leZabasebenzi.
Inkqubo emayilandelwe
Ikopi yesiliphu serejista esiphuma ePosini
Ingxelo esayiniweyo yalo mntu uhambise ikopi yefom, engqina ukusiwa kwefom
Ikopi yesiliphu esingqinayo sefeksi, okanye nabuphi na obunye ubungqina obanelisayo benkonzo
Ixesha elithatyathwayo kunye nomgangatho ofikelelwayo
Kungathabatha iintsuku ezingama 30 ukuze kusekwe eli qonga.
